# physics.atom-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Limit on the nuclear Schiff moment of europium-153](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12084)
*Bassam Nima,Mingyu Fan,Xubo Wang,Sen Wang,En Fu Zhou,Andrew M. Jayich,Jiang Ming Yao,Lan Cheng,Amar Vutha*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过测量Y₂SiO₅晶体中极化方向相反的¹⁵³Eu³⁺离子核自旋共振（nuclear spin resonance），将¹⁵³Eu原子核的Schiff矩（Schiff moment）限制在|𝒮(¹⁵³Eu)| < 1.7×10⁻⁸ e·fm³（95%置信度）。该测量利用处于毫米级晶体中的八极核（octupolar nuclei），将新物理约束在TeV能标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原子核的Schiff矩是一种破缺宇称（parity）和时间反演（time-reversal）对称性的核矩，其存在预示着超越标准模型（Standard Model）的新物理。通过对该矩的精确测量，可探索TeV能标下的新物理信号。

Method: 采用两套极化方向相反的¹⁵³Eu³⁺离子系综（ensembles），在Y₂SiO₅晶体中进行核自旋共振（nuclear spin resonance）实验，测量并约束¹⁵³Eu原子核的Schiff矩。

Result: 在95%置信度下，¹⁵³Eu原子核的Schiff矩上限为|𝒮(¹⁵³Eu)| < 1.7×10⁻⁸ e·fm³。

Conclusion: 该工作利用毫米级晶体中的八极核完成了对Schiff矩的测量，将新物理的约束提升至TeV能标，展示了固体体系在基础物理检验中的潜力。

Abstract: The Schiff moment of a nucleus is a symmetry-violating nuclear moment that indicates new physics beyond the Standard Model. We place the limit, $|\mathscr{S}({}^{153}$Eu)$| < 1.7 \times 10^{-8}$ $e\,$fm$^3$ (95\% confidence), on the Schiff moment of the $^{153}$Eu nucleus, using nuclear spin resonances in two ensembles of oppositely-polarized $^{153}$Eu$^{3+}$ ions in a Y${}_2$SiO${}_5$ crystal. This measurement using octupolar nuclei in a mm-scale crystal constrains new physics at the TeV energy-scale.

</details>

# cond-mat.quant-gas [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Universal critical behavior in ideal Bose-Einstein condensation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11338)
*Arturo Camacho-Guardian,Leon Kleebank,Frank Vewinger,Martin Weitz,Julian Schmitt,Rosario Paredes,Victor Romero-Rochín*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文证明理想玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（BEC）相变附近的临界行为完全由态密度（density of states）的低能标度律决定，可划分为三个不同的普适类，为无相互作用玻色系统的临界性提供了统一框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理想BEC是连续相变（continuous phase transition）的范式模型和理解量子简并玻色物质（quantum degenerate bosonic matter）的基石，但其临界行为在不同维度与约束条件下的完整分类尚需统一的理论框架。

Method: 通过分析态密度的低能标度指数（scaling exponent）——该指数由维度（dimensionality）和约束（confinement）控制——对理想玻色气体的临界行为进行分类。

Result: 发现三个截然不同的临界行为类别：通常的热力学磁化率代数发散（algebraic divergences）、带有边缘对数修正（marginal logarithmic corrections）的发散行为，以及更微妙的临界性形式——其中仅关联长度（correlation length）发散。

Conclusion: 该分类框架普遍适用于原子、光子（photonic）、极化激元（polaritonic）和磁振子（magnonic）凝聚体，其中维度、约束和谱工程（spectral engineering）可强烈重塑态密度。

Abstract: Ideal Bose-Einstein condensation (BEC) remains a paradigmatic example of a continuous phase transition and a cornerstone for understanding quantum degenerate bosonic matter. We demonstrate that critical behavior of the ideal Bose gas near the BEC phase transition falls into three distinct classes, determined exclusively by the low-energy scaling of the density of states. Depending on its scaling exponent, which is controlled by dimensionality and confinement, the transition displays either the usual algebraic divergences of thermodynamic susceptibilities, divergent behavior with marginal logarithmic corrections, or a more subtle form of criticality, where only the correlation length diverges. Our work provides a unified framework for criticality in noninteracting bosonic systems. This classification applies broadly to atomic, photonic, polaritonic, and magnonic condensates, where dimensionality, confinement, and spectral engineering can strongly reshape the density of states.

</details>


### [3] [Dynamics of repeated BEC formation and extraction in dimple traps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11428)
*Kyrylo Kovalchuk,Dominik Pfeiffer,Ludwig Lind,Mark Edwards,Alexander Yakimenko,Gerhard Birkl*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文基于动力学模型研究了在嵌入热原子库的“酒窝阱”（dimple trap）中反复形成和提取玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BEC）的过程，比较了三种提取协议，发现残余原子会加速后续BEC生长但也会增强损耗，部分BEC提取方案在短周期和高输入率下效率最高。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在酒窝阱中实现反复生成和提取BEC的可行性及优化条件，明确残余原子（seeding）对后续BEC生长与损耗平衡的动力学作用。

Method: 构建包含脉冲提取、蒸发、三体损失（three-body losses）及热原子补充过程的动力学模型（kinetic model），比较三种提取协议：全部原子提取、完整BEC提取（不含热原子）以及部分BEC提取。

Result: 残余原子会促进后续的玻色刺激生长（Bose-stimulated growth）并缩短恢复时间，但也会增强密度依赖损耗。无需补充热原子即可实现重复提取，但BEC形成次数受限于库耗竭与加热。在有连续补充的条件下，系统可进入周期性稳态；在参数范围内，部分BEC提取方案在短提取周期和高输入率时效率最高。

Conclusion: 通过残余BEC和热原子种子的动力学机制，可以优化酒窝阱中的重复凝聚体生产；部分BEC提取是更高效的策略。

Abstract: We investigate repeated Bose-Einstein-condensate (BEC) formation and extraction in a dimple trap embedded in a reservoir of thermal atoms using a kinetic model. The model includes pulsed extraction, evaporation, three-body losses, and thermal-atom replenishment. Three extraction protocols are compared: extraction of all atoms from the dimple (BEC and thermal atoms), full and partial extractions of the BEC, but not of the thermal atoms. Residual atoms in the dimple after extraction seed subsequent Bose-stimulated growth and reduce the recovery time between extractions, but also enhance density-dependent losses. For all protocols, repeated extraction of BECs can be achieved without replenishment, but the number of BEC formations is limited by reservoir depletion and heating. With continuous replenishment, the system can reach a periodic steady-state regime, after an initial transient period, controlled by the externally imposed rates of extraction pulses and thermal-atom input. Within the explored parameter range, partial BEC extraction gives the highest efficiency, particularly for short extraction periods and high input rates. These results identify seeding by residual populations of BECs and thermal atoms as a kinetic mechanism for improving repeated condensate production in dimple traps.

</details>


### [4] [Quantum tidal locking in orbiting Bose-Einstein condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11919)
*Yaoyuan Fan,Shuoyu Shi,Lang Cao,Ziyue He,Qiuxin Zhang,Dong Hu,Yu Wang,Qing Wang,Tianwei Zhou,Xiaoji Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文首次在介观量子流体——玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate, BEC）中观察到量子潮汐锁定现象，揭示了非简谐势阱中自组织同步的动力学机制，并预言了环形涡旋阵列的形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典天体力学中的潮汐锁定（tidal locking）源于角动量耦合与能量耗散，但其在介观量子流体（mesoscopic quantum fluid）中的对应物尚未被探索。本文旨在填补这一空白，研究量子体系中类似的自组织同步过程。

Method: 采用玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体在静态非简谐势阱（anharmonic potential）中作中心力运动，利用势阱非简谐性诱导的有效旋转势，通过持续的几何挤压（geometric squeezing）使凝聚体发生形变并驱动自组织同步，最终实现内禀旋转与轨道运动的锁定。

Result: 数值模拟表明凝聚体经历自组织同步过程，内禀旋转逐渐锁定至轨道运动；在更长时间尺度上，旋转物质波的相干演化导致环形涡旋阵列（ring-shaped vortex array）的形成。

Conclusion: 该发现确立了介观系统中的量子潮汐锁定（quantum tidal locking）作为一种鲁棒的自组织机制，可用于产生和稳定循环态（circulating states），拓展了对角动量耦合与同步现象在量子流体中表现的理解。

Abstract: Angular momentum coupling manifests widely in diverse physical systems, underpinning the emergent properties and collective dynamics across different scales. The tidal locking, which originates from the synchronization of rotational and orbital motions, has far-reaching impacts in celestial mechanics, reflecting fundamental processes of angular momentum transfer, energy dissipation, and evolution toward dynamical equilibrium. However, its counterpart in mesoscopic quantum fluids has remained largely unexplored. Here we demonstrate the emergence of quantum tidal locking in Bose-Einstein condensates undergoing central force motion in an anharmonic potential. The condensate follows a well-defined orbital trajectory in a static trap and experiences an effective rotating potential induced by the trap anharmonicity. The sustained geometric squeezing continuously deforms the condensate and drives a self-organized synchronization process, in which the intrinsic rotation gradually locks to the orbital motion. Numerical simulations further reveal the formation of a ring-shaped vortex array over longer timescales, arising from the coherent evolution of the rotating matter wave during the locking dynamics. Our findings establish quantum tidal locking in mesoscopic systems as a robust self-organized mechanism for generating and stabilizing circulating states.

</details>


### [5] [Grand-canonical phase diagram and chiral-current suppression at $π$ flux in a bosonic two-leg ladder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12159)
*Meng Zhang,Qingyun Xu,Zhi Lin*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文利用团簇古茨威勒平均场方法（cluster Gutzwiller mean-field method），系统研究了人工磁通下双支腿梯子上排斥相互作用玻色子的基态相图。通过分析超流序参量、各支腿流、手性流等物理量，区分了莫特绝缘体（Mott insulator）与超流（superfluid）相，识别了迈斯纳类（Meissner-like）、涡旋类（vortex-like）及偏置梯子（biased-ladder）等相态，构建了首个巨正则 $t$–$\mu$ 相图，并探索了以往难以触及的高填充和中等相互作用区间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人工规范场（artificial gauge field）下的玻色子梯子系统具有丰富的量子相结构，但此前研究多依赖密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）方法，计算成本高昂，难以覆盖大范围参数空间。本工作旨在发展一种兼顾计算效率与物理精度的平均场方案，以系统绘制该体系的全局相图，并探索前人未能触及的参数区域。

Method: 采用团簇古茨威勒平均场方法（cluster Gutzwiller mean-field method），在强横档耦合（strong-rung-coupling）条件下，对 $2\times4$ 团簇进行自洽计算。通过分析超流序参量（superfluid order parameter）、各支腿电流（leg-resolved currents）、手性流（chiral current）、相邻支腿电流比以及两支腿间的密度不平衡（density imbalance），区分不同相态。

Result: 在已有DMRG研究覆盖区域内，计算结果与已知相结构定性一致，验证了团簇古茨威勒方法的可靠性。首次构建了该体系的巨正则 $t$–$\mu$ 相图，揭示了磁通如何改变莫特瓣（Mott lobe）的形状、倾斜程度和范围。探索了高填充（$ρ\gtrsim1$）和中等相互作用（$U/t\in[7.69,9.09]$）等此前难以触及的区域。特别在 $\varphi=π$ 处，由于等效三角梯子映射的奇异性以及 $\varphi=π$ 与 $-π$ 模 $2π$ 的等价性，体系表现出非手性莫特绝缘态（nonchiral Mott-insulating state），与预期的手性超流趋势形成对比。

Conclusion: 团簇古茨威勒方法为绘制通量梯子玻色子体系的全局相结构提供了一条计算高效的路径，其结果可为未来超冷原子（ultracold-atom）人工规范场实验提供理论指导。

Abstract: We investigate the ground-state phase diagram of repulsively interacting bosons on a two-leg ladder threaded by a uniform artificial magnetic flux, using the cluster Gutzwiller mean-field method. In the strong-rung-coupling regime, self-consistent calculations are performed on a $2\times4$ cluster. By analyzing the superfluid order parameter, leg-resolved currents, chiral current, the current ratio on adjacent legs, and the density imbalance between the two legs, we distinguish Mott-insulating from superfluid regimes and characterize the observed states as Meissner-like, vortex-like (superfluid or Mott insulating), or biased-ladder. In regions overlapping with previous DMRG studies, our results qualitatively agree with the established phase structure, demonstrating that the cluster Gutzwiller approach balances computational efficiency and physical accuracy. We then construct the first grand-canonical $t$--$μ$ phase diagrams for this system, revealing how the magnetic flux modifies the shape, tilt, and extent of the Mott lobes. We further explore previously inaccessible regimes, including higher fillings $ρ\gtrsim1$ and the intermediate interaction window $U/t\in[7.69,9.09]$. Special attention is paid to $\varphi=π$, where the effective triangular-ladder mapping becomes singular. Owing to the equivalence of $\varphi=π$ and $-π$ modulo $2π$, a combined symmetry forbids net chiral currents, leading to a nonchiral Mott-insulating state, in contrast to the chiral-superfluid tendency expected away from $\varphi=π$. Our results offer a computationally efficient route for mapping the global phase structure of bosonic flux ladders and provide guidance for future ultracold-atom experiments in artificial gauge fields.

</details>


### [6] [Weakly interacting Bose gases in the canonical ensemble](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12208)
*Jonata S. Soares,Axel Pelster,Arnaldo Gammal*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该论文基于无相互作用玻色气体的正则系综描述，通过微扰方式系统研究了弱两体相互作用对热力学和统计性质的影响。在一阶微扰下，推导出正则配分函数的递归公式，其形式与巨正则系综中的费曼图相同但遵循不同规则。通过重新求和递归公式，能够刻画基态占据数的统计性质（累积量），并用接触相互作用的稀薄玻色气体在盒势阱中的实例验证了该方法，采用了与数字微镜器件实验相关的狄利克雷边界条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献中对弱相互作用玻色气体的描述多采用巨正则系综框架，但正则系综下有限粒子数系统的统计性质（如基态占据数分布）尚缺乏系统的微扰分析方法。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 从无相互作用玻色气体的正则系综描述出发，利用微扰论（perturbation theory）处理弱两体相互作用。在一阶近似下，推导出正则配分函数的递归公式，该公式的图结构与巨正则系综的费曼图（Feynman diagrams）相同，但遵循不同的费曼规则（Feynman rules）。通过对递归公式进行重新求和（resummation），提取基态占据数的累积量（cumulants）。作为具体应用，分析了盒势阱中具有接触相互作用（contact interaction）的稀薄玻色气体，并采用狄利克雷边界条件（Dirichlet boundary conditions）以与当前数字微镜器件实验对接。

Result: 得到了正则配分函数的一阶递归公式，并证明了该公式与巨正则系综的费曼图拓扑结构一致但规则不同。通过递归求和方法，成功表征了基态占据数的各阶累积量。在盒势阱中的具体示例表明该方法适用于当前实验可实现的系统配置。

Conclusion: 该工作为正则系综框架下弱相互作用玻色气体的统计性质分析提供了一种系统化的微扰方法，尤其适用于有限粒子数系统中基态占据数分布的表征。结合现代冷原子实验技术（如数字微镜器件实现的盒势阱），该方法具有直接的实验可检验性。

Abstract: Based on the canonical description of a non-interacting Bose gas, we work out how both thermodynamic and statistical properties change perturbatively with respect to weak two-particle interactions. Up to first order, we obtain a recursion formula for the canonical partition function, which consists of the same Feynman diagrams as the grand-canonical description but with different Feynman rules. Resumming this recursion formula for the canonical partition function allows one to characterize the statistics of the ground-state occupancy by its respective cumulants. We demonstrate the applicability of this approach by analyzing a dilute Bose gas with contact interaction in a box trap. To this end, we used Dirichlet boundary conditions in view of their relevance for current experiments with atomic gases, where the box trap is implemented, for instance, with digital mirror devices.

</details>


### [7] [A Pfaffian quantum Hall state of ultracold bosons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12409)
*Joyce Kwan,Perrin Segura,Yanfei Li,Tizian Blatz,Annie Zhi,Brice Bakkali-Hassani,Annabelle Bohrdt,Martin Greiter,Fabian Grusdt,Markus Greiner*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文在超冷原子光晶格体系中，通过Floquet合成磁场和贝叶斯优化绝热协议，实验实现了三粒子玻色子Pfaffian态，并测量到其特征性的配对关联与霍尔漂移响应，为工程化非阿贝尔拓扑序（non-Abelian topological order）和探索任意子编织（anyonic braiding）奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分数量子霍尔态（fractional quantum Hall states）是拓扑物理学的基石，其中Moore-Read提出的Pfaffian态具有p波配对结构并支持非阿贝尔交换统计（non-Abelian exchange statistics）的激发，有望实现拓扑保护的量子信息处理。然而，在电子体系中直接访问其配对结构一直受限。

Method: 利用超冷⁸⁷Rb原子在光晶格（optical lattice）中通过Floquet工程（Floquet engineering）合成磁场，再结合贝叶斯优化绝热协议（Bayesian-optimized adiabatic protocol）制备出三粒子玻色子Pfaffian态。通过位点分辨的多点密度关联测量以及霍尔漂移（Hall drift）实验来表征该态。

Result: 制备的态展现出Pfaffian配对关联（Pfaffian pairing correlations）；位点分辨的多点密度关联测量表明短程三体巧合事件被显著抑制，反映了其内在的配对结构；霍尔漂移测量进一步探测了态的输运响应。

Conclusion: 该结果建立了一种自下而上（bottom-up）工程化非阿贝尔拓扑序的实验途径，并为未来在合成物质中探索任意子编织（anyonic braiding）奠定了基础。

Abstract: Fractional quantum Hall states are a cornerstone of topological physics, hosting fractionally charged quasiparticles with exotic statistics that promise to enable topologically protected quantum information processing. Among these, the Pfaffian state introduced by Moore and Read implements a p-wave pairing structure that supports excitations with non-Abelian exchange statistics. Despite extensive study in electronic systems, direct access to its pairing structure has remained limited. Here we realize a three-particle bosonic Pfaffian state of ultracold $^{87}\mathrm{Rb}$ atoms in an optical lattice subject to a Floquet-engineered synthetic magnetic field. Using a Bayesian-optimized adiabatic protocol, we prepare a state exhibiting Pfaffian pairing correlations. Site-resolved measurements of multi-point density correlations reveal a pronounced suppression of short-range three-body coincidences, reflecting the underlying pairing structure. We further probe the state's transport response through Hall drift measurements. Our results establish a bottom-up approach to engineering non-Abelian topological order and lay the groundwork for future explorations of anyonic braiding in synthetic matter.

</details>

# hep-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [8] [Tripartite Entanglement in $e^+ e^- \to t \bar{t} Z$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11296)
*Dorival Gonçalves,Alberto Navarro,Kazuki Sakurai*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用标准模型螺旋度振幅，在$e^+e^-\to t\bar tZ$过程中重建12×12自旋密度矩阵，通过单对负性（one-to-one negativity）、一对多负性（one-to-other negativity）和真多体负性（genuine multipartite negativity）表征三分体系的自旋纠缠结构。研究发现：成对纠缠弱于集体纠缠和真多体纠缠，所有纠缠度量均随相空间积分范围增大而减小；在高亮度极化轻子对撞机上可观测到集体纠缠，但直接观测真多体纠缠具有挑战性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多体纠缠（multipartite entanglement）是复合量子态中超越二分纠缠（bipartite entanglement）的独特量子关联形式，但目前在高能碰撞过程中对其研究尚不充分。本文旨在探索在$e^+e^-\to t\bar tZ$过程中多体纠缠的可观测性，为高能物理中的量子纠缠研究提供新的实验平台。

Method: 基于标准模型螺旋度振幅（Standard Model helicity amplitudes），重建末态$t\bar tZ$的三分自旋系统的完整12×12自旋密度矩阵。利用单对负性、一对多负性和真多体负性三种度量，在三个递进阶别的相空间积分（phase space integration）水平上表征纠缠结构。

Result: 成对纠缠普遍被集体纠缠和真多体纠缠所压制；所有纠缠度量均随更多运动学信息被积分掉而降低。在$\sqrt{s}=1$ TeV的全轻子衰变通道中，假设量子层析（quantum tomography）可用，高亮度极化轻子对撞机（polarised lepton collider）可实现集体纠缠的可观测，而直接观测真多体纠缠则较为困难。

Conclusion: $e^+e^-\to t\bar tZ$过程是探索高能碰撞中多体纠缠的有吸引力的实验平台。真多体纠缠的直接观测需要进一步优化事件分析和观测量选择。本文建立的混合态（mixed state）框架可推广至任意三分自旋系统。

Abstract: Multipartite entanglement is a uniquely quantum form of correlation that captures collective properties of a composite quantum state beyond those encoded in its bipartite subsystems. We investigate this phenomenon in the process $e^+e^-\to t\bar tZ$ at a future lepton collider, where the final state spins span the tripartite Hilbert space $\mathscr{H}=\mathbb{C}^{2}\otimes\mathbb{C}^{2}\otimes\mathbb{C}^{3}$. Starting from the Standard Model helicity amplitudes, we reconstruct the full $12\times 12$ spin density matrix and characterise its entanglement structure through one-to-one negativities, one-to-other negativities, and the genuine multipartite negativity, evaluated at three increasingly inclusive levels of phase space integration. Pairwise entanglement is generally suppressed relative to the collective (one-to-other) and the genuine multipartite entanglement, and all measures decrease as more kinematic information is integrated out. Assuming quantum tomography in the fully leptonic decay channel at $\sqrt{s}=1$ TeV, we find that the collective entanglement is accessible at a realistic high-luminosity polarised lepton collider, while a direct observation of genuine multipartite entanglement is challenging and would benefit from further optimisation of the event analysis and observable choice. The study establishes $e^+e^-\to t\bar tZ$ as an attractive laboratory for probing multipartite entanglement in high-energy collisions and provides a general mixed state framework that applies to any tripartite spin system.

</details>


### [9] [Nonexistence of hidden-charm pentaquarks in $J/ψ$ photoproduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11808)
*Samson Clymton,Sang-Ho Kim,Hyun-Chul Kim*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过耦合道重散射机制分析J/ψ光产生过程，发现来自D̄*Σ_c道的重散射贡献比D̄*Λ_c道小约一个数量级，导致隐藏粲五夸克态（Pc̄c）信号在光产生中被抑制，从而解释了GlueX和CLAS12实验未观测到五夸克信号的原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GlueX和CLAS12实验在J/ψ光产生（photoproduction）过程γp→J/ψp中未观测到隐藏粲五夸克态（hidden-charm pentaquark）信号，这与LHCb合作组在先前的实验中报道的五夸克态（pentaquark）信号存在矛盾。本文旨在从理论角度阐明该“零结果”（null result）的物理根源。

Method: 采用耦合道重散射机制（coupled-channel rescattering mechanism），利用先前耦合道分析中动力学产生Pc̄c态的跃迁振幅。核振幅（kernel amplitudes）包含t-道重介子交换（t-channel heavy-meson exchange）和u-道重重子交换（u-channel heavy-baryon exchange）。整体归一化由单一参数控制。

Result: 发现来自D̄*Σ_c道的重散射贡献比来自D̄*Λ_c道的贡献小约一个数量级，原因是耦合常数gD̄*NΣ_c约为gD̄*NΛ_c的五分之一。Pc̄c共振主要通过D̄*Σ_c中间态（intermediate states）耦合到J/ψN道，因此该道贡献的抑制导致五夸克信号在光产生中无法显现。模型很好地描述了GlueX和CLAS12的截面数据。

Conclusion: 光产生实验中的零结果与LHCb观测到的五夸克信号之间并不必然存在冲突，本文的理论机制为此提供了一致性解释。

Abstract: We investigate $J/ψ$ photoproduction off the proton, $γp \to J/ψp$, to elucidate the nonexistence of hidden-charm pentaquark signals reported by the GlueX and CLAS12 experiments. Within a coupled-channel rescattering mechanism, we employ the transition amplitudes from a previous coupled-channel analysis that dynamically generates the $P_{c\bar{c}}$ states. The kernel amplitudes for the transition to the $J/ψN$ channel include both $t$-channel heavy-meson exchange and $u$-channel heavy-baryon exchange. We find that the rescattering contributions from the $\bar{D}^{(*)}Σ_c$ channels -- indispensable for the formation of the $P_{c\bar{c}}$ resonances -- are about one order of magnitude smaller than those from $\bar{D}^{(*)}Λ_c$, since $g_{\bar{D}^{(*)}NΣ_c}$ is roughly five times smaller than $g_{\bar{D}^{(*)}NΛ_c}$. Since the $P_{c\bar{c}}$ resonances couple to the $J/ψN$ channel predominantly through the $\bar{D}^{(*)}Σ_c$ intermediate states, their suppression prevents the pentaquark signal from appearing in photoproduction. With only a single parameter controlling the overall normalization, the present work describes the GlueX and CLAS12 cross sections well. These results suggest that the null result from photoproduction need not be in conflict with the pentaquark signals observed by the LHCb Collaboration.

</details>


### [10] [Revisiting the Axial Anomaly and Chiral Magnetic Effect in Dense Matter, with Applications to Axion Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11713)
*Deog Ki Hong*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文明确计算了致密物质中的轴反常（axial anomaly），证明其形式在真空和介质中保持不变，并通过反常Ward恒等式中的抵消机制解释这一结果。随后重新审视了在手征化学势和外磁场下的手征磁效应（chiral magnetic effect），发现介质中存在由费米子携带的持久守恒反常电流，其大小由手征化学势和费米速度决定。最后讨论了该结果在轴子物理（axion physics）中的应用，其中轴子暗物质充当有效的手征化学势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证致密物质（dense matter）中轴反常的形式是否因介质效应而改变，并澄清手征磁效应在介质中的具体表现，特别是其与反常电流的关系。此外，将理论结果与暗物质候选者轴子（axion）的物理现象相联系，拓展应用场景。

Method: 通过明确计算致密物质中的轴反常，并分析反常Ward恒等式（anomalous Ward identity）中由介质贡献的轴向流散度（divergence of the axial current）与赝标量密度（pseudoscalar density）之间的微妙抵消效应，论证反常形式的不变性。在手征磁效应的研究中，考虑耦合手征化学势（axial chemical potential）和外磁场（external magnetic field）的费米子介质，计算反常电流并验证其与手征化学势和费米速度的关系。

Result: 致密物质中的轴反常形式与真空中相同，即使在零质量极限下也不改变。在具有手征化学势和外磁场的费米子介质中，存在一种持久且守恒的反常电流（persistent, conserved anomalous current），该电流由手征化学势决定，并受费米速度（Fermi velocity）抑制，与反常轴向流关联函数（anomalous axial-current correlation functions）一致。

Conclusion: 致密物质中的轴反常形式不因介质效应而改变，手征磁效应在介质中以持久守恒的反常电流形式存在。这些结果可应用于轴子暗物质（axion dark matter）研究中，轴子场可等效为有效的手征化学势，从而将微观反常现象与宇宙学观测联系起来。

Abstract: We explicitly compute the axial anomaly in dense matter and show that its form remains unchanged from that in vacuum, even in the massless limit. This result follows from a subtle cancellation in the anomalous Ward identity between the medium-induced contributions to the divergence of the axial current and to the pseudoscalar density. We then revisit the chiral magnetic effect in a fermionic medium coupled to an axial chemical potential under an external magnetic field. We show that the medium supports a persistent, conserved anomalous current carried by fermions. The current is determined by the axial chemical potential and suppressed by the Fermi velocity, in agreement with anomalous axial-current correlation functions. We finally discuss applications to axion physics, where axion dark matter acts as an effective axial chemical potential.

</details>


### [11] [Evidence for New $D_s$-Family Molecular States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11717)
*Dan Jiang,Yin Huang,JiongJiong Zhao*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于高斯展开法求解薛定谔方程，利用多种介子交换势系统研究K*D(*)分子态，发现D_{s1}(2700)可解释为纯P波DK*分子，而D_{s1}(2860)和D_{s3}(2860)可描述为D*K*分子态，并预言了更多具有不同J^P量子数的分子态，为粲奇异谱和重味夸克味对称性破缺效应提供了新的理论基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受已观测到的KD(*)分子候选态D_{s0}(2317)和D_{s1}(2460)启发，其底奇异对应态K\bar{B}^{(*)}分子态被自然期待但尚未实验确认，这一差异可能反映了显著的重味夸克味对称性破缺（heavy-quark flavor symmetry breaking）并引入模型不确定性。现有研究对参数依赖性强，需要进一步的实验输入来约束这些效应，特别是其他可能的K^{(*)}D^{(*)}和K^{(*)}\bar{B}^{(*)}分子态。

Method: 采用高斯展开法（Gaussian expansion method）求解薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation），利用σ、ρ、ω、π和η介子交换势，系统性地纳入S波（S-wave）及更高分波（higher partial waves）贡献。

Result: D_{s1}(2700)可被解释为一个纯P波（P-wave）DK*分子；D_{s1}(2860)和D_{s3}(2860)可分别被描述为以^{1}P_{1}和^{5}P_{3}成分为主的D*K*分子态。此外，还预言了更多具有不同J^P量子数（quantum numbers）的分子态。

Conclusion: 这些结果为粲奇异谱（charmed-strange spectrum）提供了一种新的描述，并为重味夸克味对称性破缺效应的研究提供了有用的基准（benchmark）。

Abstract: Motivated by the observed $KD^{(*)}$ molecular candidates $D_{s0}(2317)$ and $D_{s1}(2460)$, their bottom--strange counterparts, $K\bar{B}^{(*)}$ molecular states, are naturally expected, although not yet experimentally established. This discrepancy may reflect sizable heavy-quark flavor symmetry breaking, which introduces significant model uncertainties. Current studies of heavy-quark flavor symmetry breaking effects still exhibit strong parameter dependence, and further experimental input is required to constrain these effects, in particular regarding possible additional $K^{(*)}D^{(*)}$ and $K^{(*)}\bar{B}^{(*)}$ molecular states. In this work, we examine whether additional $K^{*}D^{(*)}$ molecular states can be identified among the observed $D_s$ resonances. Within the Gaussian expansion method, we solve the Schrödinger equation using $σ$, $ρ$, $ω$, $π$, and $η$ exchange potentials, systematically including $S$-wave and higher partial waves. We find that $D_{s1}(2700)$ can be interpreted as a pure $P$-wave $DK^{*}$ molecule, while $D_{s1}(2860)$ and $D_{s3}(2860)$ are well described as $D^{*}K^{*}$ molecular states dominated by the $^{1}P_{1}$ and $^{5}P_{3}$ components, respectively. We also predict additional molecular states with various $J^{P}$ quantum numbers. These results provide a new description of the charmed--strange spectrum and a useful benchmark for heavy-quark flavor symmetry breaking effects.

</details>


### [12] [Factorizing quarkonium LDMEs and TMDSTFs using effective field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12175)
*Marston Copeland*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用有效场论（effective field theory）对NRQCD框架中的夸克偶素（quarkonium）产生矩阵元进行因子化，通过Hubbard-Stratonovich变换和场重定义，在速度幂次计数领头阶下解耦软与超软自由度，从而将产生矩阵元重新因子化为色单态复合场算符的期望值，并推导出TMD框架下新的软跃迁函数关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 夸克偶素产生过程涉及多个能标，其非微扰矩阵元（如NRQCD中的长程矩阵元LDMEs）之间缺乏系统性的关联约束，导致理论预测中存在较大不确定性。本文旨在通过有效场论方法揭示不同S波夸克偶素产生矩阵元之间的内在关系，并为横向动量依赖因子化（TMD factorization）框架下的非微扰算符提供更强的约束条件。

Method: 基于NRQCD框架，利用有效场论（effective field theory）将产生矩阵元进行因子化。具体地，采用Hubbard-Stratonovich变换和适当的场重定义（field redefinitions），在速度幂次计数（velocity power-counting）的领头阶下，将NRQCD中的软（soft）与超软（ultrasoft）自由度从重夸克和反重夸克场中解耦，得到混合vNRQCD/pNRQCD拉格朗日量。在此基础上将产生矩阵元重新因子化为色单态复合场（color-singlet composite fields）的矩阵元，并表达为原点波函数（wave-function at the origin）以及与色电场（chromo-electric）和色磁场（chromo-magnetic）胶子场相关的真空关联函数。

Result: 该方法验证了最初基于pNRQCD推导出的不同S波夸克偶素长程矩阵元（LDMEs）之间的幂次关系。此外，该方法还推导出TMD因子化框架中产生矩阵元的新关系，即TMD软跃迁函数（TMD soft transition functions），从而对这些非微扰算符施加了更强的约束条件。

Conclusion: 本文显著推进了对夸克偶素产生机制的理解，特别是在TMD因子化框架下，为相关非微扰算符提供了系统性的约束，有助于提高对夸克偶素产生过程的理论预测精度。

Abstract: We use effective field theory to factorize production matrix elements that appear in the NRQCD framework for quarkonium cross sections. By applying a Hubbard-Stratonovich transformation and appropriate field redefinitions, we show that the soft and ultrasoft sectors of NRQCD can be decoupled from the heavy quark and antiquark fields in a hybrid vNRQCD/pNRQCD Lagrangian at leading order in the velocity power-counting. This enables us to re-factorize quarkonium production matrix elements in terms of matrix elements of color-singlet composite fields, which we can write as the wave-function at the origin, and state independent vacuum correlators of chromo-electric and chromo-magnetic gluon fields. This approach verifies powerful relationships between the LDMEs of different S-wave quarkonia originally derived using pNRQCD. Additionally, it allows us to derive new relationships for the production matrix elements used in the transverse momentum dependent factorization (TMD) framework, known as TMD soft transition functions, providing a much stronger set of constraints on these nonperturbative operators. This work significantly advances our understanding of quarkonium production, particularly in the TMD framework.

</details>


### [13] [The Fundaments of Unity: ${\mathcal O}(1)$ Couplings in Quantum Field Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12393)
*Ben Allanach*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文批判性地审视了量子场论中无量纲耦合常数应约为单位1的预期，并提出“展宽”（spread）——即最大与最小无量纲耦合量级之比——作为量化该预期偏离程度的指标。若将独立同分布（IID）耦合用于参数化不确定性，耦合比值可能远超直觉预期，且其分布呈现肥幂律尾（fat power-law tails）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验量子场论中一个常见假设——拉格朗日密度中的无量纲耦合常数（dimensionless couplings）的量级均应约为1——是否在统计意义上成立，并量化该预期的偏差程度。

Method: 提出“展宽”（spread）作为度量指标，定义为所有无量纲耦合常数中最大绝对值与最小绝对值之比。对独立同分布（IID）耦合进行概率分析，推导出比值分布的闭合解析结果（closed-form results）。

Result: 对于20个IID标准正态耦合，两个耦合比值超过100的概率为0.29。即使IID耦合具有指数抑制尾（exponentially suppressed tails），比值分布仍呈现肥幂律尾（fat power-law tails），且该肥尾随独立耦合数量增加而增长。

Conclusion: 在统计不确定性参数化下，耦合比值远大于直观预期是常见现象，表明“所有无量纲耦合均为单位1量级”的预期并不稳健。

Abstract: We critically examine the expectation that in a fundamental quantum field theory, dimensionless couplings in the Lagrangian density should all be of order unity. We propose a measure to quantify the adherence of a theory to this: the spread (the ratio of the largest to the smallest of the magnitudes) of such dimensionless couplings, obtaining various closed-form results. If we take independent identically distributed (IID) couplings to parameterise our uncertainty on the values of the order unity couplings, ratios of couplings can be much larger than one might naively expect. For a theory with 20 IID unit normal couplings, the probability that the magnitude of the ratio of two of them is greater than 100 is 0.29, for example. Even when the IID couplings have exponentially suppressed tails, the distribution of ratios of order one couplings has fat power-law tails which grow with the number of independent couplings.

</details>

### [14] [Superconductivity near quarter- and half-filling of a strongly correlated triangular Hubbard band in twisted trilayer WSe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11495)
*Yungi Jeong,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Joonho Jang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究报告了在交替扭曲三层WSe2（triangular-lattice TTWSe2）中发现了超导电性，该体系实现了三角晶格哈伯德模型（Hubbard model），在四分之一填充和半填充附近均出现超导态，并与多种关联相共存，表明该平台是研究强关联三角晶格物理的有力系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三角晶格哈伯德模型是研究几何阻挫（geometric frustration）关联电子系统的基础模型，而扭曲双层过渡金属硫族化合物（TMD）为中等关联强度提供了实验平台。交替扭曲三层TMD因其镜面对称性有望实现比双层体系更强的关联效应，因此本文旨在探索该体系中可能出现的超导及其他关联相。

Method: 研究基于交替扭曲三层WSe2（alternating twisted trilayer WSe2, TTWSe2）实验平台，通过调节填充数（filling）和位移场（displacement field），系统测量了体系在不同参数下的电子输运性质，观测其关联绝缘态、超导态及关联金属相的出现和演化。

Result: 在半填充附近，观测到一个强关联绝缘态（correlated insulating state），其在较宽的位移场范围内稳定存在。在该绝缘态掺杂后，超导电性（superconductivity）在相图的一个广阔区域中出现。在四分之一填充附近，发现了另一个超导态，其两侧被关联金属相（correlated metals）所包裹。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，交替扭曲三层WSe2是一个极具潜力的实验平台，可用于研究强关联三角晶格哈伯德物理（strongly correlated triangular-lattice Hubbard physics），为探索几何阻挫体系中的超导机制和关联电子行为提供了新的途径。

Abstract: The triangular-lattice Hubbard model is one of the paradigmatic settings for studying correlated electronic systems with geometric frustration that can give rise to a variety of phases. Recently, twisted bilayer TMD systems have emerged as attractive experimental platforms for realising such a model in the moderate-correlation regime. Alternating twisted trilayer TMD systems are expected to realise stronger correlations than bilayer systems owing to their mirror symmetry. Here we report the discovery of superconductivity near quarter- and half-filling, together with various correlated phases, in alternating twisted trilayer WSe2 (TTWSe2). At half filling, a robust correlated insulating state persists over a broad range of displacement fields, signalling the strongly correlated regime. Upon doping, superconductivity emerges over an extended region of the phase diagram. Near quarter filling, another superconducting state appears flanked by correlated metals. Our results establish the TTWSe2 system as a compelling platform for studying strongly correlated triangular-lattice Hubbard physics.

</details>


### [15] [Unveiling the Interplay of Charge and Magnetic Excitations in HgBa$_2$Ca$_2$Cu$_3$O$_{8+δ}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11524)
*Karn Rongrueangkul,Martina Fedele,Leonardo Martinelli,Giacomo Merzoni,Roberto Sant,Nicholas B. Brookes,Dorothée Colson,Alain Sacuto,Götz Seibold,Sergio Caprara,Marco Moretti Sala,Giacomo Ghiringhelli,Riccardo Arpaia*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 利用共振非弹性X射线散射（RIXS）对最高常压临界温度铜氧化物超导体HgBa₂Ca₂Cu₃O₈₊δ（Hg1223）的电荷响应进行测量，发现动态电荷密度涨落（CDF）与磁激发（paramagnon）在相同动量处存在显著耦合，表现为磁激发能量的软化，揭示了电荷、晶格与自旋激发之间的强相互作用，从而支持一种协同配对机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铜氧化物高温超导体中电子形成库珀对（Cooper pair）的机制尚未明确。虽然磁相互作用和晶格振动（lattice vibrations）被认为分别主导关键电子性质，但两者是否以及如何协同作用从未被直接观测到。

Method: 以常压下临界温度最高的铜氧化物超导体HgBa₂Ca₂Cu₃O₈₊δ（Hg1223）作为研究对象，利用共振非弹性X射线散射（resonant inelastic X-ray scattering, RIXS）技术探测其电荷响应，并分析电荷、晶格与自旋激发之间的关联。

Result: 电荷响应由能量范围高达数百meV的动态电荷密度涨落（charge density fluctuations, CDF）主导；在CDF强度最大的动量位置处，磁激发（paramagnon）能量出现明显软化（softening），表明电荷、晶格与自旋激发之间存在强耦合。

Conclusion: 研究结果指向一种协同机制：动态电荷涨落在晶格、电荷与自旋自由度之间起中介耦合作用，为理解高温超导的根源提供了新视角。

Abstract: Unraveling the mechanism that binds electrons into Cooper pairs in cuprate high-temperature superconductors remains one of the most fundamental challenges in condensed-matter physics. While both magnetic interactions and lattice vibrations are known to govern key electronic properties, their possible cooperation has never been directly observed. We investigate HgBa$_2$Ca$_2$Cu$_3$O$_{8+δ}$ (Hg1223) - the cuprate with the highest $T_{\mathrm{c}}$ at ambient pressure - as a magnifying glass to probe the possible entwining of the excitations at the core of the pairing. Using resonant inelastic X-ray scattering, we find that the charge response is dominated by dynamic charge density fluctuations (CDF) extending up to several hundred meV, where magnetic excitations reside. At the same momentum where CDF are most intense, the paramagnon energy exhibits a pronounced softening, revealing a strong interplay among charge, lattice, and spin excitations. Our results point to a cooperative mechanism in which dynamic charge fluctuations mediate the coupling between lattice, charge and spin degrees of freedom-shedding new light on the fundamental origin of high-$T_{\mathrm{c}}$ superconductivity.

</details>


### [16] [Ambient and Pressure Dependent Superconductivity with Hydrogen Storage Potential in Quaternary Hydride LiMgZr2H12: A Comprehensive First-principles Insights](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11721)
*Jubair Hossan Abir,Tauhidur Rahman,Salauddin Muhammad Anis,Saleh Hasan Naqib,Raihana Shams Islam*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）设计了一种具有Pmmm对称性的LiMgZr2H12氢化物，其在常压下表现出约72.76 K的超导临界温度（critical temperature），且具有力学稳定性、良好的延展性和较高的可加工性，同时具备5.36 wt%的储氢能力，为常压高温超导氢化物的设计提供了新方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分子氢化物（molecular hydrides）因其氢准分子单元在超导中通常电子不活跃而较少被关注，而富氢化合物虽被认为是实现室温超导的强候选者，但其对极端高压条件的依赖严重限制了实际应用。因此，研究者希望探索在常压条件下稳定的富氢超导材料。

Method: 基于MgZrH2n家族的最新研究，设计了一种具有Pmmm对称性的LiMgZr2H12结构。采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）系统研究了该化合物的力学、热力学和动力学稳定性，以及电子和光学性质。

Result: Li掺杂显著增加了费米能级（Fermi level, EF）附近的氢贡献，并增强了电子-声子耦合常数（electron-phonon coupling constant, λ）。LiMgZr2H12在常压下超导临界温度（critical temperature）为72.76 K，在10 GPa下升至77.3 K。材料在0–10 GPa压力范围内保持力学稳定，具有延展性（ductile）和高可加工性（machinability index），远高于不锈钢。此外，其质量储氢容量（gravimetric hydrogen storage capacity）为5.36 wt%。

Conclusion: LiMgZr2H12是一种在常压下稳定且具有较高超导临界温度（72.76 K）的富氢超导材料，兼具优良力学性能和储氢能力，为在常压条件下设计高温超导氢化物（high-Tc hydrides）提供了新方向。

Abstract: Molecular hydrides have attracted relatively less attention in the search for high Tc superconductors because their hydrogen quasi-molecular units tend to be electronically inactive for superconductivity. In contrast, hydrogen rich compounds under high pressure have been widely considered strong candidates for achieving room-temperature superconductivity. However, their dependence on extreme pressure conditions significantly constrains their practical applicability. This work investigates hydrogen-rich superconducting materials that may be stable under ambient pressure conditions. Motivated by recent studies on the MgZrH2n family, a LiMgZr2H12 structure with Pmmm symmetry was designed. The mechanical, thermodynamic, and dynamical stability of the compound, together with its electronic and optical properties, were systematically investigated using first-principles calculations. Li doping in LiMgZr2H12 significantly increases the hydrogen derived contribution near the Fermi level (EF) and strengthens the electron-phonon coupling constant (λ) compared with MgZrH6. LiMgZr2H12 exhibits a critical temperature of 72.76 K at ambient pressure, which is further enhanced by applying pressure. At 10 GPa the critical temperature increases to 77.3 K. Elastic property analysis shows that the material remains mechanically stable over the pressure range studied (0-10 GPa). It also behaves like a ductile material suitable for current carrying applications. The material has a high machinability index, which is much higher than that of stainless steels. In addition, LiMgZr2H12 exhibits a gravimetric hydrogen storage capacity of 5.36 wt%, indicating its potential as a promising candidate for hybrid hydrogen storage technologies. This work offers a new direction for designing high-Tc hydrides at ambient conditions.

### [17] [Mathematical Basis for Analyzing Superconducting Phase Transitions Using Catastrophe Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11810)
*Jiu Hui Wu,Hua Tian,Kejiang Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过Lyapunov-Schmidt约化，建立了从量子多体路径积分到尖点突变模型（cusp catastrophe model）的严格数学桥梁，为利用突变理论研究超导相变提供了理论基础，并进一步将这一框架与提出的吸附势理论（adsorption potential theory）联系起来，揭示了高温超导中电子配对机制的突变拓扑本质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为超导相变（superconducting phase transition）分析提供突变理论（catastrophe theory）这一数学框架，并弥补量子多体路径积分与有限维突变模型之间的理论空白。

Method: 采用Lyapunov-Schmidt约化证明无限维有效作用量（effective action）在临界点附近微分同胚于有限维突变；从Ginzburg-Landau自由能泛函出发，将Euler-Lagrange偏微分方程约化为尖点突变模型；通过Hubbard-Stratonovich变换、Matsubara频率展开和Grassmann代数，从费米子虚时路径积分（fermionic imaginary-time path integral）推导出尖点突变模型。

Result: 严格证明了在临界点附近无限维有效作用量与有限维突变之间的微分同胚关系；将Ginzburg-Landau理论中的Euler-Lagrange方程约化为尖点突变模型；从费米子路径积分出发推导出了尖点突变模型的形式。

Conclusion: 该框架与提出的吸附势理论相连，阐明了高温超导中电子配对机制的突变拓扑本质；从第一性原理电子结构计算中精确微观推导吸附势将进一步增强该理论的预测能力。

Abstract: We establish a rigorous mathematical bridge from quantum many-body path integrals to the cusp catastrophe model by Lyapunov-Schmidt reduction, which provides a theoretical foundation for analyzing superconducting phase transition using the catastrophe theory. First, it is proved that, near the critical point the infinite-dimensional effective action is diffeomorphic to a finite-dimensional catastrophe. Secondly, starting from Ginzburg-Landau free energy functional, the Euler-Lagrange partial differential equation can be reduced to the cusp catastrophe model. Thirdly, the fermionic imaginary-time path integral to the cusp catastrophe is derived through the Hubbard-Stratonovich transformation, Matsubara frequency expansion, and Grassmann algebra. Furthermore, we connect this framework with the adsorption potential theory we proposed, elucidating the catastrophic topological nature of the electron pairing mechanism in high-temperature superconductivity. The precise microscopic derivation of the adsorption potential from first-principles electronic structure calculations would strengthen the predictive power of the theory.

</details>


### [18] [Proximity-induced unconventional superconductivity and chiral topological phases in twisted graphene/NbSe$_2$ van der Waals heterostructure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12104)
*Adam Hložný,Marko Milivojević*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文利用Bogoliubov-de Gennes形式化方法，研究扭转石墨烯/NbSe₂范德瓦尔斯异质结中近邻诱导的非传统超导性，发现由于23.4°扭转角将体系对称性降至C₃群，石墨烯层中可产生手性拓扑超导相，其陈数（Chern number）可达±2、±4，为手性拓扑超导的实验探测提供了可行平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在扭转石墨烯/NbSe₂范德瓦尔斯异质结中，通过对称性约化（symmetry reduction）诱导出手性拓扑超导相（chiral topological superconducting phase）的可能性。

Method: 基于Bogoliubov-de Gennes形式化方法，从第一性原理（ab initio）提取23.4°扭转角下近邻化石墨烯的正常态参数；根据C₃群不可约表示（irreducible representation）构建对称性允许的超导能隙函数（superconducting gap function），包含单态（singlet）与三重态（triplet）配对通道及其混合；通过计算拓扑不变量（topological invariant）随混合参数的变化绘制相图。

Result: 发现手性拓扑超导相（chiral topological superconducting phase）的丰富相图，其特征为陈数（Chern number）取值为-4、-2、2、4。

Conclusion: 范德瓦尔斯异质结的形成与对称性约化可改变配对通道的相对稳定性，可能稳定由NbSe₂近邻诱导至石墨烯中的手性分量，从而触发拓扑相；该扭转异质结是可通过准粒子干涉成像与输运测量探测手性拓扑超导性的有前景平台。

Abstract: We study proximity-induced unconventional superconductivity in a twisted graphene/NbSe$_2$ van der Waals heterostructure using the Bogoliubov-de Gennes formalism. The normal-state parameters of proximitized graphene are extracted from ab initio calculations at a twist angle of $23.4^\circ$, which reduces the common symmetry of the heterostructure to $\mathbf{C}_3$. We construct symmetry-allowed superconducting gap functions of the graphene layer according to the irreducible representations of the $\mathbf{C}_3$ group, containing singlet and triplet pairing channels and their mixtures. Computing the topological invariants as a function of the mixing parameters, we find a rich phase diagram of chiral topological superconducting phases, characterized by nonzero Chern numbers $C\in\{-4,-2,2,4\}$. While the nature of the superconducting order parameter of NbSe$_2$ remains debated, the formation of the van der Waals heterostructure and the related symmetry reduction can alter the relative stability of competing pairing channels, potentially stabilizing a chiral component that is proximity-induced into graphene and triggers the topological phases identified here, making the twisted graphene/NbSe$_2$ heterostructure a promising platform for chiral topological superconductivity detectable via quasiparticle interference imaging and transport measurements.

</details>


### [19] [Structural Changes and Transport Properties of $\mathrm{YBa_2Cu_3O_7}$ Locally Modified by a He$^+$ Focused Ion Beam](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12145)
*Ross Carter,Robin Hutt,Paul Zimmermann,Ainur Abukaev,Jan Ullmann,Simon Koch,Christoph Schmid,Manfred Burghammer,Reinhold Kleiner,Dieter Koelle,Edward Goldobin,Ivan A. Zaluzhnyy*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过实验研究了30 keV He⁺离子辐照对YBa₂Cu₃O₇超导薄膜结构相变与电输运性质的影响，揭示了辐照剂量与辐照区域横向尺寸对晶格膨胀、临界温度Tc降低及绝缘体转变的调控作用，为超导纳米器件的制备提供了技术基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离子辐照可诱导材料产生缺陷，进而引发结构相变与物性改变。本文旨在系统研究He⁺离子辐照对YBa₂Cu₃O₇高温超导薄膜的晶格结构、超导临界温度及电输运行为的影响，并探索聚焦He离子束（focused He-Ion beam）技术在制备超导纳米器件（superconducting nano-devices）中的应用潜力。

Method: 采用低电阻率测量（low-temperature resistivity measurements）、纳米聚焦X射线衍射（nanofocused X-ray beam diffraction）和原子力显微镜（atomic force microscopy, AFM）三种方法，对经30 keV He⁺离子辐照的外延生长YBa₂Cu₃O₇薄膜进行系统表征。辐照剂量范围为10–100 ions/nm²，辐照区域横向尺寸范围为30–5000 nm。

Result: He⁺离子辐照导致YBa₂Cu₃O₇晶格膨胀、临界温度Tc降低，并最终发生从超导体到绝缘体（insulator）的转变。通过聚焦He离子束（光斑尺寸约10 nm）可加工出绝缘区域，从而实现超导纳米器件的制备。

Conclusion: 聚焦He离子束辐照是一种有效的超导纳米器件加工技术，其效果依赖于辐照剂量和辐照区域的横向尺寸。结构演化与电输运性质改变之间存在密切关联。

Abstract: Irradiation of a material with ions can cause various defects that can lead to structural phase transitions and the modification of the material's properties. Here we study the irradiation of the epitaxyally grown thin films of the high-temperature superconductor $\mathrm{YBa_2Cu_3O_7}$ with $30\,\mathrm{keV}$ He$^{+}$ ions which leads to the expansion of the crystal lattice, decrease of the critical temperature $T_c$ and eventually transition to an insulator. Fabrication of such insulating regions with a focused He-Ion beam with a spot size of $\sim 10\,\mathrm{nm}$ is a powerful technique for fabrication of superconducting nano-devices. Using low-temperature resistivity measurements, diffraction with a nanofocused X-ray beam and atomic force microscopy, we investigated how the structure and the electric transport properties of $\mathrm{YBa_2Cu_3O_7}$ depend on the irradiation dose in a range $10$--$100\,\mathrm{ions/nm^2}$ and on the lateral size of the irradiated area in a range $30$--$5000\,\mathrm{nm}$.

### [20] [Superconductivity in the pressure-amorphized topological insulator CrP$_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12241)
*Chutong Zhang,Xiangzhuo Xing,Na Zuo,Bowen Zheng,Bin Li,Jiajia Feng,Xiaolei Yi,Yan Meng,Xiaoran Zhang,Bingchao Yang,Chao Wang,Xin Chen,Yongsheng Zhang,Xiaofeng Xu,Xiaobing Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 在高压下，Cr基拓扑绝缘体CrP₄发生不可逆非晶化并出现超导电性，最高超导转变温度达4.8 K（141.3 GPa），理论计算还预测了多重拓扑相变，这是首个Cr基非晶超导体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Cr基超导体极为稀少，尤其是兼具非平庸拓扑性质的体系，亟需发现新成员以拓展超导与拓扑物理的研究疆域。

Method: 采用高压实验压缩CrP₄拓扑绝缘体，通过电输运测量监测超导电性，并结合理论计算（theoretical calculations）分析电子结构与拓扑相变。

Result: CrP₄在约15 GPa经历从金属到类半导体态的量子相变；约70 GPa发生不可逆非晶化并伴随再次金属化及超导电性出现；超导转变温度（Tc）随压力单调上升，在141.3 GPa达到4.8 K；理论计算预测从强拓扑绝缘体（strong topological insulator）到平庸态再到强拓扑态的多次拓扑相变。

Conclusion: CrP₄是首个Cr基非晶超导体（Cr-based amorphous superconductor），为在非晶材料中探索超导与拓扑性质开辟了新范式。

Abstract: The interplay among superconductivity, magnetism, and nontrivial band topology represents one of the most compelling frontiers in condensed matter physics. The exploration of novel superconductivity in 3d transition-metal compounds, particularly the rare Cr-based systems containing strongly magnetic Cr ions, has long attracted attention owing to their unconventional pairing mechanisms that challenge conventional wisdom. Yet, Cr-based superconductors remain scarce, especially those possessing nontrivial topological character, underscoring the urgent need to uncover new members. Here we report the observation of superconductivity in pressure-amorphized Cr-based topological insulator CrP$_4$. Upon compression, CrP$_4$ undergoes an anomalous quantum phase transition from a metallic to a semiconducting-like state at around 15 GPa, driven by significant changes in the electronic structure. At approximately 70 GPa, re-metallization with superconductivity occurs alongside an irreversible amorphization. The superconducting transition temperature Tc increases monotonically with pressure, reaching 4.8 K at 141.3 GPa. Furthermore, theoretical calculations predict multiple topological phase transitions from a strong topological insulator to a trivial state and finally back to a strong topological state under pressure. Our study not only establishes CrP$_4$ as the first Cr-based amorphous superconductor but also opens a new paradigm for exploring superconducting and topological properties in amorphous materials.

### [21] [Substrate insulated Josephson junctions for superconducting quantum circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12262)
*U. Strobel,L. Radtke,L. Kamps,J. N. Voss,J. Lisenfeld,J. Luo-Hofmann,D. Reuter,S. Masis,A. V. Ustinov,H. Rotzinger*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于三维图案化低损耗衬底（three-dimensional patterned, low-loss substrate）的约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）制备技术，替代传统有机光刻胶（organic resists）工艺。该技术可制造多种几何形状和材料（包括钽、铌等高熔点超导体）的高质量三层结（trilayer junction），且电极不含已知退相干（decoherence）源的氧化物和有机物。通过制备并表征不同尺寸和几何形状的欠阻尼（underdamped）Nb/AlOx/Nb结，验证了该技术在高速、高温量子电路（quantum circuit）中的应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统约瑟夫森结制备依赖有机光刻胶，其残留物和引入的氧化物是量子退相干的主要来源，限制了量子电路在更高速度和温度下的性能表现。因此，需要一种能够避免有机和氧化物污染、同时兼容多种超导材料和几何结构的新型制备方法。

Method: 采用三维图案化低损耗衬底替代有机光刻胶，实现约瑟夫森结的制备。该方法适用于多种几何形状和材料，包括钽（tantalum）和铌（niobium）等高熔点超导体，并制作了不同尺寸和几何结构的欠阻尼Nb/AlOx/Nb三层结。

Result: 成功制备并表征了多种尺寸和几何形状的欠阻尼Nb/AlOx/Nb约瑟夫森结。电极中不含人为引入的氧化物和有机材料，有效消除了已知的退相干来源。

Conclusion: 该技术能够在避免有机和氧化物污染的前提下制造高质量约瑟夫森结，支持多种材料与几何构型，有望推动量子电路在更高运行速度和更高温度下的应用。

Abstract: We have developed a fabrication technique for Josephson junctions that employs a three-dimensional patterned, low-loss substrate instead of commonly used organic resists. The technique enables the fabrication of high-quality trilayer junctions from a wide range of geometries and materials, including high-melting-point superconductors such as tantalum or niobium. The junction electrodes are free from intentionally introduced oxides and organic materials, which are known sources of decoherence. We fabricate and characterize underdamped Nb/AlOx/Nb junctions of different sizes in several geometries. Such junctions enable manufacturing of quantum circuits operating at higher speeds and elevated temperatures.

</details>

### [22] [Bouncing Geodesics, Singularities, and the Cavity Thermal Product Formula in Asymptotically Flat and de Sitter Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11297)
*Sašo Grozdanov,Vita Movrin,Samuel Valach*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究渐进平坦Schwarzschild与Schwarzschild–de Sitter黑洞中“弹跳测地线”（bouncing geodesics）的存在性及其物理含义，证明这些轨迹对应于体区推迟格林函数中的“弹跳奇点”，并建立了弹跳奇点位置与空腔准正规模（QNMs）谱之间的普适联系，从而允许从反射超曲面上测得的QNM谱中提取黑洞内部信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动机在于理解黑洞高曲率区域（奇点附近）的物理性质，以及探测量子场在黑洞内部行为的信息。弹跳测地线作为探测这些区域的工具，其奇点结构尚未被精确描述，其与可观测谱（如空腔QNMs）之间的系统联系也缺乏建立。

Method: 结合Hadamard局部形式（local Hadamard form）与全局奇点传播定理（global propagation of singularities theorem），精确描述弹跳奇点。通过考虑弹跳测地线的各种锚定（包括零无穷远和宇宙视界），推导体区推迟格林函数出现奇点的临界时间。对于反射空腔中的黑洞，通过推导空腔版热乘积公式（thermal product formula），建立弹跳奇点位置与空腔QNM谱之间的普适联系。

Result: 给出了弹跳奇点的精确描述及其临界时间；推导了空腔版热乘积公式，该公式类似于反de Sitter（anti-de Sitter）黑洞的对应形式；通过标量场、电磁场和引力波在渐进平坦与de Sitter空腔黑洞中的具体QNM计算，验证了理论预测。

Conclusion: 弹跳奇点与空腔QNM谱之间存在普适联系，即使在宇宙学常数为零或正的情况下，也能够从反射超曲面上测量的渐近QNM谱中提取黑洞内部信息。这一结果拓展了全息对偶思想的适用范围。

Abstract: We investigate the existence and implications of ``bouncing geodesics'' in asymptotically flat Schwarzschild and Schwarzschild--de Sitter black holes. These trajectories, which probe the high-curvature regions near the black hole singularity, correspond to specific ``bouncing singularities'' in the bulk retarded Green's function. We provide a precise description of these singularities by combining the local Hadamard form with the global propagation of singularities theorem. We then derive the critical times at which the bulk retarded correlator becomes singular, considering all possible anchorings of the bouncing geodesics, including null infinity and the cosmological horizon. Finally, for black holes enclosed in a reflecting cavity, we establish a universal connection between the locations of the bouncing singularities and the spectrum of cavity quasinormal modes (QNMs) by deriving a cavity version of the thermal product formula, analogous to the one known for anti-de Sitter black holes. This relation allows one to extract information about the black hole interior from the asymptotic QNM spectrum measured at a reflecting hypersurface, even when the cosmological constant is zero or positive. We confirm this prediction through explicit examples by computing the cavity QNMs of scalar and electromagnetic fields, as well as gravitational waves, in spacetimes with asymptotically flat and de Sitter black holes.

</details>


### [23] [Lectures on Semiclassical Methods for Composite Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11317)
*Francesco Sannino*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 这些讲义通过半经典框架（semiclassical framework）对共形场论（conformal field theory）及其中的复合算符（composite operators）——特别是 $φ^n$ 形式的算符——进行了自洽的系统性介绍，旨在填补文献空白并帮助厘清相关概念。核心物理思想是：大 $n$ 下的重算符（heavy operator）产生高占据态，通过态-算符对应（state-operator correspondence）该态位于圆柱 $\mathbb{R}\times S^{d-1}$ 上，其标度维度（scaling dimension）对应于圆柱上的能量。讲义从共形对称性（conformal symmetry）出发，逐步构建半经典动力学，并在 $O(N)$ $φ^4$ 理论中具体计算了大 $n$ 标度维度的单圈修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 填补现有文献关于复合算符半经典处理的系统性介绍空白，帮助研究者理解重算符及其标度维度的计算框架。

Method: 采用半经典框架（semiclassical framework），结合态-算符对应（state-operator correspondence）、双标度极限（double-scaling limit）、作用变量（action variable）、Bohr-Sommerfeld 量子化（Bohr-Sommerfeld quantization）、周期鞍点（periodic saddles）、Floquet 理论（Floquet theory）、涨落行列式（fluctuation determinants）、Gel'fand-Yaglom 方法（Gel'fand-Yaglom method）以及 Gutzwiller 迹公式（Gutzwiller trace formula）。

Result: 在自由标量理论中通过三种独立方式恢复了 $φ^n$ 的维度；在 $d=4-ε$ 的 $O(N)$ $φ^4$ 理论中，于 Wilson-Fisher 不动点（Wilson-Fisher fixed point）处推导出经典椭圆解（classical elliptic solution）、Lamé 涨落谱（Lamé fluctuation spectrum）、零模（zero modes）和大 $n$ 标度维度的单圈贡献（one-loop contribution）。

Conclusion: 复合算符可作为量子场论（quantum field theory）集体扇区（collective sectors）的探针，该框架可推广至规范理论（gauge theories）、共形窗口（conformal windows）以及渐近安全场论（asymptotically safe field theories）。

Abstract: These lecture notes are intended as a coherent introduction to conformal field theory in general, and composite operators in particular, through a semiclassical framework for computing scaling dimensions, with emphasis on operators of the form $φ^n$. In doing so, they aim to fill a gap in the literature and to help decode some of the relevant concepts. The physical idea is that at large $n$ an (heavy) operator creates a highly occupied state. Through the state-operator correspondence, this state lives on the cylinder $\mathbb{R}\times S^{d-1}$, and its scaling dimension is the corresponding energy of the theory on the cylinder. The notes are organized as a self-contained route from conformal symmetry to semiclassical dynamics. Part I reviews the conformal group, primary operators, radial quantization, the state-operator correspondence, and operator mixing. Part II builds the semiclassical framework, first in the free scalar theory, where the dimension of $φ^n$ is recovered in three independent ways, and then through the double-scaling limit, the action variable, and Bohr-Sommerfeld quantization. Part III develops the general machinery of periodic saddles, Floquet theory, fluctuation determinants, the Gel'fand-Yaglom method, and the Gutzwiller trace formula. Part IV applies the framework to the $O(N)$ $φ^4$ theory in $d=4-ε$ at the Wilson-Fisher fixed point, deriving the classical elliptic solution, the Lamé fluctuation spectrum, the zero modes, and the one-loop contribution to the large-$n$ scaling dimensions. Beyond the explicit computation, the notes emphasize the role of composite operators as probes of collective sectors of quantum field theory, with extensions to gauge theories, conformal windows, and asymptotically safe field theories.

</details>


### [24] [Weak-field waveforms for generic relativistic orbits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11423)
*Stefano De Angelis*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将爱因斯坦方程重新表述为关于世界线的普通积分-微分方程（integro-differential equations），通过Schwinger-Keldysh路径积分消去引力场，从而在弱场展开中独立推导出运动方程与引力波形（gravitational waveform），无需散射-束缚轨道映射，也无需对势与辐射模式进行分离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在计算引力双体系统的可观测量时，存在两个主要瓶颈：一是需要将散射可观测量映射到束缚轨道可观测量（bound-orbit observables），二是需要处理复杂的分部积分恒等式（integration-by-parts identities）。作者旨在建立一种无需上述步骤的通用框架，直接推导运动方程与波形。

Method: 将爱因斯坦方程重新表述为世界线的普通积分-微分方程，利用Schwinger-Keldysh路径积分（Schwinger-Keldysh path integral）消去引力场；运动方程与波形计算相互独立，可先求解运动方程再代入重建波形；在弱场展开（weak-field expansion）的前导阶（leading order）与次前导阶（next-to-leading order）提出计算策略。

Result: 建立了不依赖散射-束缚轨道映射的运动方程推导框架，可植入有效单体（Effective One-Body, EOB）框架中，自动包含推迟效应（retardation）与辐射效应（radiation effects）；波形计算可在补充适当重求和方案（resummation schemes）后作为EOB方法的替代方案。该框架避免了分部积分恒等式这一主要技术瓶颈。

Conclusion: 该框架为引力双体问题提供了一种新的独立计算路径，有望简化可观测量计算流程，并可在未来拓展到更高阶的弱场展开或强场区域。

Abstract: We recast Einstein's equations as ordinary integro-differential equations for the worldlines, integrating out the gravitational field by means of the Schwinger-Keldysh path integral. The same framework allows the gravitational waveform to be computed for unspecified orbits. The two computations are independent: solutions of the equations of motion can then be inserted to reconstruct the waveform for generic orbits. The derivation of the equations of motion does not require a map between scattering and bound-orbit observables. Thus, it could be implemented within an Effective One-Body-inspired framework, with the advantage that retardation and radiation effects are automatically included: no separation between potential and radiation modes is required. Conversely, the waveform computation may provide an alternative to the Effective One-Body approach, if supplemented by suitable resummation schemes. We emphasise that computations in this framework bypass the need for integration-by-parts identities, which are the main technical bottleneck in the computation of observables. In this paper, we outline the general framework and present a computational strategy at leading and next-to-leading order in the weak-field expansion.

Abstract: A nontopological soliton of the Q-ball type in a Chern-Simons-Higgs gauge model is studied using both analytical and numerical methods. The general non-self-dual case is considered. It is shown that the soliton solution is an extremum of the energy functional at a fixed Noether charge. A differential relation between the energy, Noether charge, and the boundary value of the gauge potential of the soliton is derived. A linear relation between the components of the soliton energy is obtained. The parametric domain of existence of the soliton solution is determined. It is established that the soliton properties depend significantly on the form of the self-interaction potential of the scalar field. In particular, the energy and charge of the soliton can take arbitrarily large values only if the self-interaction potential has two degenerate zero minima.

### [27] [Modular quantization and black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11984)
*Suchetan Das*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文基于Witten提出的与背景无关的量子引力代数框架，通过变形CFT哈密顿量的模量子化（modular quantization），构造了描述黑洞非微扰性质的冯·诺依曼代数（von Neumann algebra），并利用开闭弦对偶和AdS/CFT对应，展示了光滑BTZ背景的Hartle-Hawking关联函数在半经典极限下的涌现，以及有限引力常数下非光滑描述（含拉伸视界与边界截断）的替代图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Witten提出的与背景无关的量子引力代数框架下，作者旨在通过变形CFT哈密顿量的量子化，捕捉黑洞系统的非微扰（non-perturbative）方面，并建立从模代数到背景几何涌现之间的严格对应关系。

Method: 作者在圆柱面上对一类变形共形场论（CFT）哈密顿量进行量子化，通过在哈密顿流（Hamiltonian flow）的不动点附近施加共形边界条件（conformal boundary conditions）并截断（cut-off），基于“涌现模Virasoro代数”（emergent modular Virasoro algebra）的最高权表示构造GNS希尔伯特空间（GNS Hilbert space），从而建立类型-I的冯·诺依曼代数。通过将哈密顿量识别为与固定参考KMS（Kubo–Martin–Schwinger）真空态相关的尖锐子区域（sharp subregion）的模哈密顿量（modular Hamiltonian），代数变为类型-III$_{1}$因子。利用“开闭弦对偶”（open-closed string duality）引入由不动点标量构成的涌现非平凡中心（center），并进一步通过模量子化重建精确的Hartle-Hawking关联函数。

Result: 在严格半经典极限下，边界极限中的精确Hartle-Hawking关联函数从光滑BTZ背景中涌现，并可通过模量子化从真空关联函数精确复现；而在有限牛顿常数$G_{N}$下，对应的描述本质上是非光滑的，同时包含拉伸视界（stretched horizon）和边界截断（boundary cutoff）。通过AdS/CFT将中心（center）纳入边界关联函数后，光滑视界被包含显式微观结构（microstructures）的拉伸视界所取代。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，模量子化框架能够将半经典光滑几何与有限$G_{N}$下的非光滑微观描述统一在一个代数结构中，为从边界CFT出发重建黑洞内部微观结构提供了一条新的途径。

Abstract: Witten recently proposed a background-independent algebraic framework for quantum gravity, wherein an observer endowed with a Hamiltonian defines a diffeomorphism invariant worldline algebra manifested by the modified Hamiltonian constraint. In the semiclassical limit, this construction admits a lift to a von Neumann algebra acting on a Hilbert space defined by geodesic in a fixed background. Motivated by this, we revisit quantization of certain class of deformed CFT Hamiltonian on a cylinder to capture non-perturbative aspects of black holes. We construct a type-I Von-Neuman algebra by imposing conformal boundary conditions on cut-offs near fixed points of Hamiltonian flow, acting on a GNS Hilbert space built from highest-weight representation of `emergent modular Virasoro algebra'. Upon identifying the Hamiltonian with the modular Hamiltonian of a sharp subregion associated to a fixed reference KMS (vacuum) state, the algebra changes to type-III$_{1}$ factor. We also discuss the structure of emergent Hilbert spaces using `open-closed string' duality after incorporating an emergent non-trivial center made out of scalars at fixed points. We further employ this modular quantization of a single holographic CFT to demonstrate how the boundary limit of exact Hartle-Hawking correlator of smooth BTZ background emerge in the strict semiclassical limit in an alternative dual description, while at finite $G_{N}$, the corresponding description is intrinsically non-smooth, featuring both a stretched horizon and a boundary cutoff. The exact correlator has also been precisely reproduced from the vacuum correlators in modular quantization. We further discuss the effect of incorporating gravity by including the center via AdS/CFT on boundary correlators, for which the description of a smooth horizon is replaced by a (stretched) horizon containing explicit microstructures embedded within it.

### [28] [Gauge Symmetry Degeneration in Lorentzian Deformed Light-Cone Null Reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11996)
*Limin Zeng*

TL;DR: 本文通过变形的光锥零约化（deformed light-cone null reduction）方法研究复 Maxwell 理论在 $c\to 0$ 极限下的行为，发现局域 U(1) 规范结构退化为守恒律，自由度从 $2(d-1)$ 增至 $2d$；并证明在单模 Kaluza-Klein 类假设下，无法同时保留非平凡动力学与第一类 Gauss 约束，最终出现的自由复标量理论只是截断过程的伪迹，而非 Carroll 电动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用显式规范不变的变形的光锥零约化（deformed light-cone null reduction）方法，分析复 Maxwell 理论在 $c\to 0$ 极限下的约束结构与自由度演化，并引入单模 Kaluza-Klein（KK）类假设进行严格证明。

Result: 在 $c\to 0$ 极限下，局域 U(1) 规范结构退化，Gauss 约束从初始数据限制变为守恒律，释放纵模为独立自由度，物理场数从 $2(d-1)$ 增至 $2d$。单模 KK 类假设下，速度型与约束型贡献不匹配，无法同时保持非平凡动力学与第一类 Gauss 约束，证明了一个不可行定理（no-go theorem）。

Conclusion: $c\to 0$ 极限下出现的自由复标量理论并非通过群收缩（group contraction）得到的 Carroll 电动力学（Carrollian electrodynamics），而只是截断程序的人为产物。

Abstract: In this work, we apply deformed light-cone null reduction method to a complex Maxwell theory in a manifestly gauge-invariant formulation. We show that the local U(1) gauge structure degenerates in the $c\to 0$ limit: the Gauss law constraint reduces from a restriction on initial data to a conservation law, releasing the longitudinal gauge mode as an independent degree of freedom (d.o.f). This raises the physical field count from $2(d-1)$ to $2d$. We prove a no-go theorem: under the single-mode Kaluza-Klein(KK)-like ansatz, no scaling of the field components can simultaneously preserve nontrivial dynamics and a first-class Gauss law, due to an inherent mismatch between velocity-type and constraint-type contributions in the parent action. Rather than representing the Carrollian electrodynamics derived via group contraction, the free complex scalar theory that emerges is merely an artifact of the truncation procedure at $c\to0$.

### [30] [Nonlocal Rarita-Schwinger theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12237)
*Fernando M. Belchior,Roberto V. Maluf*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文构建了自旋-3/2 费米子（Rarita-Schwinger 理论）的非局域扩展，引入两类解析形因子（标量形因子和狄拉克算子形因子），并证明在质量情形下自由 Rarita-Schwinger 约束保持完整，非物理的自旋-1/2 扇区不会动力学化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准 Rarita-Schwinger 理论描述自旋-3/2 费米子，但其局域框架存在紫外发散和鬼态等问题；通过引入非局域形因子（form factor），有望改善理论的高能行为并控制无质量与有质量情形下的传播子结构。

Method: 构造非局域 Rarita-Schwinger 拉格朗日量，分别引入标量形因子 $f(\Box)$ 和狄拉克算子形因子 $f(\slashed{\partial})$；对无质量理论采用协变非局域规范固定（covariant nonlocal gauge fixing），使传播子直接用自旋-3/2 投影子表示；对有质量理论，检验自由 Rarita-Schwinger 约束是否被形因子破坏。

Result: 对于 $f(\Box)$，传播子的张量-旋量结构与局域理论相同，但极点方程（pole equation）被标量形因子形变。对于 $f(\slashed{\partial})$，物理模服从非局域狄拉克型方程，色散关系（dispersion relation）发生修正，指数形因子下可显式写出。质量情形下自由约束保持完整，自旋-1/2 扇区不会动力学化。

Conclusion: 该非局域构造在自由层次上可以做到不含鬼态（ghost-free），但引入相互作用之前存在固有的局限性需要解决。

Abstract: In this paper, one constructs a nonlocal extension of the Rarita-Schwinger theory for spin-$3/2$ fermions. Two classes of analytic form factors are considered: scalar form factors $f(\Box)$ and Dirac-operator form factors $f(\slashed{\partial})$. The massless theory is treated together with a covariant nonlocal gauge fixing, which allows the propagator to be written directly in terms of the spin-$3/2$ projector. In the massive theory, we show that the free Rarita-Schwinger constraints remain intact for analytic form factors, so that the unphysical spin-$1/2$ sector does not become dynamical. For $f(\Box)$ the tensor-spinor structure of the propagator is the same as in the local theory, while the pole equation is deformed by the scalar form factor. For $f(\slashed{\partial})$ the physical modes obey a nonlocal Dirac-type equation, leading to modified dispersion relations that can be written explicitly for exponential form factors. We discuss the conditions under which the construction is ghost-free at the free level and identify the natural limitations that must be addressed before interactions are introduced.

</details>


### [31] [Entanglement generation between field modes mediated by a fluctuating conducting wall](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12338)
*Luca Giovanni Cammarata,Tommaso Fazio,Roberto Passante,Lucia Rizzuto*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了两个固定板之间一个可移动有限质量导电平板的量子力学行为，该平板由谐波势束缚在平衡位置。通过微扰理论计算了系统基态和场约化密度算符，并分析了两个子腔中光场模式之间的纠缠（entanglement）。结果表明，可移动壁的存在使两个子腔中的光场产生纠缠，这与固定壁情况形成对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究可移动导电平板的量子力学效应对两个子腔之间光场纠缠的影响，特别是与固定壁情况的对比差异。

Method: 采用Law哈密顿量的推广形式描述系统；通过二阶微扰论（second order perturbation theory）计算相互作用系统的基态；通过求迹（tracing out）壁的自由度获得每个子腔中场的约化密度算符（reduced density operator）；利用负性（negativity）解析计算两个场模间的纠缠，并数值计算总多模负性（total multimode negativity）。

Result: 两种情况下（双模和总多模），两个子腔中的光场均表现出纠缠，这与固定壁情况形成对比。

Conclusion: 可移动壁的存在使得两个子腔中的光场产生纠缠，纠缠量依赖于可移动壁的质量、振荡频率、与固定壁的距离以及所考虑场模的频率等物理参数。

Abstract: We consider a movable conducting plate of finite mass, between two fixed ones, whose mechanical degrees of freedom are treated quantum-mechanically and bound to its equilibrium position by a harmonic potential. The movable wall is thus subjected to quantum fluctuations of its position. This creates a system of two sub-cavities separated by the movable fluctuating plate, and two massless one-dimensional scalar fields, one in each sub-cavity. This system is described by an appropriate generalization of the Law Hamiltonian. The presence of the movable wall yields an effective plate-fields interaction, as well as an effective interaction between the field modes. We obtain, at the second order in perturbation theory, the ground state of the interacting system and the reduced density operator of the fields in each sub-cavity by tracing out the wall's degrees of freedom. We calculate the entanglement between two field modes, one in each cavity, by evaluating analytically the negativity; we then evaluate numerically also the total multimode negativity. Our results show that in both cases the fields in the two sub-cavities are entangled, in contrast to the case in which the wall is fixed in space. We discuss the amount of the field entanglement present as a function of relevant physical parameters of the system such as the mass and oscillation frequency of the movable wall, its distance from the fixed walls and the frequencies of the field modes considered.

### [32] [Nonadditivity in Quantum Field Theory: Replica Energies, Scaling Filters, and the Renormalization Group](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12367)
*Giacomo Santoni,Francesco Scardino*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出复制能量（replica energy）ℰ 作为连接统计力学（statistical mechanics）与量子场论（quantum field theory）的热力学桥梁，通过衡量配分函数对数（log of partition function）的非广延性（nonadditivity）来统一描述边界、拓扑、缺陷、长程力等效应，并给出重整化缺陷自由能（renormalized defect free energy）与熵 F 函数（entropic F-function）等通用框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典热力学中广延系统（extensive system）的配分函数对数 W = log Z 与系统大小呈均匀标度（homogeneous scaling），但边界、拓扑、缺陷、长程力等来源破坏了这一广延性。现有理论缺乏一个统一的热力学语言来定量刻画这种非广延性（nonadditivity），并将其与量子场论中的通用固定点数据（fixed-point data）如中心荷（central charge）、球面自由能 F、欧拉反常系数 a 等联系起来。

Method: 引入复制能量 ℰ 作为配分函数对数非广延性（failure of homogeneous scaling）的度量，构造微分算子 (1 - (1/d)L ∂_L) 从 W 中去除体贡献（bulk contribution），分离出对边界、拓扑、缺陷、长程力等非广延效应敏感的部分。通过高阶推广该滤波器，从有限体积或球面配分函数中提取局域抵消项（local counterterms）和通用固定点数据；对带有纠缠缺陷（entangling defects）的复制几何（replica geometry）应用同一滤波原则，得到重整化缺陷自由能（renormalized defect free energy）。

Result: 在 2+1 维中，复制能量的 n→1 极限精确等于熵 F 函数（entropic F-function）。该框架能够区分普通有限尺寸修正（finite-size corrections）、有隙相（gapped phases）中的拓扑依赖常数、亚广延分形子简并度（subextensive fracton degeneracies），以及具有长程相互作用的真正非广延系统（如自引力热物质）。

Conclusion: 复制能量（replica energy）为加和性（additivity）、缺陷自由能和重整化群不可逆性（renormalization-group irreversibility）提供了一个统一的热力学语言，架起了统计力学与量子场论之间的桥梁。

Abstract: Extensive systems have a simple thermodynamic signature: the logarithm of the partition function scales homogeneously with the size of the system. We show that the failure of this scaling, measured by the replica energy ${\cal E}$, provides a useful bridge between statistical mechanics and quantum field theory. The associated differential operator $(1-\frac1d L\partial_L)$ removes the leading bulk contribution to $W=\log Z$ and isolates the part that is sensitive to boundaries, topology, defects, long-range forces, or other sources of nonadditivity. In quantum field theory this thermodynamic idea has two closely related uses. For ordinary finite-volume or spherical partition functions, suitable higher-order versions of the same filter remove local counterterms and extract universal fixed-point data such as the central charge, the sphere free energy $F$, and the Euler anomaly coefficient $a$. For replica geometries with entangling defects, the same filtering principle gives the renormalized defect free energy. In $2+1$ dimensions, its $n\to1$ limit is precisely the entropic $F$-function. We use this perspective to distinguish ordinary finite-size corrections, topology-dependent constants in gapped phases, subextensive fracton degeneracies, and genuinely nonextensive systems with long-range interactions such as self-gravitating thermal matter. Replica energy therefore offers a common thermodynamic language for additivity, defect free energies, and renormalization-group irreversibility.

</details>

### [33] [Reconfigurable Strain Gradient Polarity in Crystalline Oxide Nanomembranes for Controlled Bending of Functional Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11370)
*Tiffany C. Wang,Minyong Han,Varun Harbola,Harold Y. Hwang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种利用自支撑单晶锰氧化物纳米膜制备的“气泡”（bubble）几何结构，作为一种可切换的双稳态纳米鼓（bistable nanodrum），能够产生相反极性的应变梯度，并通过调控外延应变与几何/力学边界条件实现0.01%至1%的应变变化，为氧化物薄膜中应变梯度的可控力学操控提供了可扩展平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究缺乏一种能够稳定、可切换地产生局部应变梯度（local strain gradient）的力学几何结构，难以将应变梯度与局部探针耦合以操控氧化物薄膜中的磁性等物理性质。

Method: 采用自支撑单晶锰氧化物纳米膜（freestanding single-crystalline manganite nanomembranes），利用外延应变（epitaxial strain）作为预应变源，通过控制几何与力学边界条件，制备出具有可切换双稳态的纳米鼓结构，其气泡形貌可通过设计开关能量学（switching energetics）进行配置。

Result: 该器件能够支持应变变化范围从0.01%到1%的应变梯度，并具备相反极性的可切换应变梯度状态。

Conclusion: 该平台为在氧化物薄膜中实现持续应变梯度（sustained strain gradients）提供了力学框架，支持可扩展的氧化物膜应用，如与局部探针耦合实现磁性的力学操控（mechanical manipulation of magnetism）。

Abstract: We report the fabrication and mechanical characterization of a "bubble" geometry for accessing local strain gradients using freestanding, single-crystalline manganite nanomembranes: a switchable bistable nanodrum, with opposite strain gradient polarities. By leveraging epitaxial strain as a source of pre-strain and with control of geometrical and mechanical boundary conditions, the fabricated device can support strain gradients with strain variation ranging from 0.01% to 1%. Switching energetics can be designed to configure the bubble morphology. By providing a mechanical framework for sustained strain gradients, this platform supports scalable oxide membrane applications such as the mechanical manipulation of magnetism, coupled to local probes.
