### [34] [Defect Tolerance in Trigonal Selenium Photovoltaics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11403)
*Jiban Kangsabanik,Kasper Tolborg,Thomas Olsen,Kristian S. Thygesen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，系统量化了三角硒（t-Se）中多种点缺陷的肖克利-里德-霍尔（SRH）复合行为，发现t-Se具有本征缺陷容忍性（defect tolerance），非辐射复合被大幅抑制，辐射复合亦不足以解释器件效率损失，从而提出t-Se可作为缺陷容忍型宽带隙光伏材料用于叠层和室内应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 点缺陷如何从根本上影响光伏性能仍是宽带隙吸光材料（wide-band gap absorbers）领域的核心问题。三角硒（trigonal selenium, t-Se）因其接近最优的带隙（band gap）而重新成为叠层（tandem）和室内（indoor）应用中的有前途的光伏材料，但其缺陷物理机制尚不明确。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first principles calculations），对一组数量庞大且化学多样性高的点缺陷，定量分析其辅助的肖克利-里德-霍尔（Shockley-Read-Hall, SRH）复合行为，包括辐射（radiative）和非辐射（nonradiative）两种复合路径。

Result: t-Se表现出本征缺陷容忍性（intrinsic defect tolerance）。尽管能隙中存在多个深能级（deep levels），但非辐射多声子发射（nonradiative multi-phonon emission）复合过程被大幅抑制，原因在于大的晶格重组（large lattice reorganizations）和每次复合事件中至少0.5倍带隙（EG）的能量释放。辐射缺陷辅助捕获速率也过小，不足以解释观察到的器件损耗。实际点缺陷浓度下的SRH复合无法解释硒光伏中的效率限制。

Conclusion: 三角硒被确认为一种缺陷容忍型宽带隙吸光材料（defect-tolerant wide-band-gap absorber）。研究还揭示了辐射与非辐射SRH复合速率对缺陷能级位置、晶格弛豫（lattice relaxation）、电荷态（charge state）和掺杂条件（doping conditions）的复杂依赖性，为优化下一代叠层及室内光伏材料提供了可迁移的设计原则（transferable design principles）。

Abstract: Understanding how point defects fundamentally influence photovoltaic performance remains a central question for emerging wide-band gap absorbers. Trigonal selenium (t-Se) has recently re-emerged as a promising photovoltaic material due to its near-optimal band gap for tandem and indoor applications. Here we quantify defect-assisted Shockley-Read-Hall (SRH) recombination in t-Se using first principles calculations across a large and chemically diverse set of point defects. Our results suggest that t-Se is intrinsically defect tolerant. Despite the presence of multiple deep levels in the gap, recombination via nonradiative multi-phonon emission processes is strongly suppressed by large lattice reorganizations and large energy releases of at least 0.5 EG per recombination event, while radiative defect-assisted capture also remains too small to account for the observed device losses. Consequently, SRH recombination mediated by realistic concentrations of point defects cannot account for the observed efficiency limitations in selenium photovoltaics. We explore trends in both radiative and nonradiative SRH recombination rates across the defect data set, highlighting their complex dependence on defect level position, lattice relaxation, charge state, and doping conditions. These findings establish trigonal selenium as a defect-tolerant wide-band-gap absorber and provide transferable design principles for optimizing next-generation photovoltaic materials for tandem and indoor applications.

</details>


### [35] [Topological Phase Transition in Mechanical Honeycomb Lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11427)
*Yi Chen,Xiaoning Liu,Gengkai Hu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过一个统一的质-弹簧蜂窝晶格（mass-spring honeycomb lattice）模型，解析地探索了面内弹性波（in-plane elastic wave）的多种拓扑相变（topological phase transitions），首次在同一晶格中实现了谷霍尔（valley Hall）、陈（Chern）和自旋霍尔（spin Hall）三种弹性拓扑绝缘体，并发现了谷霍尔与陈绝缘体界面上的拓扑界面模式（topological interface mode）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的三种弹性拓扑相（弹性谷霍尔、陈和自旋霍尔绝缘体）分别在截然不同的结构中实现，缺乏统一的理论框架。本文旨在通过一个简化的解析模型，在单一晶格中实现这三种拓扑相，并揭示其拓扑相变（topological phase transitions）的统一物理机制。

Method: 采用质-弹簧蜂窝晶格（mass-spring honeycomb lattice）作为统一模型，通过设计质量、刚度或引入科里奥利效应（Coriolis' effect）实现不同拓扑相。利用微扰方法（perturbation method）推导能带简并点（band degeneracy）附近的有效连续模型，并通过拓扑不变量（topological invariants）评估揭示拓扑相变（topological phase transitions）的物理本质。

Result: 首次在同一蜂窝晶格中实现了三种弹性拓扑相；首次发现谷霍尔（valley Hall）与陈（Chern）绝缘体界面支持拓扑界面模式（topological interface mode）；系统分析了拓扑保护界面态（topologically protected interface states）的衰减轮廓及弹性波特有的赝自旋指示极化（pseudo-spin-indicating polarization），并通过布洛赫波分析（Bloch wave analysis）和瞬态模拟（transient simulation）数值验证了结果。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了一个简洁统一的解析模型，用于探索弹性波的拓扑本质，并为连续力学拓扑材料（continuum mechanical topological materials）的设计提供了直观指导。

Abstract: Topological materials provide a new tool to direct wave energy with unprecedented precision and robustness. Three elastic topological phases, the valley Hall, Chern and spin Hall insulators, are currently studied, and they are achieved separately in rather distinct configurations. Here, we explore analytically various topological phase transitions for in-plane elastic wave in a unified mass-spring honeycomb lattice. It is demonstrated that the three elastic topological phases can be realized in this single lattice by designing mass, stiffness or introducing Coriolis' effect. In particular, the interface between valley Hall and Chern insulators is found to support topological interface mode for the first time. Perturbation method is used to derive the analytic effective continuum model in the neighbor of band degeneracy, and the physics in topological phase transitions are revealed through evaluation of topological invariants. The topologically protected interface states, their decaying profile as well as the pseudo-spin-indicating polarization specific for elastic wave are systematically analyzed, and these results are further confirmed numerically by Bloch wave analysis of domain wall strip and transient simulation of finite sized sample. This study offers a concise and unified analytical model to explore topology nature of elastic wave, and can provide intuitive guidance to design of continuum mechanical topological materials.

</details>


### [36] [Residual stress gradient in a thin film within the dislocation pile-up theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12007)
*A. V. Druzhinin,C. Cancellieri*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 基于位错塞积理论（dislocation pile-up theory），提出了一种预测薄膜段（thin film segment）残余应力梯度（residual stress gradient）的模型。通过力平衡条件推导出奇异积分-微分方程，并用配置法（collocation method）对多种初始应力分布进行数值求解，揭示了残余应力分布对膜段厚宽比和初始应力分布的依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为预测薄膜段中的残余应力梯度提供一个基于位错塞积理论的解析-数值框架，为约束材料系统（尤其是薄膜）中残余应力形成的更复杂模型奠定基础。

Method: 基于位错塞积理论，假设薄膜段初始剪切应力通过螺型位错（screw dislocation）在不可穿透的膜-基界面（film-substrate interface）处形成塞积而释放；将塑性应变与位错密度关联，得到连接残余应力与位错密度的基本方程；通过力平衡条件解析推导出非均匀残余应力剖面下塞积内位错的分布，得到奇异积分-微分方程，并用配置法对常数、线性、抛物线和指数函数等四种初始应力分布进行数值求解。

Result: 建立的残余应力剖面强烈依赖于薄膜段的厚宽比（thickness-to-width ratio）和初始应力分布；厚宽比越大，远离膜-基界面的应力松弛越有效；所有平衡状态下，塞积中均同时包含正和负伯格斯矢量（Burgers vector）的位错；位错总数及其密度分布随初始应力剖面显著变化。

Conclusion: 该模型为理解约束材料系统中残余应力的形成提供了关键一步，尤其适用于薄膜系统。

Abstract: A model for predicting the residual stress gradient in a thin film segment is developed on the basis of the theory of dislocation pile-ups. The initial shear stress within the film is relaxed via the formation of a pile-up of screw dislocations against the impenetrable film-substrate interface. Plastic strain is related to the dislocation density, leading to a fundamental equation, which links the residual stress to this density. The distribution of dislocations within the pile-up for an arbitrary, non-uniform residual stress profile is derived analytically by applying the force balance condition. This results in a singular integro-differential equation for the residual stress profile. The equation is solved numerically by a collocation method for various initial stress distributions: constant, linear, parabolic, and exponential functions. The solutions demonstrate that the established residual stress profile strongly depends on the film segment's thickness-to-width ratio and the initial stress distribution. As this ratio increases, stress relaxation becomes more effective away from the film-substrate interface. In all cases, equilibrium requires a pile-up containing dislocations with both positive and negative Burgers vectors. The total number of dislocations and their density distribution vary significantly with the initial stress profile. This model provides a critical step towards more complex models of residual stress formation in constrained material systems, specifically, thin films.

</details>


### [37] [Screening of the Coulomb interaction in Carbon Nanotubes: A First-Principles cRPA study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11441)
*Mohadese Rezayi,Hanif Hadipour*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文基于第一性原理（first-principles）计算，在随机相位近似（random-phase approximation）框架下，系统研究了不同手性（chirality）碳纳米管（carbon nanotubes）中远程库仑相互作用的电子屏蔽（electronic screening）行为，发现屏蔽效率不仅取决于金属性，还对手性和能带拓扑（band topology）高度敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究碳纳米管中降维（reduced dimensionality）和电子结构如何共同决定一维系统中的电子屏蔽行为，并澄清手性和能带拓扑对屏蔽效率的具体影响。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算，结合随机相位近似方法，对具有不同手性的碳纳米管进行长程库仑相互作用（long-range Coulomb interactions）的电子屏蔽分析，并将结果与纳米带（nanoribbon）等低维碳纳米结构进行对比。

Result: 碳纳米管中现场库仑相互作用（on-site Coulomb interactions）强度为3.5–5 eV，比纳米带化合物低约2–3 eV，进而影响长程相互作用强度并与激子（exciton）结合能较小的实验结果一致；类扶手椅型（armchair）和锯齿型（zigzag）纳米管尽管电子特性相似，但屏蔽效率显著不同。

Conclusion: 建立了碳纳米管中电子屏蔽的统一微观图像（unified microscopic picture），并将其与先前关于低维碳纳米结构的第一性原理研究直接联系起来。

Abstract: We investigate the electronic screening of long-range Coulomb interactions in carbon nanotubes with different chiralities using first-principles calculations within the random-phase approximation. Depending on their wrapping vector, carbon nanotubes exhibit either metallic or semiconducting behavior, providing an ideal platform to explore how reduced dimensionality and electronic structure govern screening in one-dimensional systems. The strength of on-site Coulomb interactions in these compounds falls within the range of 3.5 to 5 eV, which is approximately 2-3 eV smaller than the corresponding values in nanoribbon compounds. This reduction subsequently affects the value of long-range interactions, consistent with experimental results regarding the smaller binding energy of excitons in nanotubes. Despite their common carbon backbone, we find that the effective interaction landscape depends not only on metallicity but also sensitively on chirality and band topology. In particular, armchair and zigzag nanotubes with similar electronic character exhibit markedly different screening efficiencies. Our results establish a unified microscopic picture of electronic screening in carbon nanotubes and place them in direct context with previous first-principles studies of low-dimensional carbon nanostructures.

</details>


### [38] [Nucleation instability preempts relativistic domain wall transport in high-exchange ferrimagnetic nanowires](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11488)
*Pietro Diona*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过磁光克尔效应显微镜研究GdCo纳米线中的自旋轨道力矩驱动畴壁运动，发现高交换相互作用的亚铁磁体中，畴核化（nucleation）会先于相对论性输运发生，阻止了畴壁速度接近自旋波速度。实验绘制了畴壁输运与核化不稳定性之间的动态相边界，并确认核化阈值随脉冲持续时间降低，符合热辅助势垒穿越机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清亚铁磁体中电流驱动畴壁运动能否进入相对论性（relativistic-like）动力学区域的材料条件，尤其是高交换相互作用体系中阻碍这一机制实现的具体原因尚未明确。

Method: 采用磁光克尔效应显微镜（magneto-optical Kerr effect microscopy）观测高交换GdCo纳米线中自旋轨道力矩（spin-orbit torque）驱动的畴壁运动，测量不同电流密度和面内磁场下的畴壁速度与核化行为，并分析脉冲持续时间对核化阈值的影响。

Result: 在GdCo中未观察到速度饱和或高场坍塌现象；大交换相互作用将最大自旋波群速度（spin-wave group velocity）提升至约7–9 km/s，远高于实验可达的畴壁速度；但在此极限接近之前，增大电流密度和面内磁场会诱导畴核化，破坏稳态传播。

Conclusion: 核化是阻止高交换亚铁磁体进入相对论性动力学区域的关键机制；研究建立了稳态畴壁传播与核化之间的动态相边界（dynamical phase boundary），为理解亚铁磁畴壁运动提供了相图框架。

Abstract: Current-driven domain wall motion in ferrimagnets can approach the spin-wave velocity, giving rise to relativistic-like dynamics. While this regime has been experimentally observed in crystalline ferrimagnetic garnets and amorphous GdFeCo, the material conditions that determine whether it can be accessed remain unresolved. Here, we investigate spin-orbit-torque-driven domain wall motion in high-exchange GdCo nanowires using magneto-optical Kerr effect microscopy. We find that nucleation preempts relativistic transport. In GdCo, no velocity saturation or high-field collapse is observed. Instead, the large exchange interaction raises the maximum spin-wave group velocity to $\approx 7\text{--}9~\mathrm{km/s}$, far above the experimentally accessible domain wall velocities. Before this limit can be approached, increasing current density and in-plane magnetic field induce domain nucleation, disrupting steady-state propagation. We map the boundary separating domain wall transport from nucleation instability and show that the nucleation threshold decreases with pulse duration, consistent with thermally assisted barrier crossing. These results identify nucleation as the mechanism that prevents access to the relativistic regime in high-exchange ferrimagnets and establish a dynamical phase boundary between steady propagation and nucleation.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）和线性自旋波理论（linear spin-wave theory）对单层CuF₂进行分析。

Result: 交错磁序通过对称各向异性交换（symmetric anisotropic exchange）驱动强各向异性磁振子手性（magnon chirality），Dzyaloshinskii–Moriya相互作用仅起弱二级调制作用；声子与磁振子的手性响应在方向上互补；磁振子能带携带量化陈数C^M = ±2，确认了非平凡的交错磁拓扑性质。

Conclusion: 单层CuF₂是一个由单一对称性框架同时调控磁振子、声子和拓扑响应的平台，为二维材料中交错磁性与自旋-晶格手性之间建立了直接联系。

Abstract: Altermagnetism establishes momentum-dependent spin splitting through non-symmorphic crystal symmetries, yet whether these same symmetries simultaneously govern spin and lattice collective excitations remains open. Here we show, using first-principles calculations and linear spin-wave theory, that monolayer CuF$_2$ hosts both chirality-split magnons and cycloidal phonons controlled by the same $P2_1/c$ symmetry operations. The altermagnetic order drives strongly anisotropic magnon chirality via symmetric anisotropic exchange, with Dzyaloshinskii--Moriya interactions acting as a weak secondary modulation. Crucially, the phonon and magnon chiral responses are directionally complementary: cycloidal phonon angular momentum emerges precisely where magnon chirality is symmetry-suppressed, and vice versa. The magnon bands further carry quantized Chern numbers $C^M = \pm 2$, confirming non-trivial altermagnetic topology. These results establish monolayer CuF$_2$ as a platform where a single symmetry framework engineers magnonic, phononic, and topological responses, providing a direct connection between altermagnetism and spin-lattice chirality in two-dimensional materials.

### [40] [Unveiling Orbital-mediated Ultrafast Demagnetization in Rare Earth-Transition-Metal Ferrimagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11591)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁记录和自旋电子器件的速度极限由超快退磁过程中角动量转移的效率决定，但稀土-过渡金属（Rare-Earth-Transition-Metal, RE-TM）铁磁体中这一微观路径长期存在争议。

Method: 采用时间分辨磁光克尔（magneto-optical Kerr）测量技术，并结合扩展四温度模型（extended four-temperature model），在多种RE-TM体系（RE = Sm, Gd, Tb, Dy, Ho；TM = Fe, Co, CoNi）中进行实验验证。

Result: 建立了轨道介导的框架：强3d自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）如RE-Co中，通过直接轨道-晶格转移实现亚皮秒单步退磁；弱3d-SOC如RE-Fe中，角动量先转移到4f轨道，产生较慢的两步动力学，且第二步速率与4f-SOC强度成正比。

Conclusion: 3d与4f轨道通道之间的SOC驱动竞争是调控RE-TM铁磁体超快退磁的通用机制，为下一代自旋电子器件开关速度的理性设计提供了依据。

Abstract: The ultimate speed limit of magnetic recording and spintronic devices is set by the efficiency of angular-momentum transfer during ultrafast demagnetization, yet its microscopic pathway in Rare-Earth-Transition-Metal (RE-TM) ferrimagnets remains debated. Here, we establish an orbital-mediated framework in which 3d spin-orbit coupling (SOC) governs angular momentum (AM) dissipation. Strong 3d-SOC in RE-Co enables sub-picosecond, single-step demagnetization via direct orbital-to-lattice transfer, whereas weak 3d-SOC in RE-Fe redirects AM into 4f orbitals, producing slower two-step dynamics. The second-stage rate scales with 4f-SOC strength, revealing a distinct orbital-mediated dissipation channel. Using time-resolved magneto-optical Kerr measurements, supported by an extended four-temperature model, corroborate this picture across diverse RE-TM systems (RE = Sm, Gd, Tb, Dy, Ho and TM = Fe, Co, CoNi). Our results identify the SOC-driven competition between 3d and 4f orbital channels as the universal mechanism governing ultrafast demagnetization in RE-TM ferrimagnets, enabling rational design of the switching speed for next-generation spintronic devices.

Method: 采用高分辨率非弹性X射线散射（high-resolution inelastic X-ray scattering）技术，在300 K和500 K下对短周期GaAs/AlAs超晶格（superlattice）进行测量；并结合第一性原理晶格动力学（ab initio lattice dynamics）计算进行分析。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，声子相干性在高温下具有鲁棒性（robustness），为通过灵活的、自下而上的纳米结构方法（bottom-up nanostructuring approach）工程化声子能带结构和高阶声子-声子散射开辟了新途径，在声子超材料（phononic metamaterials）、微电子学和热电器件（thermoelectrics）中具有广泛应用前景。

Abstract: Similar to the behavior of elementary particles, such as photons and electrons, the interference of phonon waves in artificial periodic nanostructures coherently modulates phonon band structures, serving as the foundation for phonon band engineering. However, direct observation of such coherently modulated phonon band structures remains challenging despite substantial insights from existing literature. Here, utilizing high-resolution inelastic X-ray scattering, we observed coherently modulated phonon band structures with phononic band gaps in a short-period GaAs/AlAs superlattice at 300 K and 500 K. Our findings provide the first direct evidence of phonon coherence at and above room temperatures, signifying a major advancement in the artificial engineering of phonon band structures. Furthermore, our experimental observations and ab initio lattice dynamics revealed that the coherently modulated phonon band structure enhances three-phonon scattering channels, strengthening high-order anharmonic effects such as three-phonon scattering and optical phonon softening. Our observations demonstrate the robustness of phonon coherence at high temperatures, and opens new routes for engineering phonon band structure and high-order phonon-phonon scattering by employing a flexible, bottom-up nanostructuring approach, with extensive applications in phononic metamaterials, microelectronics, and thermoelectrics.

Abstract: Artificial intelligence is driving intense interest in alternative computing hardware capable of neural information processing beyond conventional charge-based electronics. Here we demonstrate integrated magnonic neural circuits based on nonlinear threshold neurons realized in nanoscale yttrium iron garnet waveguides. The neurons perform weighted summation of multiple spin-wave inputs, while a pump-controlled nonlinear activation defines continuously tunable firing thresholds. Owing to deeply nonlinear spin-wave dynamics, the activated neurons emit self-normalized outputs whose intensities are largely independent of the input amplitudes, while nonlinear phase self-adjustment suppresses sensitivity to the relative input phases, enabling deterministic neuron-to-neuron cascading without external signal restoration. Abstract: We present a high-pressure single-crystal X-ray diffraction study of the atomically precise $\mathrm{Au}_{25}(\mathrm{PET})_{18}^{q}$ cluster ($q=-1,0$) up to 10 GPa under strictly hydrostatic conditions. Notably, the internal Au-Au distances exhibit a monotonic contraction that quantitatively mirrors the compressibility of bulk gold. This invariant rigidity at the sub-nanometer scale demonstrates that the fundamental stiffness of the metallic bond is preserved regardless of size. Our findings reconcile previous contradictions in the elasticity of metal nanostructures by isolating the intrinsic mechanical response of the gold kernel from extrinsic structural and experimental artifacts.

Abstract: Machine learning is increasingly applied to accelerate the discovery of novel materials by exploring large compositional and structural design spaces. Method: 采用化学气相沉积（chemical vapor deposition）在Au箔上生长Janus型过渡金属二硫族化物（TMD）单层（SeMoS和SeWS），并对Au箔上的单层在极性和非极性溶剂中进行超声化学处理（sonochemical treatment），随后系统比较其与母体TMD的HER催化性能。

Result: Janus单层的HER催化活性显著优于母体TMD；极性溶剂超声处理进一步大幅提升活性；其中水处理后的SeMoS单层过电位低至~63 mV，Tafel斜率~42 mV/dec，交换电流密度~10$^{-3}$ mA cm$^{-2}$，接近铂的水平。

Conclusion: Janus单层催化性能增强的主要机制是Au表面重构引起的拉伸应变（tensile strain）与缺陷形成（defect formation），实验观测与密度泛函理论（DFT）计算结果一致；超声化学处理对催化性能的提升突显了基于Janus二维材料开发新型HER催化体系的重要性。

Abstract: 2D electrocatalysts that enable hydrogen evolution at low overpotentials offer an attractive alternative to expensive platinum-based systems. Here, we report the growth of Janus transition metal dichalcogenide (TMD) monolayers (MLs), SeMoS and SeWS, on Au foils using chemical vapor deposition, and systematically compare their catalytic properties in the context of hydrogen evolution reaction (HER) with those of their parent TMDs. The Janus MLs exhibited significantly enhanced catalytic performance relative to the parent TMDs. Furthermore, these MLs on Au foils were subjected to sonochemical treatment in polar and non-polar solvents, in which the treatment with polar solvents led to a substantial improvement in the HER activity of Janus MLs. In particular, SeMoS MLs treated with water showed a low overpotential of ~63 mV, a Tafel slope of ~42 mV/dec, and an exchange current density of ~10$^{-3}$ mA cm$^{- 2}$, approaching that of platinum. Analyses indicate that enhanced electrocatalytic activity is associated with tensile strain induced by Au surface restructuring and the formation of defects in Janus MLs, as shown by experimental observations and by density functional theory calculations. The enhancement in catalytic performance due to sonochemical treatment emphasizes the importance of our results for developing novel catalytic systems for HER based on Janus 2D materials.

</details>


### [46] [Spin-Polarized Electronic Structure and Chemical Bonding Data for 2,500+ Halide Double Perovskites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11928)
*Luc Walterbos,Alex McEwan,Ravindra Shinde,Janine George,Linn Leppert*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

Method: 以Bartel等人提出的τ容差因子（τ tolerance factor）筛选出的稳定化合物为研究对象，聚焦Cs₂BB'X₆（X = I, Br, Cl, F）家族，采用杂化泛函密度泛函理论（hybrid-functional density functional theory）计算超过2,500种化合物的态密度（density of states, DOS）；同时利用Lobster工具进行化学键合分析，并基于UMAP（Uniform Manifold Approximation and Projection）提供可视化与交互式探索应用。

Abstract: Halide double perovskites (A$_2$BB'X$_6$) are a long-known class of materials that has recently been rediscovered for diverse applications, including photovoltaics, photocatalysis, and radiation detection. Their doubled unit cell provides immense chemical tunability, allowing the incorporation of magnetic ions and enabling access to a wide range of electronic-structure features, including different band-edge characters, alignments, and symmetries. Magnetic elements may further introduce spin degrees of freedom and magnetic behaviour, thereby broadening the functional landscape of these compounds. Here, we present the first comprehensive database of spin-polarised electronic-structure data for all halide double perovskites predicted to be stable by the recently introduced $τ$ tolerance factor by Bartel et al. The dataset focuses on the Cs$_2$BB'X$_6$ family, with X = I, Br, Cl, and F, and includes density of states (DOS) for $>$2,500 compounds, calculated using hybrid-functional density functional theory. Among these, 719 compounds exhibit band gaps in the visible range and 118 display half-metallic character. In addition, we provide chemical-bonding analysis using \textsc{lobster}, which provides insights into orbital interactions across the dataset. To facilitate exploration, we further offer UMAP-based visualisations and an interactive app for systematic investigation of chemical composition, electronic structure, and magnetic properties.

### [47] [Boron Co-Alloying in AlScN Wurtzite Ferroelectrics: Insights from an 850-Sample Combinatorial Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11954)
*Federica Messi,Nathan Rodkey,Manuel Kober-Czerny,Sebastian Siol*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过组合高通量方法系统研究了AlScBN四元铁电材料体系的全部组分空间，发现硼（B）与钪（Sc）共掺杂可将矫顽场（coercive field）从7 MV/cm降至3 MV/cm并提升循环耐久性（cycling endurance），同时减少对稀缺元素Sc的依赖，将AlScBN确立为一种可规模化、CMOS兼容的铁电材料（ferroelectric）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AlScN纤锌矿型铁电材料（wurtzite ferroelectrics）在高能效非易失性存储器（non-volatile memory）领域具有前景，但其高矫顽场（coercive field）和有限的循环耐久性（cycling endurance）制约了性能优化。为了独立调控化学与结构性质，研究者提出在AlScN中掺入硼（B）形成AlScBN四元体系（quaternary system），但尚未有系统研究覆盖其全部组分空间。

Method: 采用组合方法（combinatorial approach），包括在250°C低温下使用高功率脉冲磁控溅射（HiPIMS）进行梯度沉积（gradient deposition），并结合薄膜性质的自动分析。研究在AlScBN相空间（phase space）中分析了总计850个独特样品，同时构建并表征了组合器件库（combinatorial device libraries），并通过XPS电荷转移分析（XPS charge transfer analysis）实验验证键离子性（bond ionicity）与矫顽场的关系。

Result: XPS分析实验证实，在AlScN和AlScBN体系中，键离子性（bond ionicity）与矫顽场降低相关，而AlBN体系呈现相反趋势。Sc和B共掺杂可将矫顽场从7 MV/cm降至3 MV/cm，同时保持130-150 μC/cm²的高剩余极化（remanent polarization）。B共合金化可降低降低矫顽场所需的Sc含量，从而减少对稀缺元素Sc的依赖；此外，B共合金化显著提升了循环耐久性，这与缺陷密度（defect density）降低有关。

Conclusion: AlScBN被确立为一种可规模化、CMOS兼容的铁电材料（CMOS-compatible ferroelectric），是AlScN的有力替代方案。

Abstract: AlScN wurtzite ferroelectrics are promising candidates for energy-efficient non-volatile memory. However, AlScN suffers from a high coercive field and reduced cycling endurance, and the limited tunability of its properties constrains further optimization. Co-doping AlScN with boron offers the promise of independently tailoring the chemical and structural properties, making AlScBN an attractive quaternary system. This material has already been explored for a few selected compositions, however, no systematic study of the full AlScBN compositional space exists. A combinatorial approach consisting of gradient deposition with HiPIMS at low temperatures of 250°C and automatic analysis of film properties allowed us to analyze a total of 850 unique samples within the AlScBN phase space. In addition to a full screening of the materials' chemical and structural properties, we fabricate and characterize combinatorial device libraries. XPS charge transfer analysis experimentally confirms that bond ionicity correlates with a reduction in the coercive field for AlScN and AlScBN systems, opposite trends are instead observed for AlBN. While the films maintain a high remanent polarization of 130-150 μC/cm2, Sc and B co-doping reduces the coercive field from 7 MV/cm to 3 MV/cm. Notably, B co-alloying lowers the amount of Sc needed to lower the coercive field, reducing reliance on this scarce element. In addition, we find that co-alloying with B, notably improves cycling endurance, which is related to a reduction in defect density. These results establish AlScBN as a scalable, CMOS-compatible ferroelectric, positioning it as an interesting alternative to AlScN.

### [48] [Interfacial Coupling and Sparse Intercalation of 7-Atom-Wide Armchair Graphene Nanoribbons by N-Heterocyclic Carbene Monolayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11973)
*Dominik Lüthi,Lin Yang,Xiuling Yu,Ji Ma,Xinliang Feng,Carlo A. Pignedoli,Roman Fasel,Gabriela Borin Barin*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过实验和理论计算研究了N-杂环卡宾（NHCs）对金基底上7-原子宽扶手椅型石墨烯纳米带（7-AGNRs）的插层行为，发现NHC的吸附几何构型（平躺二聚体 vs. 直立单体）显著影响插层效率，揭示了分子吸附几何和堆积方式是控制石墨烯纳米带-金属界面插层的关键参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金属基底上合成的石墨烯纳米带（graphene nanoribbons, GNRs）会受到基底电子耦合和屏蔽效应的影响，这些效应虽弱但会改变GNR的观测性质并增加其向器件兼容基底转移的难度。自组装单层（self-assembled monolayers, SAMs）插层有望减弱这种界面相互作用，因此需要系统研究插层过程的关键控制因素。

Method: 采用低温扫描隧道显微镜（low-temperature scanning tunneling microscopy, LT-STM）和扫描隧道谱（scanning tunneling spectroscopy, STS）、拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）以及密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算，系统研究了N-杂环卡宾（N-heterocyclic carbenes, NHCs）对Au(111)表面上7-原子宽扶手椅型石墨烯纳米带（7-AGNRs）的插层行为。

Result: 甲基取代的NHCs形成平躺二聚体，可部分插层GNRs，产生局部去耦合的片段；而体积更大的异丙基取代NHCs则形成直立单体，将GNR嵌入单层内，阻止了插层。总体插层产率较低，表明将纳米带从金表面抬升在能量上是代价高昂的。

Conclusion: 分子的吸附几何构型（adsorption geometry）和堆积方式（packing）是控制GNR-金属界面插层的关键参数。该发现为合理设计去耦合层（decoupling layers）以促进基于GNR的器件集成路径提供了指导意义。

Abstract: Graphene nanoribbons (GNRs) synthesized on metal substrates experience electronic coupling and screening from the underlying surface, which, although often weak, can modify their observed properties and complicate their transfer to device-compatible substrates. Intercalation of GNRs by self-assembled monolayers (SAMs) offers a possible route to reduce this interaction. Here, we investigate the intercalation of 7-atom-wide armchair graphene nanoribbons (7-AGNRs) on Au(111) using N-heterocyclic carbenes (NHCs). Low-temperature scanning tunneling microscopy and spectroscopy, Raman spectroscopy, and density functional theory calculations reveal that the adsorption geometry of the NHCs strongly influences the intercalation yield for GNRs. Methyl-substituted NHCs form flat-lying dimers that partially intercalate the GNRs, producing locally decoupled segments. In contrast, bulkier isopropyl-substituted NHCs form upright monomers that embed the GNRs within the monolayer, preventing intercalation. The low intercalation yield indicates that lifting the nanoribbon from the Au surface is energetically costly. These results establish molecular adsorption geometry and packing as key parameters controlling intercalation at GNR-metal interfaces, with implications for the rational design of decoupling layers for GNR-based device integration pathways.

### [49] [Coupling Chirality, Polar Order, and Altermagnetic Spin Splitting in a Hybrid Manganese Chloride](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11985)
*Li Liang,Ding Ning,Mingqiang Gu,Shanshan Wang,Alessandro Stroppa*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算与自旋空间群分析，预测杂化锰卤化物中补偿磁态具有交错磁（altermagnetism）自旋劈裂，揭示了手性、极性和磁自由度耦合对电子与磁光响应的符号规则，并提出通过有机阳离子设计调控自旋劈裂的化学路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在单一晶格中实现分子手性（chirality）、极性序（polar order）和磁交换（magnetic exchange）的共存，并探索这些自由度如何协同调控自旋劈裂与磁光响应，以开辟通过化学设计控制自旋电子学性质的途径。

Method: 结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）与自旋空间群分析（spin-space-group analysis），对合成的对映体对[(R)/(S)-MPA]2[MnCl4(H2O)]进行理论预测。

Result: 预言该材料在非相对论极限下具有交错磁自旋劈裂；推导出电子和磁光响应的符号规则：同时反转手性和极性或单独反转磁畴会翻转整个布里渊区的自旋劈裂符号，而单独反转手性或极性仅在对称性选择的区域改变符号；考虑自旋轨道耦合后，反转手性或磁序会翻转克尔旋转角，而改变极性变体则无影响。

Conclusion: 手性、极性和磁自由度的耦合决定了自旋劈裂的符号与动量模式，可通过调控有机阳离子的手性和极性来设计杂化锰卤化物中的自旋劈裂，为分子手性向对称性控制的自旋电子学和磁光读出功能转化提供了可行的化学路径。

Abstract: Hybrid manganese halides enable the coexistence of molecular chirality, polar order, and magnetic exchange within a single lattice. Here, we combine first-principles calculations with spin-space-group analysis to investigate the synthesized enantiomeric pair [(R)/(S)-MPA]2[MnCl4(H2O)] (MPA = beta-methylphenethylammonium). We predict that its compensated magnetic state hosts altermagnetic spin splitting in the nonrelativistic limit, and that the coupled chiral, polar, and magnetic degrees of freedom define a symmetry-related manifold. From this manifold, we derive simple sign rules for the electronic and magneto-optical response: reversing both chirality and polarity, or reversing the magnetic domain alone, inverts the spin splitting throughout the Brillouin zone, whereas reversing chirality alone or polarity alone changes the spin-splitting sign only in symmetry-selected regions. With spin-orbit coupling, reversing chirality or magnetic order flips the Kerr rotation angle, while changing the polar variant leaves it unchanged. These results reveal a chemically accessible route to translate molecular handedness into symmetry-controlled spin splitting and magneto-optical readout in hybrid manganese halides. Critically, we show that the sign and momentum pattern of the splitting are governed by the interplay of the chiral, polar, and magnetic degrees of freedom. This interplay opens the possibility to control the spin splitting through a judicious design of the organic cations, by modulating their chirality and polarity.

### [50] [In Situ Dynamics of the Microscopic Crystallographic Dehydration Pathway in a Model Channel Hydrate, Theophylline](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12029)
*Natalia Koniuch,Sang T. Pham,Mohsen Danaie,Fanny Costa,Zabeada Aslam,Stephanie Foster,Helen Blade,Les Hughes,Nicole Hondow,Rik Drummond-Brydson,Sean M. Collins,Andy P. Brown*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究利用原位低剂量扫描电子衍射（SED）技术，以茶碱一水合物为模型，揭示了分子晶体水合物固态脱水经历两步重构型拓扑定向相变（reconstructive topotactic solid-state transformation），阐明了表面控制的质量损失、形态变化与晶格取向如何共同驱动这一过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固态相变在分子晶体水合物（molecular crystal hydrates）中决定其稳定性与功能性能，广泛应用于制药、农用化学品及配位框架材料等领域。尽管脱水过程中会发生显著的结构重组，但微观晶体学路径仍不清楚，因此需要直接的原位观测手段来阐明其机制。

Method: 以茶碱一水合物（theophylline monohydrate）为模型体系，采用原位低剂量扫描电子衍射（scanning electron diffraction, SED）技术，同时对单个颗粒的形貌变化、晶体学相及晶体取向进行成像和追踪。

Result: 脱水过程通过两步重构型拓扑定向固态相变（reconstructive topotactic solid-state transformation）完成：首先在靠近水通道侧的特定表面发生各向异性的质量损失（暗示一水合物具有非中心对称晶体结构）；随后在母体一水合物表面局部成核并生长无水II型晶相（anhydrous form II），并在共同平面上保持相似的分子取向。

Conclusion: 该工作直接提供了水合物脱水的局部晶体学见解，表明表面控制的质量损失、形态变化和晶格取向共同主导分子水合物的固态相变。同时，验证了低剂量扫描电子衍射（low-dose SED）是探测光束敏感分子晶体中动态相变的有效方法。

Abstract: Solid-state phase transformations in molecular crystal hydrates govern stability and functional performance across a range of applications, including pharmaceutical, agrochemical and coordination framework materials. During dehydration, these hydrates can undergo substantial structural reorganisation involving changes in molecular orientation, intermolecular interactions, and lattice symmetry. Despite extensive study, the microscopic crystallographic pathways by which such transformations proceed remain poorly understood. Here, we investigate the dynamics of solid-state dehydration of theophylline monohydrate as a model molecular hydrate using in situ low-dose scanning electron diffraction (SED). Simultaneous observations of changes in morphology and crystallographic phase and orientation mapped across single particles reveal how complete dehydration proceeds via a two-step, reconstructive topotactic solid-state transformation: anisotropic, surface-specific mass loss of material near water channel sides (suggesting the monohydrate adopts a non-centrosymmetric crystal structure) is followed by surface-localised nucleation and growth of anhydrous form II on the parent monohydrate while preserving similar molecular orientations at a common plane. By providing direct, local crystallographic insight into hydrate dehydration, this work demonstrates how surface-controlled mass loss, morphological changes, and lattice orientation jointly govern solid-state transformations in molecular hydrates. More broadly, it establishes low-dose SED as an effective approach for probing dynamic phase transformations in beam-sensitive molecular crystals.

### [51] [Multilayer Screening of Double and Conventional Perovskite Solar Cells Using SCAPS-1D and Machine Learning: Optimization of ETL, HTL, and Absorber for High-Efficiency Architectures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12083)
*Neda Nasiri,Seyed Mahdi Mastoor,Amirhosein Ahmadkhan Kordbacheh*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过整合SCAPS-1D器件模拟与机器学习，系统探索了由五种电子传输层、五种吸收层（含无铅双钙钛矿）和五种空穴传输层构建的125种钙钛矿太阳能电池器件架构。仅用代表性子集训练机器学习模型即可预测其余未探索结构的功率转换效率，SHAP分析揭示空穴传输层带隙、吸收层带隙和电子传输层电子亲和力为最关键描述符。模型识别的高性能结构经完整SCAPS-1D验证，其中FTO/TiO₂/Cs₂AgBiBr₆/NiO/Ag器件达到28.85%的PCE，ML建议结构FTO/SnO₂/Cs₂AgInBr₆/NiO/Ag表现28.62%，且前11种结构中有8种使用无铅双钙钛矿Cs₂AgInBr₆。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多层钙钛矿太阳能电池（perovskite solar cells）的组合设计空间极其庞大，对所有可能的材料组合进行穷举式实验或计算筛选仍然不切实际，亟需一种高效的方法加速高性价比、环境友好型器件构型的发现。

Method: 将SCAPS-1D器件模拟与机器学习（machine learning, ML）集成，从五种电子传输层（ETL）、五种吸收层（含无铅双钙钛矿）和五种空穴传输层（HTL）构建共125种器件架构，用代表性子集训练ML模型预测其余未探索结构的功率转换效率（power conversion efficiency, PCE），并利用SHAP（SHapley Additive exPlanations）分析进行特征重要性解释。

Result: 留一组群交叉验证（Leave-One-Group-Out cross-validation）获得Spearman秩相关系数，证明模型具备可靠的排序能力；SHAP分析表明HTL带隙、吸收层带隙和ETL电子亲和力为最影响性能的描述符。ML识别的FTO/TiO₂/Cs₂AgBiBr₆/NiO/Ag器件PCE达28.85%，ML建议的FTO/SnO₂/Cs₂AgInBr₆/NiO/Ag结构达28.62%，较相近文献架构提升约4个百分点（绝对值）；前11种结构中有8种采用无铅双钙钛矿Cs₂AgInBr₆。

Conclusion: 基于物理的数据驱动工作流——结合SCAPS-1D、机器学习与SHAP——能够加速发现高效率、环境友好的钙钛矿太阳能电池，同时提供透明的设计规则，且该方法可推广至其他多层光电器件系统。

Abstract: The combinatorial design space of multilayer perovskite solar cells is vast, yet exhaustive experimental or computational screening of all possible material combinations remains impractical. Here, we integrate SCAPS-1D device simulations with machine learning to systematically explore 125 device architectures constructed from five electron transport layers (ETL), five absorbers (including lead-free double perovskites), and five hole transport layers (HTL). A representative subset of configurations is used to train a machine learning (ML) model, which predicts the power conversion efficiency (PCE) of the remaining unexplored structures. Leave-One-Group-Out cross-validation yields a Spearman rank correlation, demonstrating reliable ranking capability. SHAP (SHapley Additive exPlanations) analysis reveals that the HTL band gap, absorber band gap, and ETL electron affinity are the most influential descriptors, providing physical insights into interfacial recombination and charge extraction. The machine learning model identifies several high-performance configurations that are subsequently verified by full SCAPS-1D simulations. Among them, the device FTO/TiO$_2$/Cs$_2$AgBiBr$_6$/NiO/Ag achieves a PCE of 28.85%, and the ML-suggested structure FTO/SnO$_2$/Cs$_2$AgInBr$_6$/NiO/Ag exhibits 28.62%, outperforming a closely related literature architecture by approximately 4% absolute. Notably, eight of the top-11 structures employ the lead-free double perovskite Cs$_2$AgInBr$_6$. This work demonstrates that a physics-based, data-driven workflow combining SCAPS-1D, ML, and SHAP can accelerate the discovery of high-efficiency, environmentally friendly perovskite solar cells while providing transparent design rules. The approach is generalizable to other multilayer optoelectronic systems.

</details>

Abstract: Melting and solidification of eutectic systems is a classical topic in physical metallurgy, yet the mechanisms at nanoscale are less investigated, due to experimental limitations in spatiotemporal resolution. Abstract: The interdiffusion of immiscible elements is generally considered both thermodynamically unfavorable and kinetically hindered. At the nanoscale, however, the mixing behavior of multielements materials often diverges from bulk equilibrium, yet a quantitative, atomically resolved description of this transformation has remained challenging. Using ex situ four dimensional atomic resolution electron tomography combined with in situ scanning transmission electron microscopy, here we reveal the atomic scale miscible transition driven by interdiffusion in immiscible PdIr nanoparticles at temperatures far below the melting point. The pathway involves surface reconstruction atom hopping at 200oC and surface flattening at 300oC, followed by a critical transition at 400oC where Ir interfacial diffusion and discrete Ir intermediates drive miscible intermixing. Upon reaching the nanoscale melting point 900oC, collective inward Ir diffusion yields the thermodynamically stable IrPd configuration. Our findings provide quantitative atomic scale insights into how metastable nanostructures evolve through distinct intermediates, offering a design framework for advanced multielement materials.

### [56] [Quantum dynamic simulation of triplet formation in an effective model of Y6 (BTP-4F)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12221)
*Isabel Creed,Lucy J. F. Hart,Pranay Venkatesh,Tom Ward,Jarvist Moore Frost*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 基于五态模型求解Y6二聚体的非绝热动力学，发现三重态主要通过分子间电荷转移单重态→三重态Frenkel激子路径生成；硒化可增强自旋-轨道耦合加速该路径；Marcus理论长时产率不准，而记忆核投影方法能从HEOM方程导出半经典速率，得到定量正确的动力学与产率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究对Y6光激发后的三重态布居机制尚不清晰，特别是单体和聚集体间动力学差异以及跃迁路径的性质有待阐明。

Method: 构建Y6二聚体的五态模型，采用分层运动方程（Hierarchical Equations of Motion, HEOM）求解非绝热动力学；通过单粒子跃迁密度矩阵分析电荷转移态与Frenkel激子态的空间分布差异；并引入记忆核投影方法（memory-kernel projector method）从HEOM方程推导半经典速率。

Result: 三重态主要通过瞬态激发的分子间电荷转移单重态→三重态Frenkel激子路径布居，该路径在单体中不存在；电荷转移态与Frenkel激子态空间上分离，因此该跃迁的大自旋-轨道耦合来源于轨道特征变化；硒化增强自旋-轨道耦合后加速了该路径；Marcus理论定性正确但长时产率有误，而记忆核投影方法可得到定量正确的动力学和产率。

Conclusion: Y6的聚集直接促进了快速、高产率的系间窜越（intersystem crossing）；电荷转移介导的路径是三重态生成的关键；记忆核投影方法是模拟更大聚集体动力学的有效工具。

Abstract: We construct a five-state model for photoexcitation in Y6 (BTP-4F) dimers, and then solve the non-adiabtic dynamics using the Hierarchical Equations of Motion (HEOM) method. We find that triplets are populated mainly via a transiently excited \textit{intermolecular} charge-transfer singlet to triplet Frenkel exciton route; this route is not available to the monomer. Analysis of one-particle transition density matrices suggests that the charge-transfer states are spatially distinct to the Frenkel exciton states, indicating that the large spin-orbit-coupling for this transition is due to it being permitted by an associated change in orbital character.
  Aggregation in Y6 therefore directly enables fast and high-yield intersystem crossing. We selenise our model dimers, significantly enhancing spin-orbit-coupling, which then accelerates this charge-transfer mediated route. Looking forwards to simulations on larger aggregates, we show that, though Marcus theory gives qualitatively correct dynamics, the long-time yields are incorrect due to it missing quantum recurrences. Instead, we show that the recently developed memory-kernel projector\cite{Gestsson2025-ez} method can produce semi-classical rates directly from the HEOM equations which lead to quantitatively correct dynamics and yields.

### [58] [Plasmonic properties and correlation energies from a compact multipole representation of the dielectric response in 2D metals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12274)

Method: 将多极-帕德近似推广至二维金属的整个布里渊区，构造一种保持对称性、各向异性的逆介电函数（inverse dielectric function）解析形式。对七种分属不同电子区间的二维金属构建紧凑表示，验证少量色散等离激元模式（dispersive plasmonic modes）的表示能力。

Conclusion: 所提出的表示法在第一性原理（ab initio）计算与分析屏蔽模型之间建立了直接桥梁，为凝聚态系统的应用开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Multipole-Padé approximants provide a compact representation of dynamical response functions in terms of a small number of collective modes. Here, we generalize this framework to incorporate momentum dependence across the full Brillouin zone of 2D metals by constructing a symmetry-conserving, anisotropic representation of the inverse dielectric function. This analytic form enables efficient and accurate evaluation of quantities involving dynamical screening, including spectral features and correlation energies. We construct such compact representations for a set of seven two dimensional metals spanning distinct electronic regimes, and show that a small number of dispersive plasmonic modes suffices to accurately describe the dielectric response across the full Brillouin zone, while also yielding accurate correlation energies. The proposed representation therefore establishes a direct bridge between {\it ab initio} calculations and analytical models of screening, opening new avenues for applications in condensed matter systems.

### [59] [Effect of polar distortions on the anomalous Hall conductivity of altermagnetic $α$-MnTe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12311)
*Mathews Benny,Sahar Izadi Vishkayi,Amar Fakhredine,Chanchal K. Barman,Carmine Autieri*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文研究了反铁磁α-MnTe表面因晶体对称性破缺与奈尔矢量取向共同作用导致的对称性降低（从六方P6₃/mmc到正交Amm2），进而产生沿z轴和y轴的极性畸变及弱铁磁性，并探讨了内禀反常霍尔效应与晶格极化在外电场下的相互影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索交替磁体（altermagnet）α-MnTe在表面处因晶体对称性破缺与奈尔矢量（Néel vector）取向的相互作用所产生的丰富输运现象，特别是反常霍尔电导率（anomalous Hall conductivity, AHC）与晶格极化（lattice polarization）之间的耦合机制。

Method: 通过分析α-MnTe体相和表面的对称性，将表面问题简化为在体相中施加面内电场，并研究掺杂离子半导体中内禀反常霍尔效应与晶格极化的相互作用。

Result: 表面处空间群从六方P6₃/mmc降至正交Amm2，导致沿z轴的极性畸变以及沿y轴的极性畸变和弱铁磁性（weak ferrimagnetism）；晶格极化效应可显著影响反常霍尔电导率。

Conclusion: α-MnTe表面展现出多重极性畸变和弱铁磁性，且晶格极化与内禀反常霍尔效应共存，叠加了非线性反常霍尔效应（non-linear anomalous Hall effect），揭示了交替磁体中丰富的输运现象学。

Abstract: Altermagnetic $α$-MnTe with Néel vector along the $y$-axis exhibits a finite anomalous Hall conductivity (AHC) and weak ferromagnetism along the $z$-axis. As already demonstrated in the bulk, there is the breaking of the C$_6$ symmetry by the in-plane Néel vector, leaving a C$_2$-type magnetic symmetry. The surface of $α$-MnTe breaks the C$_2$, leaving only a time-reversed mirror symmetry with respect to the $x=0$ plane. Therefore, we demonstrate that on the surface, the interplay between breaking of the crystal symmetry and Néel vector orientation produces a reduction of the space group from hexagonal P6$_3$/mmc to orthorhombic Amm2. As a result, the surface exhibits not only a polar distortion along the $z$-axis, but also a polar distortion and a weak ferrimagnetism along the $y$-axis. To describe the surface of MnTe in an accessible way, we simplify the problem and examine the effect of the in-plane electric field in bulk MnTe. Moreover, as a doped ionic semiconductor, the properties of MnTe can be influenced by lattice polarization under an applied electric field. We investigate the interplay between the intrinsic anomalous Hall effect and lattice polarization, showing that polarization effects can substantially affect the AHC. Since the electric field breaks inversion symmetry, this contribution from the lattice polarization coexists with the non-linear anomalous Hall effect, highlighting the rich transport phenomenology of altermagnets.

</details>

### [60] [Kohn-Sham models for encapsulated two-dimensional materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11785)
*Éric Cancès,David Gontier,Solal Perrin-Roussel*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了放置在两个平行导电电极之间的二维材料（如石墨烯、扭曲双层石墨烯等摩尔超晶格材料）的Kohn-Sham密度泛函理论（DFT）模型。证明在该几何构型下，电极施加的狄利克雷边界条件使库仑相互作用变为短程的汤川（Yukawa）型，并证明了对于周期性和准周期性材料，非线性Kohn-Sham DFT模型是适定的（well-posed）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维材料在实际器件中常被置于三维环境（如两个导电电极之间），但现有DFT理论对该几何构型下电子结构模型的数学适定性（well-posedness）缺乏严格分析。

Method: 从数学分析角度，研究电极处狄利克雷边界条件（Dirichlet boundary conditions）对库仑相互作用的屏蔽效应，将长程相互作用约化为短程汤川势（Yukawa potential），并利用非线性泛函分析工具证明Kohn-Sham DFT模型的适定性。

Result: 证明了在电极屏蔽的三维环境中，非线性Kohn-Sham DFT模型对周期性二维材料（如石墨烯）和准周期性二维材料（如扭曲双层石墨烯及其他摩尔超晶格材料在不可公度转角下）均是适定的。

Conclusion: 该工作为二维材料在导电电极间电子结构的第一性原理模拟提供了严格的数学基础，特别适用于摩尔超晶格（moiré materials）等准周期体系的理论研究。

Abstract: We study Kohn-Sham Density Functional Theory (DFT) models describing the electronic structure of two-dimensional materials placed in a three-dimensional environment, encapsulated between two parallel conducting electrodes. In this geometry, the Dirichlet boundary conditions at the electrodes screen the Coulomb interaction, which becomes effectively short-ranged, of Yukawa type. We prove that some nonlinear Kohn-Sham DFT models are well-posed in this setting, both for periodic materials (such as graphene) and for quasi-periodic materials (such as twisted bilayer graphene and other moiré materials for generic incommensurate twist angles).

### [62] [Numerical simulations of the spread from the mean of the SLE and Multiple SLE dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11254)
*Phillip Kim,Vlad Margarint*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过数值实验研究Schramm-Loewner Evolution（SLE）及其多型变体（Multiple SLE）在固定时刻的动力学扩散行为，发现单SLE在初始点靠近原点时分布呈双峰（bimodal），远离时呈钟形（bell-shaped）；而Multiple SLE在所有情形下均呈钟形分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究SLE曲线在固定时刻的统计扩散特性，特别是动力学相对于平均行为的偏离，旨在为未来的理论研究提供数值预测。

Method: 采用Euler方法数值求解Loewner微分方程，在固定时刻计算|g_t(z) - \overline{g_t(z)}|和Re(g_t(z)) - Re(\overline{g_t(z)})这两个随机变量，用以衡量动力学扩散程度。分别对标准SLE（驱动为布朗运动）和Multiple SLE（驱动为Dyson布朗运动）进行实验，并考察参数κ和β对分布的影响。

Result: 单SLE情况下，初始点靠近原点时分布呈双峰，远离原点时变为钟形；Multiple SLE情况下，所有情形下的分布均为钟形；分布形状随参数κ和β变化。

Conclusion: 给出了SLE和Multiple SLE固定时刻扩散行为的数值预测，揭示了初始位置和参数对分布形态的影响，为后续理论分析提供了参考。

Abstract: The Schramm-Loewner Evolution (SLE) describes a family of fractal curves that arise in the study of the scaling limits of many planar Statistical Physics models. These curves are modeled using the Loewner Differential Equation for the conformal maps $g_t(z)$ with a Brownian motion driver. Using Euler's Method, in the current work we performed numerical experiments to study at a fixed time the quantities $|g_t(z) - \overline{g_t(z)}|$ and $Re(g_t(z)) - Re(\overline{g_t(z)})$, where $Re$ denotes the real part and $\overline{g_t(z)}$ refers to the sample average. These random variables measure the 'spread' of the dynamics from the average behavior at fixed time. One of the scopes of this work is to give numerical predictions for future theoretical investigations on these quantities. When investigating these quantities in the SLE case our experiments predict that the distribution is bimodal when the dynamics started close to the origin, and it can become bell-shaped if the dynamics is started further from the origin. In the second part, we performed experiments for a Multiple SLE model whose driver is Dyson Brownian Motion. Due to singularity in the dynamics of the drivers and the many data points needed, this part is challenging from a computational perspective. In the multiple SLE case, our experiments predict that the distribution is bell-shaped in all cases. In addition, we check the changes in the distributions as we vary the parameter $κ$ in the SLE case and $β$ in the Multiple SLE case.

### [63] [Compressed minimum-purity time evolution for late-time quantum dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11392)
*Moksh Bhateja,Jonas B. Rigo,Markus Schmitt*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出压缩最小纯度时间演化（CoMPuTE）方法，通过最小纯度原理截断局域约化密度矩阵的层次运动方程，在保持微观方程精度的同时提升长时动力学模拟效率。基准测试显示该方法能准确描述一维混合场伊辛模型的能量扩散、适用于纯态出发的非平衡Floquet动力学，但在XXZ链中受非局域守恒量限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 简单初态的幺正时间演化会迅速产生纠缠和复杂关联，限制直接数值模拟；而物理观测量的晚期动力学常呈现流体动力学或动理学理论等有效简化形式。因此需要探索是否可以通过受控地丢弃无关信息，使微观运动方程在长时间尺度上仍保持准确和可处理。

Method: CoMPuTE方法追踪一组自洽的约化局域密度矩阵（reduced local density matrices），并利用最小纯度原理（minimum-purity principle）封闭层次运动方程。

Result: 基准测试表明：(i) 准确描述一维混合场伊辛模型（mixed-field Ising model）中的能量扩散；(ii) 适用于纯态出发的非平衡Floquet动力学（Floquet dynamics）；(iii) 在描述XXZ链Δ=1处的输运时，局域约化密度矩阵近似受限于日益非局域的守恒量。与局域信息时间演化算法（local-information time evolution algorithm）相比，CoMPuTE方法显著提升计算效率。

Conclusion: CoMPuTE方法通过最小纯度原则有效截断局域密度矩阵层次，兼顾长时动力学精度与计算效率，有望推广至高维系统。

Abstract: Unitary time evolution of initially simple quantum many-body states rapidly generates entanglement and complex correlations, which limits direct numerical simulations. The late-time dynamics of physical observables, however, typically exhibits an effective simplicity in the form of hydrodynamics or kinetic theory. This leads to the question whether microscopic equations of motion can remain accurate and tractable up to long time scales by discarding irrelevant information in a controlled manner. Here, we introduce compressed minimum-purity time evolution (CoMPuTE) as an approach to keep track of a consistent set of reduced local density matrices, closing the hierarchical equations of motion using a minimum-purity principle. In benchmark applications we demonstrate (i) accurate description of energy diffusion in the one-dimensional mixed-field Ising model, (ii) the applicability to genuinely out-of-equilibrium Floquet dynamics starting from a pure state, and (iii) the limitations of the local reduced density matrix approximation when describing transport in the XXZ chain at $Δ=1$ that is governed by increasingly non-local integrals of motion. The CoMPuTE method enhances computational efficiency in comparison to the closely related local-information time evolution algorithm, opening a possible route towards an extension to systems in higher spatial dimensions.

</details>


### [64] [A stochastic model for elastoplastic contact of rough surfaces incorporating scale-dependent hardness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11765)
*Yang Xu,Hengxu Song,Jianqiao Hu*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文基于随机过程理论，首次采用复合Chapman-Kolmogorov方程（compounded Chapman-Kolmogorov equations）求解涉及尺度相关硬度的弹塑性接触问题，建立了描述弹性接触压力、塑性接触面积及非接触面积概率密度函数演化的三个积分方程，并推导出一个新的地形屈服参数（topographic yield parameter），为粗糙表面接触分析提供了随机过程框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于随机过程理论（stochastic theory），首次引入复合Chapman-Kolmogorov方程求解涉及尺度相关硬度的弹塑性接触问题。建立了三个积分方程，分别描述弹性接触压力（elastic contact pressure）、相对塑性接触面积（relative plastic contact area）和相对非接触面积（relative non-contact area）的概率密度函数（probability density function, PDF）随几何尺度的演化。

Result: 通过调节不同的力学和材料属性，模型预测了从线性弹性到弹塑性行为再到完全塑性的平滑过渡。推导了一个新的地形屈服参数，该参数整合了更广泛的材料和几何属性，可用于识别接触状态。通过曲线拟合实现了弹性和塑性极限的高精度确定，并提供了用于快速识别接触状态的新图表。

Conclusion: 本研究开创性地将复合Chapman-Kolmogorov方程应用于粗糙表面接触分析的随机过程框架，所建立的描述界面性质随尺度演化的积分方程，可为地震学、电接触（electrical contact）和接触起电（contact electrification）等多尺度粗糙度起关键作用的多学科领域提供有价值的参考。

Abstract: The stress concentrations caused by inherent roughness of natural and manufactured surfaces often induce plastic deformation at contact interfaces, a challenge compounded by competing influences of the size effect of plastic deformation and self-affine rough surface topography. To address this, we developed a novel methodology based on stochastic theory using compounded Chapman-Kolmogorov equations, for the first time, to solve elastoplastic contact problems involving scale-dependent hardness. Our approach formulates three integral equations describing the evolution of probability density functions of elastic contact pressure, relative plastic contact area, and relative non-contact area across geometrical scales. We thoroughly investigate the effects of scale-dependent hardness on contact pressure distribution, relative elastic and plastic contact areas, and the area-to-load relationship. By adjusting various mechanical and material properties, our model predicts a smooth transition from linear elasticity to elastic-plastic behavior and finally to full plasticity. A key advancement is the derivation of a new topographic yield parameter incorporating a wider range of material and geometrical properties, aiding identification of contact status. Numerical solutions enable highly precise determination of elastic and plastic limits via curve-fitting, and we also provide a new diagram for rapid identification of contact status. This study pioneers a stochastic process framework for applying the compounded Chapman-Kolmogorov equation to rough surface contact analysis, and the integral equations characterizing how interfacial properties evolve with scale could offer valuable insights for other multidisciplinary fields where multiscale roughness is critical, such as earthquakes, electrical contact, and contact electrification.

### [65] [Universal Information-Theoretic Structure of the Quasi-Stationary Domany--Kinzel Automaton](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11885)
*Hyun-Yong Lee,Kenji Harada,Naoki Kawashima*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过矩阵乘积态（matrix-product-state）表示概率分布，表征了Domany–Kinzel自动机中键定向逾渗线（bond directed-percolation line）的拟稳态分布（QSD），揭示了从活性相到非活性相转变中生存簇的空间结构与信息论特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于矩或采样的方法无法获取拟稳态分布（QSD）的完整条件分布，从而限制了信息论诊断的应用。本文旨在利用矩阵乘积态表示绕过这一局限，深入理解吸收态系统中QSD的空间结构及其信息论特征。

Method: 通过投影出吸收态并迭代转移矩阵，获得概率分布的矩阵乘积态（matrix-product-state）表示，从而直接计算拟稳态分布（QSD）的完整条件分布及信息论诊断量，如二分互信息（bipartite mutual information）。

Result: 活性相中QSD具有类体相（bulk-like）的有限密度结构；非活性相中幸存活动坍缩为占据链上极小比例的单一群组（single flock），其内部填充从深非活性相的单个团簇（single cluster）到近临界点的松散部分填充组不等。非活性相中，二分互信息等于单个二元选择（该群组位于切割左侧还是右侧）的熵，即幸存簇编码仅1比特位置信息，等价于单个有效簇（single effective cluster）。

Conclusion: 本文成功将矩阵乘积态技术拓展至定义拟稳态分布（QSD）的投影本征向量，为吸收态系统提供了体观测量（bulk-observable）方法无法触及的信息论诊断工具。

Abstract: We characterize the quasi-stationary distribution (QSD) of the bond directed-percolation line of the Domany--Kinzel automaton using a matrix-product-state representation of the probability distribution, obtained by projecting out the absorbing state and iterating the transfer matrix. Unlike moment- or sampling-based methods, this yields the full conditional distribution and direct access to information-theoretic diagnostics. The spatial structure of the QSD changes sharply across the transition: the active phase is bulk-like with finite density, whereas in the inactive phase the surviving activity collapses into a single flock occupying a vanishing fraction of the chain, with an internal filling that ranges from a single cluster deep in the inactive phase to a loose, partially filled group near criticality. This picture carries a sharp information-theoretic signature: throughout the inactive phase the bipartite mutual information of the QSD equals the entropy of a single binary choice -- whether the flock lies to the left or right of the cut -- so the surviving clusters together encode just one bit of positional information, corresponding to a single effective cluster. The approach extends matrix-product-state techniques to the projected eigenvector defining a QSD, opening information-theoretic diagnostics for absorbing-state systems that bulk-observable methods cannot reach.

### [66] [Estimation of conserved charges for a one dimensional system with inhomogeneous hopping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11991)
*Triparna Mondal*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文基于可积矩阵理论（integrable matrix theory）提出一个统一框架，用于在一维有限尺寸晶格上的单粒子非均匀最近邻跳跃系统中提取守恒荷（conserved charges）。通过研究系统从混沌到可积（chaotic–integrable crossover）的统计性质，发现守恒荷的数量在可积极限下接近系统尺寸，表明该数量可作为量子可积性（quantum integrability）的度量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子可积性（quantum integrability）的特征在于系统拥有大量守恒荷（conserved charges），但在一般量子系统中寻找这些守恒荷极具挑战性。本文旨在利用可积矩阵理论（integrable matrix theory）为特定类别的系统提供一个统一框架来获取守恒荷，并探索守恒荷数量是否可作为量子可积性的度量。

Method: 将可积矩阵理论应用于一维有限尺寸晶格上的单粒子系统，该系统具有非均匀最近邻跳跃（inhomogeneous nearest neighbor hopping）。首先研究随机矩阵模型的本征能谱（eigenspectrum），然后估计守恒荷并分析其在系统从混沌到可积（chaotic–integrable crossover）转变过程中的性质。

Result: 在系统从混沌到可积的交叉过程中，计算了守恒荷（conserved charges）的数量，发现在可积极限（integrable limit）下该数量几乎等于系统尺寸。

Conclusion: 结果表明，利用可积矩阵理论（integrable matrix theory）估计的守恒荷数量可以作为量子可积性（quantum integrability）的一种度量指标。

Abstract: Quantum integrability in a system is characterized by a large number of conserved charges. However, finding the conserved charges in a generic quantum system is highly challenging. The integrable matrix theory provides a unified framework to obtain the conserved charges in a certain class of systems. We demonstrate this framework in case of a single-particle system on a 1D finite-sized lattice with inhomogeneous nearest neighbor hopping to study the statistical properties of the system across its chaotic--integrable crossover from the perspective of the conserved charges. The eigenspectrum of our random matrix model is studied first. We then estimate the conserved charges and find their properties throughout the chaotic to integrable transition of the system. We calculate the number of conserved charges across this crossover and observe that it is nearly equal to the size of the system at its integrable limit. Our result suggests that the number of conserved charges, estimated using the integrable matrix theory, can be a measure of quantum integrability.

### [67] [Path convergence in diffusion models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12161)
*Roi Holtzman,Roman Beauvallet,Werner Krauth*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究扩散模型（diffusion model）中连接目标分布与参考分布的插值路径，分析了有限模式数 p 下路径向无穷模式情形的收敛行为（1/√p 尺度），并提出外推（extrapolation）算法用于密度估计（density estimation）与泛化（generalization）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨仅通过 p 个模式（patterns）已知的目标分布与可采样的参考分布之间的扩散模型路径，旨在理解有限样本下路径的收敛性质并实现路径外推。

Method: 采用对称或前向（加噪，noising）/后向（去噪，denoising）方式构造插值路径；在同质扩散噪声下分析路径随模式数 p 向无穷模式路径的收敛性；在一维测试案例中证明收敛尺度为 1/√p 但均方偏差（mean square deviation）无穷大；提出基于路径收敛的外推算法作为密度估计与泛化策略。

Result: 在一维测试案例中，路径收敛尺度为 1/√p，但均方偏差发散至无穷；路径收敛性可实现向 p=∞ 路径的外推，从而采样目标分布。

Conclusion: 路径收敛与外推可作为密度估计与泛化的可行策略；提供了所有算法的伪代码及 Python 实现。

Abstract: We discuss diffusion-model paths interpolating between a target distribution known only through p patterns and a reference distribution that can be sampled. These interpolating paths can be constructed symmetrically or else in forward direction (often referred to as a "noising") from the target patterns to the reference distribution or in backward direction (as a "denoising") from the reference distribution to the patterns. For backward paths with identical diffusion noise, we consider the path convergence in number of patterns p towards the path for infinitely many patterns. In a one-dimensional test case, we show that this convergence is on a scale 1/sqrt(p), but with infinite mean square deviation. We demonstrate that the path convergence allows for extrapolation towards the p=infinity path which samples the target distribution. We provide a proof-of-concept extrapolation algorithm and propose the convergence and extrapolation of paths as a possible strategy for density estimation and generalization. We illustrate all our algorithms through pseudo-codes and provide Python implementations.

</details>


### [68] [Mass generation at a fixed point: A Functional Renormalization Group Study of the tricritical O($N$) model in $d=3$ and $N=\infty$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12269)
*Shunsuke Yabunaka,bertrand Delamotte*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过功能重整化群（functional renormalization group）重新审视Bardeen–Moshe–Bander（BMB）固定点线，发现在三维大N极限下的三临界O(N)模型中，重整化群固定点（RG fixed point）可能不伴随标度不变性（scale invariance）和发散相关长度（divergent correlation length），并揭示了质量生成的非普适性及其与非解析有效势的关系，同时给出了临界指数ν在BMB线不同区域间的跳跃行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为重整化群固定点必然与标度不变性和发散相关长度相关联。本文旨在检验这一联系在三维大N极限下三临界O(N)模型中的有效性，并澄清BMB固定点线上质量生成的机制。

Method: 采用功能重整化群（functional renormalization group）方法，重新分析Bardeen、Moshe与Bander此前识别出的固定点线，研究其有效势的非解析结构及重整化流（renormalization flow）的动态演化。

Result: BMB固定点线分为正则部分（0 ≤ λ < λ_BMB）与奇异部分（λ = λ_BMB）。在正则部分，临界指数ν = 1/2；在奇异部分（BMB固定点），ν = 1/3。质量生成是非普适的（nonuniversal），源于有效势的非解析结构。奇异势在重整化流中动态涌现。

Conclusion: RG固定点与标度不变性及发散相关长度之间不一定存在必然联系；BMB固定点提供了一个反例，其中质量生成机制通过非解析有效势实现，且临界指数在固定点处发生跳跃。

Abstract: Renormalization group (RG) fixed points are commonly associated with scale invariance and a divergent correlation length. We show that this connection can fail in the tricritical $O(N)$ model in three dimensions in the limit $N\to\infty$. Revisiting the line of fixed points identified by Bardeen, Moshe, and Bander, we use the functional renormalization group to clarify the mechanism leading to mass generation at its singular endpoint (the BMB fixed point). We demonstrate that the generated mass is nonuniversal and originates from the nonanalytic structure of the effective potential. We show that the critical exponent $ν$ which takes the value $ν= 1/2$ along the regular part of the BMB line, that is, for $0 \leq λ< λ_{\rm BMB}$, jumps to $ν= 1/3$ on the singular part of this line with the BMB FP, corresponding to $λ= λ_{\rm BMB}$, being the pivotal point between these two regimes. We also show how its singular potential emerges dynamically along the renormalization flow.

</details>

### [69] [TAMBO: A Novel Neutrino Telescope for High-Energy Astrophysical Neutrino Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11230)
*P. Zhelnin,J. Dacpano,C. Argüelles*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: TAMBO（Tau Air-shower Mountain-Based Observatory）是一种新型中微子望远镜，利用其独特的深谷几何结构（deep valley geometry）在1–1000 PeV能量范围内实现卓越的信噪比（signal-to-background）区分，有望大幅推进高能中微子点源与弥散辐射的探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 天体物理中微子点源（neutrino point sources）的探测仍面临大气本底（atmospheric backgrounds）的干扰以及“look-elsewhere效应”（look-elsewhere effect）带来的统计惩罚，亟需具有更高信号-本底鉴别能力的观测装置。

Method: TAMBO基于其独特的深谷几何结构（deep valley geometry），在1–1000 PeV能量范围实现前所未有的信噪比（signal-to-background）鉴别，从而生成极纯净的中微子样本。

Result: 初步灵敏度研究（preliminary sensitivity studies）表明，TAMBO具备绘制弥散中微子发射（diffuse neutrino emissions）和点源中微子发射（point-source neutrino emissions）的能力。

Conclusion: TAMBO代表了高能中微子天文学（high-energy neutrino astronomy）的一项重要进展，有望显著提升对中微子源的精确认知。

Abstract: The detection of astrophysical neutrino point sources remains challenging due to atmospheric backgrounds obscuring signal and statistical penalties from the look-elsewhere effect. The Tau Air-shower Mountain-Based Observatory (TAMBO) is a neutrino telescope that achieves unprecedented signal-to-background discrimination in the 1-1000 PeV energy range. Leveraging its unique deep valley geometry, TAMBO will generate an exceptionally pure neutrino sample, enabling precise investigations of neutrino sources. Preliminary sensitivity studies demonstrate TAMBO's potential to map diffuse and point-source neutrino emissions, representing a significant advancement in high-energy neutrino astronomy.

### [70] [Intermediate States in Chaotic Triple Evolution and Applications to Black Hole Merger Statistics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11294)
*Dina Meylakh,Nicholas C. Stone,Nathan W. C. Leigh*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该论文利用平衡统计力学（equilibrium statistical mechanics）重新推导了三体系统中椭圆轨道结局的分布，并与双曲轨道分布结合，构建了蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）算法以模拟稠密星团中的重复二元-单星散射事件。研究发现椭圆轨道合并中可观测到偏心引力波（observably eccentric merger, OEM）的比例约为32-63%，而OEM占全部合并事件的比例在2.6-4.4%之间，并随探测灵敏度阈值变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三体相互作用是强混沌演化与层次运动的结合：在混沌阶段后，系统可能形成包含一颗逃逸星和一对双星的层次结构，进而产生引力波（gravitational wave, GW）旋近事件。然而，混沌状态的最终结局决定了此类引力波事件能否实际发生，因此需要准确建模三体相互作用的结局分布，以评估稠密星团中偏心引力波事件的观测前景。

Method: 本文采用平衡统计力学重新推导椭圆轨道结局的分布，并整合已有的双曲轨道分布；将理论分布与N体模拟（N-body simulations）对比，将椭圆结局模型从两个自由参数简化为一个自由参数。在此基础上，结合星团模型设计了一个蒙特卡洛算法，用于模拟稠密星团中重复的二元-单星散射过程。

Result: 理论预测的解离概率（disintegration probabilities）与N体模拟结果总体吻合，仅在极低角动量三体系统中存在偏差。在星团质量为[10⁵-10⁷] M⊙的模拟中，椭圆轨道合并产生的OEM约占椭圆合并总数的32–63%。假设探测灵敏度阈值为 f_min=10 Hz、e_min=0.1，OEM占全部合并事件的比例为2.6–4.4%；以LIGO-Virgo当前灵敏度（f_min ≈ 34.4 Hz）计算，该比例降至1.6–3.1%。星团总质量对逃逸双星的占比有显著影响。

Conclusion: 将平衡统计力学应用于三体混沌结局的建模可有效简化椭圆轨道分布模型，并准确描述稠密星团中二元-单星散射的宏观统计行为。基于该模型预测的OEM事件占比表明，LIGO和Virgo等探测器在当前灵敏度下有望观测到一定份额的可观测偏心引力波事件，且星团质量是影响OEM率的重要因素。

Abstract: Three-body interactions exhibit phases of strong chaotic evolution as well as hierarchical motion where one body separates from a binary and follows a hyperbolic or elliptic trajectory around it. The binaries produced during phases of hierarchical motion may lead to gravitational wave (GW) inspirals, but this depends on the outcomes of the chaotic states. In this paper we re-derive the elliptic outcome distribution using equilibrium statistical mechanics and explore it together with the hyperbolic distribution. When comparing to N-body simulations, we find that we can reduce the elliptic outcome model to one free parameter instead of the previously used two and that the predicted disintegration probabilities agree except for very low angular momentum triples. We then use both outcome distributions along with a star cluster model to design a Monte Carlo algorithm for repeated binary-single scatterings within dense star systems. We explore star cluster masses of $[10^5 - 10^7] M_{\odot}$, with the goal of quantifying observably eccentric merger (OEM) GWs, visible to instruments such as LIGO and Virgo. Assuming an OEM detection sensitivity of $f_{\rm min}=10 {\rm Hz}, e_{\rm min} = 0.1$, we find the elliptic OEMs are about $\sim (32 - 63)\%$ of the total elliptic mergers and that the total cluster mass greatly impacts the fraction of ejected binaries. The OEM to total merger fraction (OEM fraction) is found to be $(2.6 - 4.4)\%$. Considering the detection sensitivity that GW interferometers have today $(f_{\rm min} \simeq 34.4 {\rm Hz})$ we obtain the OEM fraction in the $(1.6 - 3.1)\%$ range.

</details>


### [71] [A magnetar formation in binary neutron star merger](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11299)
*Kenta Kiuchi,Alexis Reboul-Salze,Yuichiro Sekiguchi,Masaru Shibata*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文使用日本超算富岳（FUGAKU）对双中子星并合（binary neutron star merger）进行了全球广义相对论中微子辐射传输磁流体动力学（general relativistic neutrino-radiation-transfer magnetohydrodynamics）模拟，空间分辨率达到创纪录的6.25米。模拟表明，并合后约3毫秒内，Kelvin-Helmholtz不稳定性可将磁场放大至电磁饱和能量约$10^{50}$ erg，并至少在短期内形成磁星（magnetar）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双中子星并合过程中的磁场放大机制及其对磁星形成的意义尚未被高分辨率数值模拟充分探索。

Method: 基于日本超算FUGAKU，采用全球广义相对论中微子辐射传输磁流体动力学（GR neutrino-radiation-transfer MHD）模拟，空间分辨率6.25米，最大初始磁场$3.16\times 10^{12}$ G，总CPU耗时约5.3亿核小时。

Result: Kelvin-Helmholtz不稳定性在并合后3毫秒内将磁场放大至电磁饱和能量$\sim 10^{50}$ erg；磁能功率谱密度（power spectral density）重现Kazantsev谱，动能功率谱密度重现Kolmogorov谱；磁场在恒星尺度上至少放大316倍。

Conclusion: 双中子星并合后数毫秒内可能至少暂时形成磁星。

Abstract: We conduct a global general relativistic neutrino-radiation-transfer magnetohydrodynamics simulation of a $1.35$-$1.35M_\odot$ binary neutron star with the unprecedented spatial resolution of $6.25$\,m on the Japanese supercomputer FUGAKU. The total consumed CPU time is $\approx 530$ million core hours. We initialize the binary neutron star's magnetic field to be $3.16\times 10^{12}$~G at maximum, which is compatible with the upper end of the observed binary pulsars. We demonstrate that the Kelvin-Helmholtz instability that emerges when the two neutron stars touch amplifies the magnetic field to an expected electromagnetic saturation energy of $\sim 10^{50}$~erg within $3$~ms after the merger. The spectral analysis indicates that the Kazantsev and Kolmogorov spectra are reproduced in the magnetic and kinetic power spectral densities, respectively. We also find that it induces stellar-scale magnetic field amplification by at least a factor of $316$. We conclude that a magnetar may form at least temporarily following neutron star mergers in a few ms.

</details>


### [72] [Emergent gravity from Michel flow with position dependent adiabatic index](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11964)
*Apashanka Das,Souvik Ghose,Tapas K. Das*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文对 Michel 流（Michel flow）——即球对称广义相对论 Bondi 吸积——进行了多维度分析：构建了绝热指数随径向距离变化的多元组分吸积的稳态跨声速解，利用动力系统理论（dynamical systems theory）分类了跨声速点（transonic points）的性质，并通过线性径向扰动验证了稳态解的稳定性，进而提取了嵌入吸积物质中的声学时空中对应的声学黑洞视界（acoustic black hole horizon）和因果结构（causal structure）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将球对称广义相对论 Bondi 吸积（即 Michel 流）的研究从简单的稳态解推广到包含变绝热指数（adiabatic index）的多元组分情形，并从动力系统、稳定性和经典类比引力（analogue gravity）等多个视角对该吸积系统进行统一刻画。

Method: 构建了绝热指数随径向距离变化的物态方程（equation of state）下的稳态积分跨声速解；在由径向距离和马赫数（Mach number）张成的相空间中绘制相图（phase portrait）；借用动力系统理论分类跨声速点的性质；对稳态流施加线性径向扰动以分析稳定性；基于稳定性结果提取声学时空中对应的度规，并通过 Carter-Penrose 图（Carter-Penrose diagrams）构建因果结构来识别视界（horizon）。

Result: 得到了变绝热指数情形的多组分吸积的稳态跨声速解及对应的相图；成功分类了跨声速点的类型；发现该流动在线性径向扰动下是稳定的；从稳定流动中提取了声学度规，并通过 Carter-Penrose 图确认了该声学时空中视界的存在。

Conclusion: 该工作从天体物理学（astrophysical aspects）、动力系统理论以及经典类比引力现象三个角度，系统性地研究了广义相对论框架下的黑洞吸积系统，揭示了该类吸积流在稳态、稳定性和声学视界结构方面的完整图景。

Abstract: Spherically symmetric, general relativistic Bondi accretion is known as the Michel flow. The stationary integral transonic solutions for the Michel flow has been constructed for multi-component accretion described by an equation of state where the adiabatic index varies with the radial distance along which the streamlines are studied, and the corresponding phase portrait spanned by such radial distance and the flow Mach number has been obtained. Borrowing the techniques used in the dynamical systems theory, the nature of the transonic points of the aforementioned flow has been classified. The steady state flow has been perturbed to study the stability of the stationary solutions, and it has been found that such flows are stable under the (linear) radial perturbation. As a consequence of the stability analysis, the corresponding acoustic space time embedded within the accreting matter has been obtained, and the horizon of the metric of such sonic space time has been identified by constructing the causal structure with the help of the Carter-Penrose diagrams. In this way, the accreting black hole systems in the general relativistic set up has been investigated from various different perspectives - from its astrophysical aspects, from the dynamical systems point of view, as well as within the realm of the classical analogue gravity phenomena.

</details>


### [73] [Broadened Lensing Rings of Compact Boson Stars: Enhanced Imprint of Accretion Flow in Images and Visibilities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12092)
*Xiangyu Wang,Xinyu Wang,Minyong Guo,Hai-Qing Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了致密玻色子星（compact boson stars）的引力透镜效应（gravitational lensing）和观测特征，发现与黑洞不同，其光子有效势（photon effective potential）具有近乎平坦的区域，导致大角度偏转的碰撞参数范围更宽，透镜环更宽，并且成像对吸积流（accretion flow）空间分布的敏感性更强，凸显了致密玻色子星与黑洞在观测性质上的定性差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞与致密玻色子星等致密天体在强引力区域的光学表现存在潜在差异，系统研究致密玻色子星的引力透镜性质和观测特征，有助于在观测上区分这两种天体。

Method: 首先从光子有效势（photon effective potential）的角度分析碰撞参数（impact parameter）范围与偏转角的关系，然后运用光线追踪（ray tracing）技术模拟成像，并将其与黑洞模型的图像拓扑（image topology）和可视度振幅（visibility amplitudes）进行比较。

Result: 致密玻色子星的光子有效势存在一个近乎平坦的区域，其宽度随致密度的增加而增大；该平坦结构显著拓宽了产生大角度偏转的碰撞参数范围，使得各阶透镜环均明显更宽；构成这些环的光子路径更复杂，图像对吸积流空间分布的敏感性高于黑洞模型。

Conclusion: 致密玻色子星与黑洞在引力透镜成像和观测特征上存在定性差异，尤其是对吸积流结构的依赖程度不同，这为未来通过高分辨率观测区分两类天体提供了理论基础。

Abstract: In this work, we systematically study the gravitational lensing properties and observational signatures of compact boson stars. Unlike black holes, the photon effective potential of a compact boson star develops a nearly flat region, whose width increases with the compactness of the star. This flat structure significantly broadens the range of impact parameters that can produce large-angle deflections, leading to noticeably wider lensing rings of all orders. Photons constituting these rings traverse more complex paths, rendering the resulting images more sensitive to the spatial distribution of the accretion flow. Ray tracing results show that, compared to black hole models, the image topology and visibility amplitudes of compact boson stars exhibit a stronger dependence on the accretion flow structure. These results highlight qualitative differences in the observational properties of compact boson stars and black holes.

</details>


### [74] [Evidence for additional structure in the effective spin distribution hints at multiple formation pathways in GWTC-5.0](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12205)
*Sofia Alvarez-Lopez,Jack Heinzel,Salvatore Vitale*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该论文利用灵活参数化与非参数化两种联合模型分析GWTC-5.0数据，发现双黑洞并合的有效自旋（χ_eff）分布中，先前报道的偏斜（skewness）应理解为主高斯（Gaussian）本体之外存在额外结构；该额外结构在大|χ_eff|方向延伸，并呈现质量依赖的正不对称性；仅在主黑洞质量46–65 M⊙区间，数据以23:1的置信比要求存在负χ_eff成分，暗示部分层级并合（hierarchical mergers）可能发生在能产生正χ_eff过剩的环境中，如活动星系核（AGN）盘。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双黑洞的并合自旋分布χ_eff可揭示其形成通道，但此前GWTC-4.0报告的结构仅被描述为分布的偏斜，需要更精确的模型来阐明其物理起源；GWTC-5.0提供了更大样本，允许进一步检验χ_eff分布中是否存在超出简单高斯（Gaussian）假设的多峰或不对称结构，并探索其与宿主黑洞质量的关系。

Method: 采用两种联合模型——一个灵活的参数化模型（fully parametric）和一个完全非参数化模型（flexible）——同时描述χ_eff和主黑洞质量（primary mass）。利用GWTC-5.0数据集进行贝叶斯推断（Bayesian inference），将分布分解为一个以较小χ_eff为中心的非偏斜高斯（non-skewed Gaussian）本体（bulk）及其之外的额外结构，并量化该额外结构的不对称性。

Result: 发现先前报告的χ_eff分布偏斜实际上是高斯本体之外存在额外结构，该结构向较大的|χ_eff|延伸。在参数化分析和灵活分析中均发现，高斯本体之外的χ_eff分布存在质量依赖的正不对称性（positive asymmetry）——正χ_eff成分多于负χ_eff成分。唯当主黑洞质量m₁∈[46,65] M⊙时，数据以23:1的置信比要求存在负χ_eff过量。

Conclusion: 若高斯本体之外的χ_eff成分由层级并合（hierarchical mergers）产生，则部分层级并合可能发生在能生成正χ_eff过剩的天体环境中，例如活动星系核（AGN）盘；该结果为进一步区分双黑洞形成通道（如孤立双星演化与动力学通道）提供了观测约束。

Abstract: The distribution of the effective inspiral spin ($χ_\mathrm{eff}$) of the binary black holes detected by LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA can shed light on their formation pathways. We analyze the GWTC-5.0 dataset with two models-one flexible, one fully parametric-that jointly describe $χ_\mathrm{eff}$ and primary mass. We clarify that the previously-reported skewness in the $χ_\mathrm{eff}$ distribution is better understood as additional structure beyond a non-skewed Gaussian bulk centered at small $χ_\mathrm{eff}$. This additional structure extends to larger $|χ_\mathrm{eff}|$, a result previously reported using GWTC-4.0 data. We measure the asymmetry of the distribution of $χ_\mathrm{eff}$ outside the Gaussian bulk from the data. With both the parametric and the flexible analyses, we find tentative evidence for a mass-dependent excess of positive $χ_\mathrm{eff}$ over negative ones outside the Gaussian bulk. Only at $m_1 \in [46,65]\,M_\odot$ do the data require a negative $χ_\mathrm{eff}$ component outside the Gaussian bulk, with $23\text{:}1$ odds. If $χ_\mathrm{eff}$ outside the Gaussian bulk are produced by hierarchical mergers-as it has been suggested-then a fraction of those mergers may be produced in environments that can generate a surplus of binaries with positive $χ_\mathrm{eff}$, such as the disks of active galactic nuclei.

</details>


### [75] [Searching for cosmic vortices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12049)
*Marek Nikołajuk,Tomasz Karpiuk,Mirosław Brewczyk*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本研究模拟了一颗冷氦白矮星在通过黑洞时发生的强烈潮汐瓦解事件。白矮星被建模为玻色-费米液滴，通过量子流体动力学方程模拟演化。白矮星经过近星点时大量质量落入黑洞形成吸积盘，盘中出现量子化涡旋，表现为具有特征闪烁模式的强电磁辐射信号。与此同时，白矮星离开黑洞，涡旋沿其表面运动导致几何拉长，引发旋转并发射引力波。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索冷氦白矮星在黑洞强潮汐力作用下的瓦解过程及其伴随的多信使（multimessenger）信号，包括电磁辐射和引力波（gravitational wave）的起源与特征。

Method: 将白矮星建模为玻色-费米液滴（Bose-Fermi droplet），采用量子流体动力学方程（quantum hydrodynamic equations）模拟双星系统的演化。

Result: 白矮星经过近星点（periastron）时损失大量质量，这些质量落入黑洞形成吸积盘（accretion disc）。吸积盘中出现量子化涡旋（quantized vortices），表现为具有特征闪烁（flickering）模式的强电磁辐射信号，变化时标为几秒。白矮星远离黑洞时，涡旋沿其表面运动使其几何拉长，导致自转并发射引力波。

Conclusion: 冷氦白矮星的强潮汐瓦解不仅会产生吸积盘和电磁辐射，还会通过量子涡旋动力学产生独特的引力波信号，揭示了量子流体效应在天体物理（astrophysics）过程中的重要作用。

Abstract: Our study focuses on the strong tidal disruption of a cold helium white dwarf passing a black hole. We model the white dwarf as a Bose-Fermi droplet and use quantum hydrodynamic equations to simulate the binary system's evolution. As the white dwarf passes through periastron, it loses a significant amount of mass. This mass falls onto the black hole and forms an accretion disc. Quantized vortices appear in the accretion disc, manifesting as strong electromagnetic radiation signals that exhibit characteristic flickering patterns changing on a timescale of a few seconds. Meanwhile, the white dwarf moves away from the black hole. As the white dwarf moves through space, vortices run along its surface. This elongates its geometry, causing it to rotate and emit gravitational waves.

</details>
