### [76] [Breakdown of the classical rupture theory and earthquake propagation in the "forbidden" super-Rayleigh range](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11849)
*Anna Pomyalov,Fabian Barras,Eran Bouchbinder*

Main category: physics.geo-ph

TL;DR: 该研究重新审视经典破裂理论，发现当考虑断层强度对滑移速率的依赖（摩擦率依赖性）时，二维破裂可以连续地穿过传统理论认为"禁止"的超雷利（super-Rayleigh）速度区间，直接演化至超剪切（super-shear）状态，而无需经历不连续的跳跃转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典二维破裂理论认为，地震破裂传播速度在雷利波速（Rayleigh wave-speed）与剪切波速（shear wave-speed）之间的超雷利区间是被禁止的，破裂只能通过不连续的跳跃从亚雷利（sub-Rayleigh）区间进入超剪切区间。该研究旨在重新审视这一经典假设，探究摩擦律对滑移速率的依赖性是否能改变破裂传播的动力学行为。

Method: 作者重新考察了经典破裂理论中的基本假设，发展了一种考虑断层强度（摩擦阻力）对滑移速率依赖性的新破裂理论，并将其预测结果与数值模拟进行定量比较。

Result: 新理论与数值模拟在接近雷利波速的范围内定量吻合。然而，当非常接近雷利波速时，由于摩擦率的非线性（frictional rate nonlinearity），二维破裂解的特征发生改变，破裂能够连续地穿过原本"禁止"的超雷利区间进入超剪切状态，而不出现尖锐的超剪切转变。

Conclusion: 实验中被普遍观测到的摩擦率依赖性（frictional rate dependence）对快速地震破裂传播具有深远影响，能够使传统理论中禁止的超雷利区间变得可穿越，从而改变对超剪切地震破裂机制的认知。

Abstract: Earthquakes propagating faster than the shear wave-speed are commonly thought to undergo a super-shear transition upon which they discontinuously jump from the sub-Rayleigh regime to the super-shear one. The super-Rayleigh regime, i.e., the range of propagation speeds between the Rayleigh and shear wave-speeds, is regarded as "forbidden" by the two-dimensional classical rupture theory. Here, we revisit the assumptions underlying the classical theory and develop a rupture theory that takes into account the dependence of the fault strength (frictional resistance) on the slip rate. The theory quantitatively agrees with numerical simulations nearly up to the Rayleigh wave-speed. Yet, very close to the latter, two-dimensional rupture solutions change their character due to frictional rate nonlinearity and rupture continuously propagates through the "forbidden" super-Rayleigh range into the super-shear regime, without a sharp super-shear transition. These results demonstrate that frictional rate dependence, generically observed in experiments, can have profound implications for fast earthquake propagation.

</details>


### [77] [Effects of microstructural heterogeneity on the macroscopic spectrum of elastically accommodated grain-boundary sliding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12090)
*Zhengxuan Li,John F. Rudge*

Main category: physics.geo-ph

TL;DR: 通过二维有限元模拟发现，晶界粘度的宽分布（而非晶粒几何不规则性）是导致弹性调节晶界滑移（EAGBS）的德拜型损耗峰被抑制并展宽为弱背景的主要原因，解释了为何干燥橄榄石实验中观测不到显著的EAGBS峰。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典理论预测弹性调节晶界滑移（EAGBS）会产生局域的德拜型（Debye-like）损耗峰，但干燥橄榄石实验中该峰缺失或仅微弱表达，作者试图检验微结构不均匀性（microstructural heterogeneity）能否解释这一理论与实验间的偏差。

Method: 在周期性Voronoi镶嵌（Voronoi tessellation）模型上开展二维有限元模拟（2-D finite-element simulations），分别系统调控晶粒尺寸方差（grain-size variance）和晶界粘度分布（grain-boundary viscosity distribution），考察二者对EAGBS响应的影响。

Result: 不规则晶粒几何改变了基线EAGBS响应，但仅增大晶粒尺寸方差对模量和峰高的改变有限，且几乎不展宽频谱；相反，宽分布的晶界粘度会逐步抑制并展宽德拜型损耗峰，使其成为跨越宽频率区间的弱背景，这种展宽源于具有不同特征时间尺度的局域弛豫过程的叠加。

Conclusion: 干燥橄榄石中EAGBS峰的缺失并不意味着EAGBS机制本身不存在；若晶界采样到足够宽的粘度分布，宏观EAGBS贡献在实验中可能仅表现为宽衰减背景的一部分，但仍对地幔地震波衰减（seismic attenuation）和速度频散（velocity dispersion）具有相关性。

Abstract: Elastically accommodated grain-boundary sliding (EAGBS) is a plausible source of upper-mantle seismic attenuation and dispersion, yet classical theory predicts a localized Debye-like peak that is absent or only weakly expressed in dry olivine experiments. Here we test whether microstructural heterogeneity can explain this discrepancy using 2-D finite-element simulations on periodic Voronoi tessellations. We find that irregular grain geometry changes the baseline EAGBS response relative to the regular hexagonal benchmark, but increasing grain-size variance alone produces only modest changes in modulus and peak height, with little spectral broadening. In contrast, a broad distribution of grain-boundary viscosities progressively suppresses and broadens the Debye-like loss peak into a weak background spanning a wide frequency interval. This broadening arises from the superposition of many localized relaxation processes with distinct characteristic timescales and motivates a reduced-order 0-D description of the aggregate response. These results suggest that the absence of a pronounced EAGBS peak in dry olivine does not necessarily imply the absence of EAGBS mechanism itself. If grain boundaries sample a sufficiently broad viscosity distribution, the macroscopic EAGBS contribution may appear experimentally only as part of a broad attenuation background, while still remaining relevant for upper-mantle seismic attenuation and velocity dispersion.

### [78] [Linear stability analysis of particle-laden Couette-Poiseuille flows: effect of porous walls](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11360)
*Ananthapadmanabhan Ramesh,Abbas Moradi Bilondi,Mohammadreza Mahmoudian,Parisa Mirbod*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文对含颗粒的Couette-Poiseuille流在 porous 边界下的三维线性稳定性进行了分析，发现多孔层引入了渗透率相关的失稳机制，改变了经典稳定性规律，颗粒载荷在某些情况下会降低临界雷诺数（critical Reynolds number）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对颗粒悬浮液在不可渗透壁面上的稳定性已有较多认识，但多孔边界对颗粒负载流动（particle-laden flow）稳定性的影响尚不明确。该研究旨在揭示 porous 底层如何通过渗透率相关的耦合作用改变经典稳定性趋势。

Method: 采用两区域（two-domain）数值解构，悬浮颗粒仅限流体层内，不进入多孔介质；颗粒相用“弥漫气体”（dusty-gas）框架建模，多孔层内流动由体积平均Navier-Stokes（VANS）方程描述。对含颗粒的Couette-Poiseuille流进行三维线性稳定性分析（three-dimensional linear stability analysis）。

Result: 当渗透率（permeability）足够高时，颗粒载荷可降低临界雷诺数，即使在同一参数下颗粒原本对刚性壁流动起稳定作用。多孔边界引入的渗透率相关失稳机制会根本性地改变经典趋势；此外，流体-颗粒耦合在可渗透界面附近引入额外扰动分支，虽保持稳定，但通过改变耦合路径影响主导不稳定性。与不可渗透壁不同，多孔壁配置下增加Couette分量反而单调降低临界雷诺数。

Conclusion: 多孔边界可通过渗透率依赖的耦合作用，从根本上改变含颗粒剪切流中已明确的稳定性行为，表明 porous 介质的引入使经典稳定性规律发生质变。

Abstract: The current study presents a three-dimensional linear stability analysis of particle-laden Couette-Poiseuille flow suspended in a Newtonian fluid between two parallel plates, with the lower plate coated by a porous medium. The influence of suspended particles is examined using a two-domain formulation in which particles are confined to the fluid layer and do not penetrate the porous substrate. The particle-laden suspension is modeled using the dusty-gas framework, while the flow within the porous layer is described by the volume-averaged Navier-Stokes (VANS) equations. In particle-laden flows over impermeable walls, particle inertia may either stabilize or destabilize the flow depending on the governing parameters. In contrast, the presence of a porous layer introduces an additional permeability-dependent destabilizing mechanism that fundamentally modifies these classical trends. Consequently, particle loading can reduce the critical Reynolds number at sufficiently high permeability, even in parameter regimes where particles stabilize the corresponding rigid-wall flow. The coupled formulation also introduces additional disturbance branches associated with fluid-particle coupling near the permeable interface. Although these modes remain stable across the parameter space investigated, they modify the eigenspectrum and influence the dominant instability by altering coupling pathways. Furthermore, unlike impermeable-wall Couette-Poiseuille flow, where increasing the Couette component generally stabilizes the flow, the porous-wall configuration exhibits a monotonic decrease in the critical Reynolds number over the range examined. These results demonstrate that porous boundaries can fundamentally alter established stability behavior in particle-laden shear flows through permeability-dependent coupling between the suspension and the porous substrate.

</details>

### [79] [A singularity theorem in terms of asymptotic expansion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11825)
*Fabio Cavalletti,Andrea Mondino*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文提出一个奇点定理（singularity theorem），用渐近体积增长条件替代霍金-彭罗斯理论中的经典聚焦假设。在强能量条件（strong energy condition）下，引入与紧致柯西超曲面相关的渐近体积膨胀不变量（asymptotic volume-expansion invariants），证明这些不变量的一致正下界意味着过去类时测地不完备性（past timelike geodesic incompleteness），并给出从超曲面到其编年过去的时间分离显式上界。该定理可推广到满足合成强能量条件 $\mathsf{TCD}^e_p(0,N)$ 的整体双曲洛伦兹长度空间（globally hyperbolic Lorentzian length spaces），得到无需任何光滑性或可微性假设的不可延拓性（inextendibility）结果。此外，还证明了等距超曲面的面积比较定理（area comparison theorem）以及基于相关渐近膨胀不变量的体积奇点定理（volume singularity theorem）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典霍金-彭罗斯奇点定理依赖于聚焦假设（focusing hypothesis），该假设在广义相对论中通常由测地线汇的雷乔杜里方程（Raychaudhuri equation）导出，但需要光滑性条件。本文旨在用更基础的渐近体积增长条件替代聚焦假设，从而在不依赖微积分结构的情况下推广奇点定理，使其适用于更一般的度量空间框架。

Method: 引入与紧致柯西超曲面相关的渐近体积膨胀不变量（asymptotic volume-expansion invariants），在强能量条件（strong energy condition）下，建立这些不变量与过去类时测地线不完备性之间的定量关系。将结果进一步推广到整体双曲洛伦兹长度空间（globally hyperbolic Lorentzian length spaces），利用合成强能量条件 $\mathsf{TCD}^e_p(0,N)$ 处理无需光滑性假设的情形。

Result: 证明了在强能量条件下，渐近体积膨胀不变量的一致正下界可导出过去类时测地不完备性，并得到从超曲面到其编年过去的时间分离显式上界。在合成框架下，得到无需光滑性或可微性假设的不可延拓性结果。此外，还证明了等距超曲面的面积比较定理和基于相关渐近膨胀不变量的体积奇点定理。

Conclusion: 通过用渐近体积增长条件替代经典的聚焦假设，成功推广了霍金-彭罗斯奇点定理，使其适用于包括洛伦兹长度空间在内的更广泛几何框架。该结果为无需光滑性假设的广义相对论奇点理论提供了新的工具。

Abstract: We prove a singularity theorem in which the classical focusing hypothesis of Hawking--Penrose theory is replaced by a condition on asymptotic volume growth. Under the strong energy condition, we introduce asymptotic volume-expansion invariants associated with a compact Cauchy hypersurface and show that a uniform positive lower bound on these invariants implies past timelike geodesic incompleteness. More precisely, we obtain an explicit upper bound on the time-separation from the hypersurface to its chronological past. The theorem extends to globally hyperbolic Lorentzian length spaces satisfying the synthetic strong energy condition $\mathsf{TCD}^e_p(0,N)$, yielding an inextendibility result valid without any smoothness or differentiability assumption. We also prove an area comparison theorem for equidistant hypersurfaces and a volume singularity theorem based on related asymptotic expansion invariants.

</details>


### [80] [Massey products, sphere bundles and T-duality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12004)
*Gil R. Cavalcanti*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究了迭代球面丛（iterated sphere bundles）的球面T-对偶性（spherical T-duality），证明了其Gysin序列中的上同调数据可重组为消失的Massey积（Massey product）数据，并指出当这些丛配备一个超渡次数为一的整上同调类时，存在一个T-对偶的迭代球面丛，其对应于反向读取的同一Massey积。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索迭代球面丛这一几何结构中的球面T-对偶性，并揭示其Gysin序列与Massey积之间的内在联系。

Method: 通过分析迭代球面丛的Gysin序列中的上同调数据，将其重新组织为消失的Massey积的数据结构；进一步引入超渡次数为一（transgressive degree one）的整上同调类来构造T-对偶丛。

Result: 证明了对于一类迭代球面丛，其Gysin序列中的上同调数据等价于一个消失的Massey积的数据；并且，若该丛带有一个超渡次数为一的整上同调类，则存在一个T-对偶的迭代球面丛，该对偶丛对应于反向读取的同一Massey积。

Conclusion: 迭代球面丛的球面T-对偶性可由消失的Massey积来刻画，且对偶性通过反向读取Massey积实现，揭示了该对偶结构在迭代球面丛情形下的一种代数刻画方式。

Abstract: We study spherical T-duality for iterated sphere bundles. We show that for a class of iterated sphere bundles the cohomological data contained in its Gysin sequences can be repackaged into data for a vanishing Massey product. We further show that if these bundles are endowed with an integral cohomology class of transgressive degree one, then they have a T-dual iterated sphere bundle, namely, the one associated to the same Massey product read backwards.

### [81] [Slowly rotating traversable wormholes supported by radially varying string-fluid matter: From regular geometries to photon trajectories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11261)
*A. Errehymy,B. Turimov,M. A. Khan,S. Usanov,Z. Yasakov,Z. Avezmuratova*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了由径向变化弦流体（radially varying string fluid）支撑的缓慢旋转可穿越虫洞（slowly rotating traversable wormhole），该流体从类德西特（de Sitter-like）核心平滑过渡到弦主导区，形成无视界、渐近平坦的时空。旋转产生的参考系拖曳效应（frame-dragging effect）扭曲光子路径，在共转与反转轨迹间产生细微差异，而光子环结构则受红移函数、虫洞几何和旋转的共同调控，为观测旋转和内部物质分布提供了潜在信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可穿越虫洞模型多采用理想化的物质分布，缺乏对物质属性随空间位置自然变化的考量。本研究旨在构建一种物理上更自洽的弦流体模型，其性质随喉部距离径向变化，从而更真实地描述虫洞内部及周边的物质结构，并探讨旋转效应对光传播的观测影响。

Method: 采用径向变化的弦流体作为虫洞物质源，使横向压力（transverse pressure）依赖于半径位置，从而自适应周围几何结构。通过引入缓慢旋转，分析参考系拖曳效应对光子路径和圆形光子轨道（circular photon orbit）的影响，并比较不同径向分布下光子环模式的差异。

Result: 模型生成了正则、无视界且渐近平坦的时空；能量密度和形状函数（shape function）行为良好。旋转效应在喉部附近最为显著，而在远处退化为静态引力势主导。红移函数、虫洞形状和旋转共同决定了光子球（photon sphere）结构，不同弦流体径向剖面（radial profile）产生各具特征的光子环模式。

Conclusion: 径向变化的弦流体为可穿越虫洞提供了一种灵活且物理一致的物质来源，平滑连接真空主导区与弦主导区，同时支持缓慢旋转并保持时空正则性。研究展示了各向异性物质（anisotropic matter）如何影响曲率和光传播，为无视界奇异时空提供了现实框架，并为探索可穿越虫洞周围的细微观测效应开辟了新途径。

Abstract: This work investigates slowly rotating traversable wormholes supported by string fluids whose properties vary with distance from the throat. This radial variation allows the matter to transition smoothly from a de Sitter-like core near the center to a string-dominated environment further out, producing a regular, horizon-free, and asymptotically flat spacetime. By letting the transverse pressure depend on radius, the fluid naturally adapts to the surrounding geometry, resulting in a well-behaved energy density and shape function. Even modest rotation introduces frame-dragging effects that gently twist photon paths, creating subtle differences between co-rotating and counter-rotating trajectories. These effects are strongest near the throat, while at larger distances the spacetime is largely governed by the static gravitational potentials. Circular photon orbits reveal that the interplay of the redshift function, wormhole shape, and rotation shapes the photon-sphere structure. Different radial profiles of the string fluid generate distinctive photon-ring patterns, offering potential observational signatures of both the rotation and the internal matter distribution. Overall, radially varying string fluids provide a flexible and physically consistent source for traversable wormholes, bridging smoothly between vacuum-like and string-dominated regions while maintaining regularity and supporting slow rotation. This study highlights how anisotropic matter can influence both curvature and light propagation, providing a realistic framework for horizonless exotic spacetimes and suggesting new avenues to explore subtle observational effects around traversable wormholes.

### [82] [Quasinormal modes and tidal responses of black holes in generic anisotropic matter environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11380)
*Yu-Qian Zhao,Paolo Pani*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个微扰框架，用于描述球对称黑洞嵌入一般（可能各向异性）物质环境中的情况，推导了包含多方径向压力的爱因斯坦星团（Einstein cluster）解析推广，并系统分析了径向压力对各向异性环境下黑洞可观测性质（如测地线结构、轴向准正则模、潮汐洛夫数）的影响。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在球对称假设下，构建了一个可处理一般各向异性物质环境的微扰框架，并在此框架内解析推导了包含多方径向压力（polytropic radial pressure）的爱因斯坦星团推广解。

Result: 测地线结构（geodesic structure）和轴向准正则模（axial quasinormal-mode）频谱主要受整体引力红移效应（gravitational redshift effect）主导，径向压力会系统性增强环境修正；潮汐洛夫数（tidal Love numbers）则对径向压力高度敏感，在足够大的各向异性下可产生量级为1的偏差，包括严格静态磁洛夫数（strictly static magnetic Love numbers）的消失与负值。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了完整线性化方程，可推广至振铃分析（ringdown analysis）和极端质量比旋进（extreme-mass-ratio inspirals）等后续研究。

Abstract: We develop a perturbative framework for a black hole embedded in a generic, possibly anisotropic, matter environment under spherical symmetry. Our approach extends previous analyses restricted to vanishing radial pressure or to perturbative matter configurations. Within this framework, we derive an analytical generalization of the Einstein cluster that incorporates a polytropic radial pressure, and we investigate the properties of this solution. We show that both the geodesic structure and the axial quasinormal-mode spectrum remain predominantly governed by an overall gravitational redshift effect, while the radial pressure systematically enhances the environmental corrections. In contrast, the tidal Love numbers are substantially more sensitive, and can exhibit order-unity deviations, including vanishing and negative strictly static magnetic Love numbers for sufficiently large anisotropy. We present the full linearized equations, which can be applied to various extensions, including ringdown analysis and extreme-mass-ratio inspirals.

### [83] [Linearized stability of T-duality quantum-inspired thin-shell wormholes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11413)
*Francisco S. N. Lobo,Manuel E. Rodrigues*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本论文通过弦论T-对偶性（string T-duality）构造了一个薄壳虫洞（thin-shell wormhole），发现量子修正可以在消除奇点的同时打开经典薄壳虫洞所不具备的无条件稳定窗口，使可穿越虫洞在动力学上变得可行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典可穿越虫洞（traversable wormhole）需要奇异物质且存在稳定性问题，因此探索量子引力修正能否同时解决奇点消除与动力学稳定性问题具有重要理论意义。

Method: 将两个由弦论T-对偶性得到的量子修正正则时空副本沿薄壳粘合，构造薄壳虫洞；推导静态构型的表面应力（surface stresses），并在线性微扰下分析其稳定性条件。

Result: 在足够大的喉径（throat radius）下，零能量条件（null energy condition）和强能量条件（strong energy condition）可以满足；稳定性分析发现三个区域：最小喉径附近不稳定、中间区域（$a \sim l_0$）出现无条件稳定窗口（unconditional stability）、大半径区域恢复Schwarzschild-like行为需刚性状态方程。

Conclusion: T-对偶性尺度$l_0$不仅是正则化参数，更是开启经典薄壳虫洞所无的无条件稳定区域的关键物理参数，表明量子引力修正可同时消除奇点并赋予可穿越虫洞动力学可行性。

Abstract: Wormholes that are traversable in principle offer fascinating insights into general relativity, yet they typically require exotic matter and suffer from stability issues. We construct a thin-shell wormhole by gluing two copies of a quantum-corrected, regular spacetime obtained from string T-duality. This regularisation replaces the classical curvature singularity with a smooth core and introduces a fundamental length scale $l_0$. For the static configuration, we derive the surface stresses and show that, unlike the Schwarzschild case, the null and strong energy conditions can be satisfied for sufficiently large throat radii. A linearised stability analysis reveals a rich landscape: close to the minimum allowed throat radius the configuration is unstable; at intermediate radii ($a \sim l_0$) the geometric stability threshold becomes negative, yielding a window of \emph{unconditional stability} where any convex surface mass function suffices; at large radii the wormhole recovers Schwarzschild-like behaviour and stability requires a stiff equation of state. The T-duality scale $l_0$ is thus not merely a regulariser but a key physical parameter that opens a novel region of unconditional stability absent in classical thin-shell wormholes. Our results suggest that quantum-gravity-motivated modifications can simultaneously cure singularities and make traversable wormholes dynamically viable, providing new targets for gravitational-wave astronomy and theoretical studies of exotic compact objects.

</details>


### [84] [On phase-space singular surfaces in $f(R)$ gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11453)
*Dražen Glavan,David M. J. Vokrouhlický*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文对Jordan框架下的度规f(R)引力进行了哈密顿约束分析，发现正则约束分类在f'(R)=0和f''(R)=0的奇异相空间曲面上退化；进一步研究了这些曲面对线性化谱和扰动演化的影响，指出穿越奇异曲面与完全位于奇异曲面上会导致不同的扰动退化行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: f(R)引力作为广义相对论的重要修正理论，其约束结构和扰动行为尚不清晰。作者旨在通过哈密顿约束分析（Hamiltonian constraint analysis）揭示f(R)引力中奇异相空间曲面的存在及其对线性化谱和扰动演化的影响，尤其是区分背景完全位于奇异曲面上与动态穿越奇异曲面这两种情形的不同后果。

Method: 采用哈密顿约束分析方法（Dirac–Bergmann算法）对Jordan框架下的度规f(R)引力进行正则约束分类，在相空间（phase space）中识别出f'(R)=0和f''(R)=0处的奇异曲面；在此基础上对精确背景解进行线性化谱分析，并考察Starobinsky模型中FLRW轨迹穿越奇异曲面时扰动约束结构的变化。

Result: 当精确背景满足f(R)=0和f'(R)=0时，线性化谱（linearized spectrum）为空，表明已知的纯R²结果是f(R)引力中更一般退化情形的特例；在Starobinsky模型中，FLRW轨迹可以穿越f'(R)=0曲面，但穿越时非均匀扰动会出现退化的约束结构；该穿越条件更适合解释为扰动演化的正则条件（regularity condition），而非Dirac–Bergmann算法中的普通约束。

Conclusion: 背景完全位于奇异曲面与动态穿越奇异曲面导致了不同的扰动退化行为：前者使线性化谱完全消失，后者则引发约束结构的临时退化；穿越条件应重新解释为扰动演化的正则条件。这些结果深化了对f(R)引力中奇异相空间结构及其扰动理论的理解。

Abstract: We perform a Hamiltonian constraint analysis of metric $f(R)$ gravity in the Jordan frame and show that the regular constraint classification degenerates on singular phase-space surfaces located at $f'(R)\!=\!0$ and $f''(R)\!=\!0$. We then study the perturbative implications of these surfaces. For exact backgrounds satisfying $f(R)\!=\!0$ and $f'(R)\!=\!0$, the linearized spectrum is empty; the known pure $R^2$ result is therefore a special case of a more general degeneracy in $f(R)$ gravity. We also show that FLRW trajectories in the Starobinsky model can cross the surface $f'(R)=0$, but that inhomogeneous perturbations develop a degenerate constraint structure at the crossing. The resulting crossing condition is better interpreted as a regularity condition for perturbative evolution than as an ordinary constraint within the Dirac--Bergmann algorithm. Together, these results distinguish backgrounds that lie entirely on a singular surface from backgrounds that cross one dynamically, and show that the two situations lead to different perturbative degeneracies.

### [85] [Statistical-Uncertainty-Driven Selection of Evaluation Frequency for Time-Dependent Sensing Calibration: A Demonstration with KAGRA Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11504)
*Shingo Hido,Takahiro Yamamoto,Dan Chen,Takahiro Sawada,Shinji Miyoki*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 提出一种统计框架，用于在引力波探测器标定频率受实际运行条件限制时，预先筛选评价频率。将该方法应用于KAGRA第四轮观测期数据，在考虑传感函数（sensing function）统计不确定性的基础上，通过结合幅值与相位区间宽度的评分机制，选出了比现有参考频率（32.7 Hz）更优的评价频率（244 Hz）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波应变h(t)的精确标定（calibration）对探测和天体物理推断至关重要。实际探测器中，传感响应（sensing response）的慢时变通过标定线（calibration lines）追踪，但实际约束可能使标定线无法注入到有利于精确估计传感侧参数（sensing-side parameters）的频率位置，因此需要一种在约束下预先筛选评价频率的统计方法。

Method: 构建一个统计框架用于预选评价频率。对每个候选评价频率构造传感函数（sensing function），基于样本分布的经验百分位数（empirical percentiles）量化其逐段统计不确定性（segment-wise statistical uncertainty），并通过一个结合幅值区间宽度和相位区间宽度的得分（score）对候选频率进行排序。

Result: 将方法应用于KAGRA第四轮观测期数据（标称腔极点频率约18 Hz，实际传感侧标定线注入频率为32.7 Hz）。当1%幅值区间宽度与1度相位区间宽度等权时，所有4096秒分析片段均选出244 Hz。与参考频率32.7 Hz相比，幅值区间宽度在宽频范围内降至约四分之一，相位区间宽度大致相当。此外还分别评估了频率平移（frequency translation）引入的差异。

Conclusion: 该统计预选框架在实际运行约束下，能够为评价频率提供有效的预选择；所提方法有望提升引力波探测器标定中传感参数的估计精度。

Abstract: Accurate calibration of the gravitational-wave strain h(t) is essential for both detection and astrophysical inference. In operating detectors, slow temporal variations in the sensing response are tracked using calibration lines, but practical constraints can prevent those lines from being injected at frequencies that are favorable for precise estimation of sensing-side parameters. We present a statistical framework for preselecting evaluation frequencies under such constraints. We apply this framework to KAGRA data from the first part of the fourth LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA Observing Run, for which the nominal cavity-pole frequency was about 18 Hz, while the sensing-side calibration line used in practice was injected at 32.7 Hz. For each candidate evaluation frequency, we construct the sensing function, quantify its segment-wise statistical uncertainty from empirical percentiles of the sample distribution, and rank the candidates using a score that combines the interval widths of the amplitude and phase. When a 1% amplitude interval width and a 1 degree phase interval width are weighted equally, 244 Hz is selected in all 4096 s analysis segments throughout the analyzed period. Relative to the reference frequency of 32.7 Hz, the amplitude interval width is reduced to about one quarter over a broad frequency range, while the phase interval width remains broadly comparable. We also assess the discrepancy introduced by frequency translation separately. These results suggest that the proposed method provides a useful statistical preselection framework for evaluation frequencies under practical operational constraints.

### [86] [Horizon absorption in eccentric precessing binary black hole inspirals and its importance for gravitational wave data analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11705)
*Alberto Álvaro-Díaz,Gonzalo Morras*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文首次在领头阶后牛顿近似下，推导了轨道偏心率与自旋诱导进动共存的双黑洞旋近过程中视界吸收（horizon absorption）的效应，将其纳入 pyEFPEHM 波形模型，并通过解析相移、波形失配与贝叶斯参数估计量化其影响。研究表明，该效应在极端质量比、大自旋分量且长旋近持续时间的系统中最为显著；对于偏心率非零的双星，视界吸收可能在高信噪比事件中被直接测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双黑洞演化中，轨道运动与黑洞视界之间的能量和角动量交换（视界吸收）会调制引力波信号，但现有波形模型尚未完整纳入该效应，尤其是在同时考虑轨道偏心率（eccentricity）与自旋诱导进动（spin-induced precession）的情景下。本文旨在填补这一空白，为精确建模和探测致密天体本质提供理论依据。

Method: 在后牛顿（post-Newtonian, PN）展开的领头阶下，首次推导了同时包含轨道偏心率和自旋诱导进动的视界吸收修正项，并将这些修正整合到 pyEFPEHM 波形模型中。通过解析轨道相移（orbital dephasing）、波形失配（waveform mismatches）以及贝叶斯参数估计（Bayesian parameter-estimation）研究，定量评估该效应的影响。

Result: 视界吸收效应在以下系统中最大：自旋分量与轨道角动量（anti-）对齐程度高（$|\vecχ_i \cdot \hat{l}| \sim 1$）、质量比高度不对称（$q=m_2/m_1 \ll 1$）、且旋近频率跨度大（$\log(f_\mathrm{max}/f_\mathrm{min}) \gg 1$）。对于近圆双星（quasi-circular binaries），忽视视界吸收导致的参数偏差大部分被参数简并（degeneracy）所吸收，难以直接探测；但对于偏心率非零的双星，更丰富的信号形态打破了这种简并，使视界吸收在高信噪比下具有潜在的可测量性。

Conclusion: 视界吸收效应在特定参数空间（极端质量比、大自旋、长旋近）中对引力波建模有不可忽略的影响，忽视该效应会在中等信噪比水平下引入参数估计偏差。偏心率的存在可打破参数简并，为直接测量视界吸收效应开辟了可能，从而提供一种检验致密天体性质的观测途径。

Abstract: During the evolution of a binary black hole, energy and angular momentum are exchanged between the orbital motion and the individual black holes through horizon absorption, modifying both the binary dynamics and the black hole masses and spins. This leaves an imprint on the emitted gravitational waves that may be relevant for the accurate modeling of signals observed by current and future detectors, while also offering a probe of the nature of compact objects. In this work, we derive, for the first time and at leading order in the post-Newtonian expansion, the effect of horizon absorption in binary black hole inspirals with both orbital eccentricity and spin-induced precession, and we incorporate these corrections into the pyEFPEHM waveform model. We then quantify their impact through analytical estimates of the orbital dephasing, waveform mismatches, and Bayesian parameter-estimation studies. The effect is largest for systems with large spin components (anti-)aligned with the orbital angular momentum ($|\vecχ_i \cdot \hat{l}| \sim 1$), highly unequal mass ratios ($q=m_2/m_1 \ll 1$), and long inspirals spanning a wide frequency range ($\log(f_\mathrm{max}/f_\mathrm{min}) \gg 1$). For such systems, neglecting horizon absorption biases the recovered binary parameters at moderate signal-to-noise ratios. In quasi-circular binaries these biases largely absorb the effect, rendering it difficult to detect. In eccentric binaries, however, the richer signal morphology breaks this degeneracy, making horizon absorption potentially measurable in high signal-to-noise-ratio events.

### [87] [Periodic orbits as probes of charged loop quantum gravity black holes through gravitational waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11728)

Method: 利用LQG聚合（polymerization）效应替换经典奇点，通过面积间隙条件（area gap condition）确定聚合参数δ_b；构建有效势以确定最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）和边际束缚轨道（MBO）；采用Levin-Perez-Giz zoom-whirl分类法对周期轨道进行标记与定位；在四极近似下估计EMRI的引力波形，并在时域和频域中获得极化结果。

Abstract: Gravitational waves from extreme-mass-ratio inspirals (EMRI) provide a direct probe of the strong-field geometry of black holes. Motivated by this, we study the motion of test particles and the resulting gravitational wave emission in the spacetime of a charged black hole inspired by loop quantum gravity (LQG), where the classical singularity is replaced by a smooth transition surface arising from the LQG polymerization, in which its radius is set by the LQG area gap condition. As a result, the polymerization parameter $δ_b$ is uniquely determined by the mass $M$ and charge parameter $Q$, so that all cases examined in this work contain LQG correction. By constructing the effective potential, the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) and the marginally bound orbit (MBO) are determined. Periodic orbits are classified using the Levin-Perez-Giz zoom-whirl taxonomy, showing how the orbit topology shapes the waveform, so that each closed trajectory is labeled by the triple integer $(z, w, v)$ and located through the rational frequency ratio $q = ω_φ/ω_r - 1$. Within the quadrupole approximation, the gravitational waveforms for an EMRIs are estimated, and the resulting polarizations are obtained in the time-domain and frequency-domain. The resulting polarizations in the time-domain exhibit a zoom-whirl morphology, with the waveform amplitude and phase dependent on the LQG parameter. The characteristic strain peaks in the millihertz band for all values of the charge parameter $Q$, and they exceed the projected sensitivities of LISA, Taiji, and TianQin, suggesting that future observations could place meaningful constraints on the LQG polymerization parameter in the strong-field regime.

### [88] [Comisso-Asenjo Mechanism in Rotating $\mathcal{N}=2,U(1)^2$ Gauged Supergravity Black Holes: Extended Comparison With Kerr Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11732)

Result: 发现可在自旋参数$a\sim0.39$（低于Kerr极端情形$a\sim1$）下实现更高效率的能量提取。极端Kerr效率极限（$\eta>1.495$）可在某些极端参数组合下被超越。可观测Lundquist数$S_{\rm obs}$在旋转黑洞时空中因lapse函数$\alpha$引入观测者依赖的角度修正，偏离标准Sweet-Parker标度律。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate energy extraction via the Comisso-Asenjo (CA) magnetic reconnection process near a coupled $\mathcal{N}=2,\,U(1)^2$ gauged supergravity Black Hole (BH). Our study focuses on the combined impact of the independent parameter set $p_i\in(N_g,g,v,e)$ with the spin parameter $a$ on the extracted energy ($ε_{\pm}$), efficiency ($η$), and extracted power ($\mathcal{P}_{CA}$), aiming to identify optimal combinations where energy can be extracted with higher efficiency in certain cases at lower spin $(a\sim0.39)$ than the Kerr extremal case $(a\sim1)$. Using the spacetime parameters, we explore various cases leading to distinct spacetimes and provide an extended comparison with the Kerr Black Hole (KBH). We also examine the influence of the orientation angle ($ξ$) and magnetization parameter ($σ_0$) on both efficiency and extracted power. The statistical Kendall's Tau approach allows us to identify the key independent parameters acting as boosters or dampers in the energy extraction process and to visualize the relationship between $(N_g,g,v,e)$ and the physical outputs $(a_{\rm ext},r_E,r_{\rm ergo},ε_{\pm},η,\mathcal{P}_{CA},R_η,R_{\mathcal{P}})$. Furthermore, we show that the observable Lundquist number $S_{\rm obs}$ in rotating BH spacetimes acquires an observer-dependent angular dependence through the lapse function $(α)$. This leads to deviations from the standard Sweet-Parker scaling when expressed in terms of observable quantities.

### [89] [Critical Coupling Surfaces in $κ(R,T)$ Gravity: Regularity, Gravitational Screening, and Phase Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11942)
*Ginés R. Pérez Teruel*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究κ(R,T)引力理论中临界耦合条件κ=0的物理性质，证明该处表观奇异性可消除，守恒律保持正则，并揭示临界超曲面作为引力筛选面（gravitational screening surfaces）分隔吸引与排斥引力相，同时阻碍全局爱因斯坦框架（Einstein frame）的描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大多数研究假设有效引力耦合非零，但临界超曲面（critical hypersurfaces）在κ(R,T)引力理论中是众多可容许耦合函数的普遍特征。本文旨在澄清κ=0处表观奇异性的本质，并系统分析其对理论结构与物理后果的影响。

Method: 通过严格分析非守恒方程（non-conservation equation）的代数形式，证明κ=0处的表观奇异性源于守恒律的重写方式，而非基本方程本身的奇异性。进一步通过导出相容性条件（compatibility condition）(∇^μκ)T_{μν}=0，系统地分析了临界超曲面的几何与物理结构。

Result: 证明了κ=0处基本方程保持正则性，表观奇异性为伪像。推导了相容性条件(∇^μκ)T_{μν}=0，将临界超曲面解释为分隔吸引与排斥引力相（attractive and repulsive gravitational phases）的引力筛选面。此外，临界耦合超曲面的存在阻碍了全局爱因斯坦框架的构建，从而将κ(R,T)引力与仅依赖能量-动量张量（energy-momentum tensor）代数重定义的引力理论区分开来。

Conclusion: 本研究澄清了κ(R,T)引力中临界耦合条件的物理本质，揭示了其作为引力筛选面的新物理解释，并指出了该理论在宇宙学和天体物理学中的潜在应用前景。同时，该结果强调了κ(R,T)引力与非最小耦合理论相比在框架选择上的根本差异。

Abstract: We investigate the critical regime $κ(R,T)=0$ in $κ(R,T)$ gravity. While most studies assume a non-vanishing effective gravitational coupling, the existence of critical hypersurfaces where $κ$ vanishes is a generic feature of many admissible coupling functions. We show that the apparent singularity of the non-conservation equation is an artifact of a rewritten form of the conservation law and that the fundamental equations remain regular at $κ=0$. We further analyze the structure of critical hypersurfaces, derive the associated compatibility condition $(\nabla^μκ)T_{μν}=0$, and discuss their interpretation as gravitational screening surfaces separating attractive and repulsive gravitational phases. The existence of critical coupling hypersurfaces also obstructs a global Einstein-frame description, distinguishing $κ(R,T)$ gravity from theories based solely on algebraic redefinitions of the energy-momentum tensor. Possible cosmological and astrophysical consequences are briefly explored.

</details>


### [90] [A post-selected quantum model of cosmic acceleration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12297)
*Dimitris Lionas,Charis Anastopoulos,Konstantinos Gourgouliatos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出宇宙加速膨胀源于量子后选择（quantum post-selection）效应，而非传统宇宙学常数或暗能量。通过构建基于后选择和粗粒化（coarse-graining）的最小预测宇宙学模型，该模型无需引入暗能量或修改广义相对论即可生成有效晚期加速，与超新星和宇宙计时器数据的拟合在统计上具有竞争力，并自然避免了巧合问题（coincidence problem），同时预测了显著不同于ΛCDM模型的加速度参数（jerk parameter）。

Method: 基于后选择准经典动力学（post-selected quasiclassical dynamics）的已有工作，构建一个最小预测宇宙学模型，核心机制为通过后选择和粗粒化（coarse-graining）生成有效晚期加速，不使用宇宙学常数、暗能量或修改广义相对论；模型仅需在标准弗里德曼演化（Friedmann evolution）基础上增加至多两个参数。

Result: 与Ia型超新星（type Ia supernova）和宇宙计时器（cosmic chronometer）数据的拟合结果显示该模型在统计上具有竞争力，且自然避免了巧合问题；模型在早期重现了标准辐射主导和物质主导行为，并预测当前加速度参数（jerk parameter）显著偏离ΛCDM模型预测值。

Conclusion: 宇宙加速膨胀可能是一种宏观量子宇宙学效应（macroscopic quantum cosmological effect），而非源于额外的宇宙学流体或修改的引力动力学。

Abstract: The origin of cosmic acceleration remains a central problem in cosmology, commonly attributed to a cosmological constant within the $Λ$CDM model or to dynamical dark energy. Here, we develop an alternative approach in which acceleration emerges from quantum post-selection, a standard feature of quantum theory that is not usually incorporated into cosmological modelling. While quantum theory admits both pre-selected and post-selected ensembles, quantum cosmological models are almost exclusively formulated in terms of initial conditions. Building on previous work on post-selected quasiclassical dynamics, we construct a minimal predictive cosmological model in which post-selection and coarse-graining generate effective late-time acceleration without introducing a cosmological constant, dark energy, or modifications of general relativity. The resulting expansion history is highly constrained theoretically and depends on at most two parameters beyond standard Friedmann evolution. Confrontation with type Ia supernova and cosmic chronometer data yields statistically competitive fits while naturally avoiding the coincidence problem. The model also reproduces the standard radiation- and matter-dominated behaviour at early times and predicts a present-day jerk parameter significantly different from the $Λ$CDM value. These results suggest that cosmic acceleration may arise as a macroscopic quantum cosmological effect rather than from additional cosmological fluids or modified gravitational dynamics.

### [91] [Learning from almost nothing: How neural networks survive heavy input corruption](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11319)
*Justin Tahmassebpur,Asadullah Bhuiyan,Hyejin Kim,Omri Lesser*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了属性噪声（attribute noise）下从被破坏输入中学习的问题。通过实验和理论分析发现，神经网络在输入被破坏超过90%时仍能保持远超随机水平的鲁棒性。作者采用平均场（mean-field）方法分析无限宽网络，推导出分类的主导决策规则为最近类均值（nearest-class-mean）原型规则，该规则对多种MLP架构、深度、激活函数和噪声分布具有普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从不完美数据中学习是机器学习中的核心议题，连接了鲁棒性的实践问题与可学习性的理论问题。属性噪声（attribute noise）——在标签完整但输入被破坏的条件下学习——相较于标签噪声（label-noise）受到的关注明显不足，因此需要对其进行深入分析。

Method: 采用两种噪声模型：加性噪声（additive noise）和替换噪声（replacement noise）。通过多层感知机（MLPs）在被破坏的分类数据集上进行实验，并利用平均场（mean-field）思想分析高破坏率下的无限宽网络，推导出分类结果的领先阶（leading-order）决策规则。

Result: 实验发现神经网络能在输入被破坏超过90%时保持远超随机水平的准确率。理论推导表明，网络实现了一个原型规则（prototype rule），即最近类均值（nearest-class-mean）决策规则：将测试点分配给其训练集平均最接近的类别。该规则对多种MLP架构、不同深度、广泛的激活函数和噪声分布具有普适性。

Conclusion: 该最近类均值机制与有限宽网络实验行为高度匹配，为即使单个训练样本几乎不携带信号时学习仍可成功提供了可解释且易于分析的说明。

Abstract: Learning from imperfect data is a central theme in machine learning, connecting practical questions of robustness to fundamental questions of learnability. Here we examine attribute noise: learning from corrupted inputs while keeping the labels intact, a setting that has received considerably less analytical attention than its label-noise counterpart. We consider two types of corruption models: additive noise and replacement noise. Through experiments with multi-layer perceptrons (MLPs) on corrupted classification datasets, we find that neural networks remain robust, maintaining well-above-chance accuracy even when inputs are >90% corrupted -- far beyond human recognition. To understand this robustness, we analyze infinite-width networks in the heavy-corruption regime using a mean-field-inspired approach and derive a leading-order decision rule for the classification outcome: the network implements a prototype rule, the nearest-class-mean, assigning each test point to the class whose training-set average it most closely resembles. This leading-order decision rule is universal across a broad range of MLP architectures, holding for any depth, as well as a wide class of activation functions and noise distributions. The same centroid mechanism closely matches finite-width network behavior in our experiments and provides an interpretable and analytically tractable account of why learning can succeed even when individual training examples carry almost no signal.

</details>


### [92] [Range-Aware Bayesian Optimization for Discovering Diverse Designs within Target Property Windows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11574)
*Shengli Jiang,Jason Wu,Charles M. Schroeder,Michael A. Webb*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发了一种范围感知贝叶斯优化（range-aware Bayesian optimization, BO）框架，其获取函数（acquisition function）直接对候选解满足目标范围的后验概率（posterior probability）进行评分。该框架自然地扩展到在共享候选空间上并行追求多个不同规格。

Result: 在基准任务中，范围感知获取函数一致地恢复了比标准BO基线和近期目标寻求方法（goal-seeking methods）更大且更多样化的有效设计集。在两个实际设计案例研究（涉及聚合物合成的反应条件优化和基于量子化学计算的序列定义低聚物发现）中进一步证明了其实用性。

Conclusion: 范围感知BO可以为规格驱动设计（specification-driven design）提供一个实用且样本高效（sample-efficient）的基础，特别是在设计灵活性和解多样性（solution diversity）是重要考量因素时。

Abstract: In many materials and product design problems, desirable candidates exhibit properties that fall within an acceptable range rather than achieve a single optimum. Recovering multiple, distinct solutions that satisfy such specifications is also practically valuable, as some candidates may be preferred for reasons of cost, processability, or robustness that are difficult to encode directly in an objective function. Here, we develop a range-aware Bayesian optimization (BO) framework in which the acquisition function directly scores the posterior probability that a candidate satisfies a target range. The framework naturally extends to parallel pursuit of multiple distinct specifications over a shared candidate space. Across benchmark tasks, range-aware acquisition consistently recovers larger and more diverse sets of valid designs than standard BO baselines and recent goal-seeking methods. Its utility is further demonstrated in two practically motivated design case studies involving optimizing reaction conditions for polymer synthesis and sequence-defined oligomer discovery for prescribed optical absorption bands, supported by quantum chemical calculations. These results suggest that range-aware BO can provide a practical and sample-efficient foundation for specification-driven design, particularly when design flexibility and solution diversity are important considerations.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有限维算子代数可以视为 $\mathrm{C}^*$、$\mathrm{W}^*$ 或 $\mathrm{H}^*$-代数，这些不同的代数结构导致了不同的模块范畴（categories of modules）和对应 2-范畴（correspondence 2-categories），目前缺乏系统理解这些差异的统一框架。

Method: 首先利用 $2\mathsf{Vect}$ 上 $O(2)$-作用的不动点引入 $G$-Hermitian 2-向量空间（$G$-Hermitian $2$-vector spaces）；然后提出此类配对何时为“正定”（positive）的判据，将 Hermitian 向量空间到 Hilbert 空间的推广过程加以泛化；最后勾勒了一个归纳性方法，用于在任意维数下定义更高 Hilbert 空间（higher Hilbert spaces）。

Result: 建立了 $G$-dagger 范畴与不同算子代数结构之间的对应关系，给出了正定配对的判据条件，并提出了向更高范畴推广的归纳方案。

Conclusion: 本文从 $G$-dagger 范畴的视角统一理解了有限维 $\mathrm{C}^*$、$\mathrm{W}^*$、$\mathrm{H}^*$-代数在范畴论层面的差异，并为未来在更高维度（beyond the 2-categorical setting）定义 Hilbert 空间结构提供了理论路径。

Abstract: Finite-dimensional operator algebras can be viewed as $\mathrm{C}^*$, $\mathrm{W}^*$, or $\mathrm{H}^*$-algebras, leading to different notions for their categories of modules and correspondence 2-categories. In this article, we show how these differences can be understood systematically using the notion of $G$-dagger category from arXiv:2403.01651 for different subgroups $G\leq O(2)$. To do so, we first introduce $G$-Hermitian $2$-vector spaces using fixed points of a certain $O(2)$-action on $2\mathsf{Vect}$. We then propose criteria for when such pairings are `positive', generalizing the passage from Hermitian vector spaces to Hilbert spaces. Finally, we outline an inductive approach to defining higher Hilbert spaces in arbitrary dimension, suggesting an extension of these ideas beyond the 2-categorical setting.

### [95] [Deterministic Single-Photon Emitter Arrays in Hexagonal Boron Nitride by Carbon-Assisted Focused Ion Beam Engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12304)
*Mangababu Akkanaboina,Rohit Kumar,Brijesh Kumar,Hrushikesh Gawali,Parul Sharma,Ikshvaku Shyam,Anshuman Kumar*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用三步无光刻制造工艺：第一步为定点选择性镓（Ga）聚焦离子束刻蚀（focused ion beam milling）；第二步在图案化区域进行纳米级保形碳沉积（conformal carbon deposition）；第三步进行热退火（thermal annealing）处理。

Result: 在100个制造位点上实现了约89%的位点关联发射体产率（site-correlated emitter yield）。二阶自关联测量（second-order autocorrelation measurements）显示显著的三能级发射体动力学特征，最佳发射体纯度达到g^(2)(0)=0.15±0.09。

Conclusion: 该方法是首个结合镓离子刻蚀、选择性碳工程和热退火的无光刻直接写入（lithography-free, direct-write）方法，可实现hBN中SPE的确定性生成。工艺可重复性已在多个独立制备样品中得到验证，为集成量子光子学中按需SPE阵列的规模化制备提供了可行路径。

Abstract: The realization of on-chip photonic circuits requires scalable and deterministic single-photon emitters (SPEs) at room temperature, which remain a challenge in van der Waals materials. In this work, we report a novel three-step fabrication process for the generation of spatially controlled SPE arrays in hexagonal boron nitride (hBN). The process comprises site-selective gallium (Ga) focused ion beam milling, nanoscale conformal carbon deposition over the patterned regions, and subsequent thermal annealing. The synergistic combination of these steps resulted in a site-correlated emitter yield of ($\sim 89\%$) across 100 fabrication sites. Second-order autocorrelation measurements revealed pronounced three-level emitter dynamics where the best emitters exhibited high purity ($g^{(2)}(0)=0.15 \pm 0.09$).To the best of our knowledge, this is the first lithography-free, direct-write approach combining Ga-ion milling, selective carbon engineering, and thermal annealing to deterministically generate \hBN{} \SPE{}s. The reproducibility of the method is validated across multiple independently fabricated samples. These results establish a scalable, lithography-free pathway toward on-demand SPE arrays relevant to integrated quantum photonics.

### [96] [Quantifying the Distribution of Biexciton Emission Efficiencies in Colloidal Quantum Shells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12398)
*Tjom Arens,Dulanjan Harankahage,Divesh Nazar,Mikhail Zamkov,Freddy T. Rabouw*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于串扰抑制的SPAD阵列光子关联方法，实现了对超过1000个胶体量子壳的多光子发射高通量量化，揭示了双激子发射效率的近高斯分布及其与粒子亮度的体积缩放关联，为解析纳米粒子集合中的多光子异质性提供了可扩展的技术路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文引入了一种串扰抑制的SPAD阵列光子关联方法（crosstalk-suppressed SPAD-array photon-correlation approach）。通过将同一样品的两幅图像投影到探测器阵列的远端区域，避免探测器像素间的短程串扰（short-range crosstalk）；利用时间门控（time gating）抑制暗计数符合事件，并区分单个发射体与团簇（clusters）。

Result: 该方法应用于量子壳（quantum shells），揭示出双激子发射效率（biexciton emission efficiency）呈现近高斯分布（near-Gaussian distribution），均值0.55，估计内禀标准差（intrinsic standard deviation）0.12。批次内双激子效率与粒子亮度（particle brightness）的相关性符合Auger淬灭（Auger quenching）的体积缩放（volume scaling）规律。

Conclusion: SPAD阵列光子关联方法为解决纳米粒子集合中多光子异质性问题提供了可扩展的技术路径，能够高通量、高精度地表征大量发射体，并为理解多激子物理机制（如Auger淬灭）提供了统计依据。

Abstract: The efficiency of multi-photon emission is an important characteristic of quantum light sources. Bright multi-photon emission is desirable for high-power lighting and lasers, while its complete suppression is required for high-purity single-photon generation. In colloidal quantum emitters, multi-photon emission can vary significantly between individual particles. Resolving this heterogeneity remains challenging with conventional particle-by-particle approaches. Here, we introduce a crosstalk-suppressed SPAD-array photon-correlation approach for high-throughput quantification of multi-photon emission from more than 1000 colloidal quantum shells. By projecting two images of the same sample onto distant regions of the detector array, we avoid short-range crosstalk between detector pixels. Time gating suppresses dark-count coincidences and distinguishes individual emitters from clusters. Applying this method to quantum shells reveals a near-Gaussian distribution of biexciton emission efficiencies, with a mean of 0.55 and an estimated intrinsic standard deviation of 0.12. Intra-batch correlations between the biexciton efficiency and the particle brightness are consistent with the volume scaling of Auger quenching. These results establish SPAD-array photon correlation as a scalable route to resolve multi-photon heterogeneities in nanoparticle ensembles.

### [97] [Tunable Snapping and Rigid Foldability in the Mars Origami Pattern](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12228)
*Menelaos Raptis,Thomas C. Hull*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文揭示火星铺砌（Mars tessellation）折纸超材料中由于几何不相容性导致的突跳失稳（snap-through instability）机制，并通过激光刻痕实现可编程调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对非刚性可折叠折纸图案中突跳失稳（snap-through instability）的起源及其可调性尚缺乏深入理解，亟需揭示其底层机制。

Method: 以火星铺砌（Mars tessellation）——一种由方形和菱形面交替组成的四度顶点（degree-4 vertex）折纸图案——为研究对象，分析其几何相容性，并借助应变场模拟（strain-field simulation）指导激光刻痕（laser scoring）引入额外对角折痕。

Result: 火星铺砌因相邻单元间折叠速度比无法一致传播而被证明非刚性可折叠；折叠时面发生弯曲，产生力-位移曲线中约92.6±5.5%平均力降的突跳不连续性（snap-through discontinuity），对应亚稳态（metastable state）之间的转变；激光刻痕可连续调控突跳幅度。

Conclusion: 该工作阐明了一种通用机制：几何阻挫（geometric frustration）可被用于在薄板超材料中编程多稳态（multistability）行为。

Abstract: Origami-inspired metamaterials exploit the interplay between geometry and elasticity to achieve programmable mechanical responses. Yet the origin and tunability of snap-through instabilities in non-rigidly foldable patterns remain poorly understood. Here we show that the Mars tessellation, a degree-4 vertex origami pattern composed of alternating square and rhombic faces, is not rigidly foldable because the folding-speed ratios required for vertex compatibility cannot be propagated consistently across neighboring units. This geometric incompatibility forces the facets to bend during folding, giving rise to a reproducible snap-through discontinuity in the force-displacement curve with a mean force drop of about 92.6 +/- 5.5 %, marking a transition between metastable states. Laser scoring of additional diagonal creases, guided by strain-field simulations, enables continuous tuning of the snap magnitude. These results reveal a general mechanism by which geometric frustration can be harnessed to program multistability in thin-sheet metamaterials.

</details>


### [98] [A quantitative approach to flowing supercooled liquids: From microscopic heterogeneities to rheology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11597)
*Dong-Xu Yu,Zhe Wang*

TL;DR: 本文基于两态范式（two-state paradigm）提出一个超冷液体（supercooled liquids）的流动理论模型，将流动视为瞬态类固体与类液体区域的动态共存。模型仅依赖由平衡态确定的参数，即可定量重现涵盖稳态和启动剪切（start-up shear）在内的流变响应，同时捕捉分子动态异质性（dynamic heterogeneity）的演化，揭示了结构性与动态异质性在流变行为中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软玻璃材料（soft glassy materials）在宏观和分子尺度上展现复杂流动行为，其基本物理机制尚不清晰，是一个悬而未决的挑战。本文旨在为超冷液体这类典型玻璃态流体的流动行为建立一个具有物理直观性的理论模型。

Method: 模型基于两态范式，将流动概念化为瞬态类固体区域与类液体区域的动态共存。核心物理要素包括：表征中等范围结构有序（medium-range structural order）的相关长度（correlation length），以及限制应力在类固体区域内传播的局域弹性介导相互作用（localized elasticity-mediated interaction）。所有模型参数均由平衡态（equilibrium state）单独确定。

Result: 在仅使用平衡态参数的情况下，模型定量重现了宽剪切率范围内超冷液体的流变响应，包括稳态剪切和启动剪切。同时，模型成功捕捉了分子动态异质性的演化特征。

Conclusion: 模型在宏观流变学与微观时空涨落两个层面上的成功，强调了结构性异质性和动态异质性在支配流变响应中的核心作用。此外，该工作为理解超冷液体的流动行为如何内嵌于其平衡态性质提供了直接的理论依据。

Abstract: Soft glassy materials display rich and complex flow behaviors across both macroscopic and molecular scales, and a fundamental understanding of these phenomena remains an outstanding challenge. Here, we propose a theoretical model for the flow of supercooled liquids -- a typical class of glassy fluids -- based on a two-state paradigm that conceptualizes the flow as a dynamic coexistence of transient solid-like and liquid-like regions. The model rests on two essential physical ingredients: a correlation length that captures medium-range structural order, and a localized elasticity-mediated interaction that restricts stress propagation within solid-like regions. Remarkably, with all parameters determined solely from equilibrium state, the model quantitatively reproduces rheological responses -- including both steady-state and start-up shear -- for a broad range of shear rates. Furthermore, it simultaneously captures the evolution of molecular dynamic heterogeneity. This dual success -- spanning macroscopic rheology and microscopic spatiotemporal fluctuations -- underscores the pivotal role of structural and dynamic heterogeneities in governing the rheological response. Moreover, it provides a direct understanding of how the flow behaviors of a supercooled liquid are embedded in its equilibrium properties.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活性固体（active solids）中的非互易相互作用（nonreciprocal interactions）违反了作用-反作用对称性，并在应变下产生净响应；现有研究缺乏统一的几何框架来描述这类体系中细长体的弹性流体动力学行为。

Method: 在欧几里得对称性（Euclidean symmetries）的假设下，推导出非互易细长体的形状空间公式，该公式将内在形变与刚体运动分离，最终形成一个非线性反应-平流-扩散系统（reaction-advection-diffusion system），代表一种几何流（geometric flow）。

Result: 该非线性系统在活性驱动不稳定性作用下生成了稳态、振荡和混沌模式；这些模式分别表现为刚性运动、游泳运动和混沌运动。

Conclusion: 该工作将非互易弹性流体动力学与几何模式形成联系起来，并统一了近年来细长活性结构中的相关观测结果。

Abstract: Nonreciprocal interactions in active solids violate action-reaction symmetry and produce a net response to strain. Assuming invariance under Euclidean symmetries, we derive a shape-space formulation for the elastohydrodynamics of nonreciprocal slender bodies that separates intrinsic deformation from rigid motion. The resulting nonlinear reaction-advection-diffusion system represents a geometric flow whose activity-driven instabilities generate steady, oscillatory, and chaotic patterns. These manifest as rigid, swimming, and chaotic motion, linking nonreciprocal elastohydrodynamics to geometric pattern formation and unifying recent observations in slender active structures.

This strategy enables the predictive construction of equilibrium paths and the inverse design of multi-layer meta-structures, using prescribed critical points to control post-critical behaviour. It provides a foundation for the inverse design and optimisation of architected mechanical metamaterials with programmable responses.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 边界条件和空间异质性共同支配着收缩性活性凝胶的力学行为。研究结果为细胞和组织尺度的应力调控提供了见解，并可能为适应性软材料（adaptive soft materials）和仿生机器人系统（bioinspired robotic systems）的设计提供参考。

Abstract: Cells dynamically generate, transmit, and dissipate stress. Central to these processes is the actomyosin cortex, an active contractile material that drives cellular mechanical behavior. To address this, we employ reconstituted actomyosin gels to investigate cellular contractility. We find that pinned contraction leads to stress buildup, delaying contraction, producing intermittent dynamics, and generating spatially nonuniform strain fields. Stress is relieved through several pathways, including active-stress-driven symmetric constriction and defect-driven processes such as boundary detachment and internal rupture. We develop a hydrodynamic model incorporating elastic, viscous, and active stress contributions that distinguishes between stress-accumulation and stress-release phases and links variations in active stress to the observed intermittent dynamics. The model predicts distinct energy relaxation rates before and after detachment events, providing insight into stress dissipation. We compare experiments with numerical simulations, which reproduce the observed behavior and reveal how internal energy is generated and dissipated during stress buildup and relaxation. Together, our results demonstrate how boundary conditions and spatial heterogeneity govern the mechanical behavior of contractile active gels. These findings provide insight into stress regulation in cellular and tissue-scale systems and may inform the design of adaptive soft materials and bioinspired robotic systems.

### [104] [Perspective: The Physics of Active Solids -- From Hamiltonians to Active Matter Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11950)

Result: 通过活性哈密顿量框架，研究能够阐明驱动系统（driven systems）与活性系统之间的对应关系，并解释增强的Mermin-Wagner-Hohenberg（MWH）涨落——该涨落可能源于空间随机活性力与长波长密度（声子）模式的强耦合。

Conclusion: 跨系统建立活性-振荡剪切对应关系（activity-oscillatory shear correspondence）对于证明其普适性、揭示底层大尺度涌现物理（emergent physics）以及为所提假设奠定更坚实的理论基础至关重要。

Abstract: The physics of active matter, wherein constituent particles consume energy to generate autonomous motion, has revolutionized non-equilibrium statistical mechanics. While a large body of work has successfully elucidated the behavior of dilute active systems, the dense regime -- characterized by ``active glasses and active solids'' -- presents profound challenges that defy conventional theoretical frameworks. Recent observations reveal two striking features in these dense systems: an apparent enhancement of Mermin-Wagner-Hohenberg (MWH) fluctuations leading to anomalous long-wavelength density fluctuations, and a remarkable correspondence between activity-induced annealing and annealing via oscillatory shear. In this perspective article, we propose a novel approach toward a deeper understanding of dense active matter: by developing active Hamiltonian models as equilibrium reference frameworks, we map out pathways toward non-equilibrium active systems. This strategy allows us to elucidate both the correspondence between driven and active systems and the enhanced MWH fluctuations, which likely arise from a strong coupling between spatially random active forces and long-wavelength density (phonon) modes. We outline a comprehensive roadmap employing complementary approaches, including the active Hamiltonian formalism, comparative studies of oscillatory shear in active and passive solids, and investigations of chiral active matter. Establishing this activity-oscillatory shear correspondence across diverse systems is essential to demonstrate its universality, reveal the underlying large-scale emergent physics, and place our hypothesis on a firmer theoretical ground.

### [105] [When and how particles are removed by drops](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12062)
*Abhinav Naga,Franziska Sabath,Doris Vollmer,Halim Kusumaatmaja*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 通过格子玻尔兹曼模拟（lattice Boltzmann simulations）和共聚焦显微镜实验（confocal microscopy experiments），揭示了液滴碰撞表面颗粒时至少存在六种不同的清除场景，并发现毛细力（capillary force）在颗粒清除中具有双重作用：切向分量促进清除，法向分量可能阻碍清除。通过引入无量纲的毛细捕获参数（capillary capture parameter），可预测不同颗粒与表面性质下的清除行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 结合格子玻尔兹曼模拟与共聚焦显微镜实验，系统研究液滴碰撞表面颗粒时毛细力（capillary force）与摩擦力（friction forces）之间的复杂相互作用。

Result: 发现至少存在六种不同的颗粒清除场景；毛细力具有双重作用——切向分量始终促进清除，而法向分量可能阻碍清除；引入无量纲的毛细捕获参数（capillary capture parameter），可预测不同颗粒与表面性质下的清除行为。

Conclusion: 这些结果为设计易于清洁的表面提供了定量设计原则，有助于在清洁过程中最小化水和化学物质的使用。

Abstract: Particulate contaminants decrease the power output of solar panels, the transparency of windows, and are detrimental to microelectronics, where even a single particle can induce a short circuit. Despite significant research on particle adhesion and self-cleaning, it remains unclear when and how a drop can remove a particle from a surface, thus efficiently cleaning the surface. Here, by combining lattice Boltzmann simulations and confocal microscopy experiments, we show that at least six different scenarios arise from the complex interplay between capillary and friction forces when a drop collides with a particle. Notably, the capillary force plays a dual role in particle removal: while its tangential component always drives removal, its normal component can also hinder it. By introducing a dimensionless capillary capture parameter, we can predict particle removal across a wide range of particle and surface properties. These results provide quantitative design principles for easy-to-clean surfaces that minimize water and chemical usage.

Motivation: 揭示溶剂介导的平均力势（PMF）与溶质排除体积之间的解析关系，并验证该框架在软物质粗粒化模拟（如DPD）中的适用性。

Method: 基于Ornstein-Zernike积分方程理论，采用超网链（HNC）闭包近似，将PMF表达为溶质特异性广义排除体积函数的卷积；并在硬球极限下与Asakura-Oosawa耗尽势进行对照验证，再推广至超软粒子体系。

Result: 在无结构点溶剂与硬核溶质极限下，该方法精确恢复了经典的Asakura-Oosawa耗尽势；在耗散粒子动力学（DPD）的超软粒子系统中，溶剂介导的PMF也能以相当高的精度恢复。

Conclusion: 在粗粒化DPD分子模拟中，若假设的分子内键长小于DPD势的作用范围，非键排斥的参数化会对键长敏感，其根源在于软排除体积函数的重叠效应。

Abstract: In the infinite dilution limit, we show that the solvent-mediated potential of mean force (PMF) between solutes, extracted from the hypernetted-chain (HNC) closure of the Ornstein-Zernike equations, can expressed as a convolution between solute-specific generalised excluded volume functions. In the limit of a structureless solvent of point particles and hard core solutes, this recovers the exact Asakura-Oosawa depletion potential as the overlap between excluded volume spheres. The methodology can be deployed for ultrasoft particle systems such as those encountered in dissipative particle dynamics (DPD), where the solvent-mediated PMF can be recovered with considerable accuracy. These results confirm that in coarse-grained molecular DPD simulations the parametrisation of the non-bonded repulsions is sensitive to the assumed intramolecular bond lengths if they are smaller than the range of the DPD potential, due to the overlap of the soft excluded volume functions.

</details>


<div id='cs.IT'></div>

# cs.IT [[Back]](#toc)

### [107] [Color-Rule-Function Encoding for Combinatorial Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11365)
*Alexander Khitun*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为颜色-规则-函数（CRF）的系统编码框架，用于在组合存储器（combinatorial memory）中表示信息。该方法通过路径选择、单元赋值、规则定义和布尔函数构建四个步骤实现编码，其设计空间规模远超传统存储器，但伴随硬件复杂度的增加。通过定制化模块设计可显著降低硬件开销，有望实现超过Exabit/cm²的数据存储密度。关键挑战在于固定硬件约束下最小汉明距离（Hamming distance）的实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 组合存储器（combinatorial memory）是一类通过在结构化网格（mesh）中编码路径集合来存储信息的存储器。现有研究缺乏系统性的编码方法，本文旨在引入一种可扩展的编码框架。

Method: 提出颜色-规则-函数（Color-Rule-Function, CRF）框架，包含四个关键步骤：（1）选择网格中的一组路径序列；（2）为每个单元分配数值（如颜色）；（3）基于每条路径上遇到的数值定义规则集；（4）构建确定每条路径状态的布尔函数（Boolean function）。

Result: CRF框架的设计空间规模在缩放速度上本质性地快于传统存储器，但这一优势伴随着硬件复杂度的提升。通过定制化模块设计可大幅降低硬件开销。估算表明数据存储密度可能超过Exabit/cm²。

Conclusion: CRF编码与定制化模块设计的结合可能在数据存储密度上带来实际优势。需要进一步研究的关键问题是：在固定硬件约束下，任意目标比特序列与CRF框架内可实现的最近序列之间的最小汉明距离（Hamming distance）。

Abstract: Combinatorial memory is a class of memory in which information is encoded in the set of paths through a structured mesh. In this work, we introduce a systematic encoding framework, referred to as the Color-Rule-Function (CRF) approach, for representing information in combinatorial memory. The method consists of four key steps: selecting a sequence of paths in the mesh, assigning values (e.g., colors) to each cell, defining a set of rules based on the values encountered along each path, and constructing a Boolean function that determines the state of each path. . The coding procedure is illustrated by several examples. The design space scales of the CRF scale fundamentally faster compared to conventional memory. This apparent advantage arises from the use of rule-based and functional representations but is accompanied by increased hardware complexity. A possible hardware realization of the CRF framework is discussed. Importantly, the hardware overhead can be substantially reduced through the use of customized modules. The examples of the customized design are described in the text. The combination of CRF coding with customized module design may lead to a practical advantage in data storage density. According to the estimates, the data storage density may exceed Exabit per centimeter squared. A key problem that requires further investigation is related to the minimum Hamming distance between an arbitrary target bit sequence and the closest sequence realizable within the CRF framework under fixed hardware constraints.

</details>

### [108] [Stabilizing Role of Uninformed Participants in Collective Decision Making](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11259)
*Leonardo Colombo,Marıa Emma Eyrea Irazu,Laura P. Schaposnik,James Unwin*

Main category: nlin.AO

TL;DR: 本文利用耗散哈密顿量（dissipative Hamiltonian）构建了一个二阶网络集体决策模型，发现低冲突时存在唯一指数稳定的折中态（compromise state），高冲突时折中态通过鞍-结分岔（saddle-node fold）终止，而模块化极化态（modular polarized states）在局部独立的分支上持续存在。无方向耗散不改变静态结构阈值，但延迟逃离鞍-结幽灵（saddle-node ghost）并推后极化现象的观测起点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对缺乏严格等级结构的群体中集体决策通常通过折中（compromise）实现这一观察，现有基于连通性（connectivity）的机制尚不能完整解释无信息参与者如何影响集体行为的稳定性。作者旨在从耗散（dissipation）角度揭示一个互补机制。

Method: 采用耗散哈密顿量公式建立二阶网络模型（second-order network model），其中有信息个体（informed agents）引入偏好方向，无信息个体（uninformed participants）仅贡献无方向耗散（direction-free dissipation）。通过结构化模块网络（structured modular network）进行稳定性与分岔分析。

Result: 低冲突下模型存在局部唯一且指数稳定的折中态。随冲突增加，折中态通过鞍-结分岔而非光滑的平均场对称性破缺相变（mean-field symmetry-breaking transition）终止。模块化极化态在局部独立于折中态的分支上持续存在。无方向耗散不改变静态结构阈值，但延迟逃离鞍-结幽灵并推后极化现象的可观测起点。

Conclusion: 该工作识别出一种耗散介导（dissipation-mediated）的机制，该机制与基于连通性的解释互补，阐明了无信息参与者如何在生物与工程群体（swarms）中稳定集体行为。

Abstract: For groups without strict hierarchy, collective decisions often emerge through compromise. We develop a second-order network model of collective decision-making using a dissipative Hamiltonian formulation, in which informed agents introduce preferred directions while uninformed participants contribute only direction-free dissipation. We show that under low conflict, the model admits a locally unique, exponentially stable compromise state. Using a structured modular network we further show that as conflict increases the local compromise branch terminates through a saddle-node fold rather than through a smooth mean-field symmetry-breaking transition. Modular polarized states persist on branches that are locally separated from the compromise branch. Direction-free dissipation does not shift the static structural threshold, but it delays escape from the saddle-node ghost and pushes the observable onset of polarization to larger conflicts. Our work identifies a dissipation-mediated mechanism, complementary to connectivity-based accounts, through which uninformed participants stabilize collective behavior in biological and engineered swarms.

### [109] [SPADE: Split-and-Delay Embeddings for Autoregressive High-Granularity Calorimeter Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11304)
*Joschka Birk,Frank Gaede,Anna Hallin,Gregor Kasieczka,Martina Mozzanica,Henning Rose*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文提出 SPADE（SPlit And Delay Embeddings）自回归Transformer架构，通过将多特征（multi-feature）令牌的各个特征独立嵌入并引入延迟流（delayed stream），使标准自注意力（self-attention）机制能够学习令牌内的特征相关性。在ILD探测器点云量能器簇射生成任务中，SPADE性能与当前最优的AllShowers模型相当，并显著超越基于VQ-VAE的前代模型OmniJet-α_C。该方法可推广至任意多特征令牌生成任务，支持对高维数据采用类大语言模型（LLM-style）的预训练流程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Transformer模型在处理具有多特征（multi-feature）令牌（token）的序列数据时，通常将同一令牌内的多个特征联合嵌入（joint embedding），这会限制模型对令牌内部特征间相关性（intra-token correlation）的学习能力。本文旨在设计一种新的嵌入机制，使标准自注意力机制能够有效捕获这种内部结构。

Method: SPADE 将每个令牌的各个特征独立嵌入为不同的特征流（feature stream），并对每个后续的特征流相对于前一流施加固定的时间延迟（delay），从而将令牌内特征间的空间相关性转化为序列方向上的时间依赖性。经过这种“分割（split）与延迟（delay）”处理后，标准自注意力机制即可沿序列维度学习令牌内与跨令牌的关联。架构基于自回归（autoregressive）Transformer。

Result: 在高度粒化（highly granular）ILD探测器的点云（point-cloud）量能器簇射生成任务中，SPADE在光子簇射（photon shower）生成上的性能与当前最优的AllShowers模型持平，并明显优于基于VQ-VAE的前代模型OmniJet-α_C。

Conclusion: SPADE的分割与延迟嵌入机制是一种通用方法，适用于任何具有多特征令牌的生成任务，使得对高维数据可采用类似大语言模型（LLM-style）的预训练工作流（pretraining workflow）。

Abstract: We introduce SPADE (SPlit And Delay Embeddings), an autoregressive transformer for sequences whose tokens carry multiple features. Rather than embedding these features jointly, SPADE embeds them independently. Delaying each feature stream relative to the previous one allows intra-token correlations to be learned by the standard self-attention mechanism. Applied to point-cloud calorimeter shower generation in the highly granular ILD detector, SPADE is competitive with the state of the art AllShowers model on photon showers, and substantially outperforms its VQ-VAE-based predecessor OmniJet-$α_C$. The mechanism is applicable to any generative task with multi-feature tokens, enabling LLM-style pretraining workflows for higher-dimensional data.

</details>

### [110] [Curvature-Induced Force Fields in Hyperelasticity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11772)
*Victor Dods*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文通过在二维旋转曲面（surface of revolution）上对超弹性（hyperelastic）扁平体的静力平衡进行数值模拟，展示了一种由于曲率不均匀而产生的“悬浮”（levitation）现象：弹性体在重力势和变形恢复力的共同作用下，可在曲面曲率梯度中达到稳定平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受在黎曼流形（Riemannian manifold）中创建第一人称计算机视觉的启发，由于一般黎曼流形缺乏非平凡等距群（isometry group），刚体力学（rigid-body mechanics）不可用，因此作者转向研究可变形体力学（deformable-body mechanics），并在超弹性框架下提出数值求解方案。

Method: 将平坦超弹性体B嵌入到二维旋转曲面S的区域Ω中，其中S的高斯曲率（Gaussian curvature）K(r)随r增大而绝对值递减（如漏斗面或抛物面）。通过引入重力势U(r)=z(r)，使弹性体受到朝向r=0的引力，并与变形恢复力达到平衡，从而将问题表述为变分（variational）形式，并用数值方法求解静态解。

Result: 当弹性体具有足够刚度并保持在区域Ω内时，存在一个平衡构型，其中变形响应力与重力完全抵消。这种平衡状态在曲面内呈现一种“悬浮”现象。

Conclusion: 本文详细给出了该问题的数值实现，并对数值解及其各种后果进行了讨论，表明超弹性体在弯曲空间中可通过曲率梯度实现无接触支撑的稳定平衡。

Abstract: Originally motivated by creating first-person computer visualizations within Riemannian manifolds -- the author was led to study deformable-body mechanics, as rigid-body mechanics is not available in a generic Riemannian manifold due to its lack of nontrivial isometry group. Hyperelasticity is a particularly nice sub-category of continuum mechanics in which a deformable, elastic body's behavior is determined by a stored energy density function. This allows problems to be posed variationally, and powerful tools brought to bear on studying and solving them.
  This article presents numerical simulations of static solutions to a particular class of problems in hyperelastic mechanics in 2-dimensional Riemannian manifolds in which a flat hyperelastic body $B$ is embedded into a region $Ω$ in a nowhere-flat surface $S$ of revolution $z=z\left(r\right)$ such that $\left|K\left(r\right)\right|$ decreases as $r\to\infty$, where $K$ denotes the Gaussian curvature of $S$. For example, the funnel $z=-r^{-1}$ or the paraboloid $z=\frac{1}{2}r^{2}$. Because $B$ is flat, the body can't achieve a zero-stored-energy configuration, and restorative forces arise in the body to move it toward a region of lower stored energy -- meaning, toward a flatter configuration.
  With the addition of a gravitational potential $U\left(r\right)=z\left(r\right)$ on $S$, forces act on the body to pull it toward $r=0$. If the body has sufficient stiffness and remains within the region $Ω$, then the body has an equilibrium configuration in which the body's deformation-response forces perfectly cancel the gravitational forces. Such a configuration represents a kind of "levitation" phenomenon within this surface.
  The numerical implementation of this problem will be detailed and the resulting numerical solutions and various consequences discussed.

</details>

### [111] [Nonminimal couplings and preheating effects in $R^2$-Higgs inflation after ACT and SPT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11929)
*Haneesh Gonuguntla,Tanmoy Modak,Arnab Samanta*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文研究非最小希格斯耦合（nonminimal Higgs couplings）在 R²-希格斯暴涨模型（R²-Higgs inflation model）中的效应，发现维度-6 算符 $|Φ|² R²$ 和 $|Φ|⁴ R$ 可解释 ACT 与 SPT 观测所偏好的增强标量谱指数 $n_s$，且同一参数空间可通过产生戈德斯通模式（Goldstone modes）诱发快速预加热（preheating），有助于匹配暴涨尺度和宇宙微波背景（CMB）参考尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于近期 ACT 和 SPT 观测结果，研究维度四和维度六非最小希格斯耦合对 R²-希格斯暴涨模型的影响，以解释观测所偏好的增强标量谱指数 $n_s$。

Method: 采用双重协变形式论（doubly covariant formalism）分析维度-6 算符 $|Φ|² R²$ 和 $|Φ|⁴ R$ 在暴涨和预加热过程中的作用。

Result: 维度-6 算符能够容纳联合 CMB+BAO（重子声学振荡）分析所偏好的增强标量谱指数 $n_s$；同一参数空间还可通过戈德斯通模式的产生诱导快速预加热。

Conclusion: 若通过该预加热机制实现高效热化（thermalization），则可能有助于使暴涨尺度与 CMB 参考尺度相匹配。

Abstract: We study the effects of dimension-four and dimension-six nonminimal Higgs couplings to the Ricci scalar $R$ in the $R^2$-Higgs inflation model in light of the recent ACT and SPT observations. We show that the dimension-six operators $|Φ|^2 R^2$ and $|Φ|^4 R$ can accommodate the enhanced scalar spectral index $n_s$ preferred by the combined CMB+BAO analyses. Using a doubly covariant formalism, we find that the same region of parameter space that explains the observed value of $n_s$ can also induce rapid preheating through the production of the Goldstone modes. If thermalization proceeds efficiently through this preheating mechanism, it may help match the inflationary scale with the CMB reference scale.

### [112] [Phase Transitions in Attention: A Bayesian Theory of Copy Head Emergence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12058)
*Itay Lavie,Kirsten Fischer,Andrey Lekov,Frederic Van Maele,Zohar Ringel,Moritz Helias*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种关于Transformer中注意力机制特征学习的贝叶斯理论，通过对单层softmax注意力网络在复制任务上的分析，揭示了注意力子电路从无序到有序的相变（phase transition）过程，并对比了softmax注意力与线性注意力在相变类型上的本质差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 注意力（attention）是Transformer上下文学习（in-context learning）的核心机制，经验观察发现注意力模式在训练过程中会突然涌现（abrupt emergence）。本文旨在从第一性原理出发，从理论上解释这一涌现现象背后的学习动力学。

Method: 建立了一个特征学习的贝叶斯理论（Bayesian theory），并聚焦于单层softmax注意力网络在复制任务（copy task）上的学习过程。推导了注意力矩阵的闭式后验（closed-form posterior），并将其约化到低维序参量空间（low-dimensional order parameter space）。通过贝叶斯采样（Bayesian sampling）和Adam优化器标准训练两种方式验证理论预测。

Result: 揭示了训练数据量上的相变（phase transition）：softmax注意力展现出**一级相变（first-order phase transition）**，即注意力结构突然涌现；而线性注意力（linear attention）则先经历**二级相变（second-order phase transition）**，随后通过平滑连续的交叉（crossover）演化为结构化注意力模式。

Conclusion: 该工作为Transformer训练中复制子电路（copy subcircuit）的突然涌现提供了第一性原理的理论解释，这一现象与大型语言模型（large language models）训练中观察到的涌现行为相似。

Abstract: Attention is the key mechanism underlying in-context learning in transformers, and attention patterns have been observed empirically to emerge abruptly during training. We present a Bayesian theory of feature learning in attention; we then focus on how the copy subcircuit in the first layer of an induction head is learned by analyzing a single-layer softmax attention network trained on a copy task. We derive a closed-form posterior over the attention matrix and reduce it to a low-dimensional order parameter space. This reduction reveals a phase transition in the amount of training data, which we verify using both Bayesian sampling and standard training with Adam. We contrast our results with linear attention and find that softmax attention exhibits a \emph{first-order phase transition} while in linear attention an initial \emph{second-order phase transition} is followed by a smooth, continuous evolution toward the structured attention pattern (\emph{crossover}). Our work provides a first-principles theoretical account of the abrupt emergence of the copy subcircuit, reminiscent of the one observed in training large language models.

</details>

### [113] [Wavelet-Based Extraction of Transient Noise in Gravitational-Wave Interferometers using a Saliency-Guided Learning Architecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11595)
*Christopher Allene,Dhruv Kumar,Yusuke Sakai,Marco Meyer-Conde,Hirotaka Takahashi*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于小波（wavelet）和显著性引导（saliency-guided）的监督框架，用于从引力波干涉仪应变数据中提取瞬态噪声（glitches），通过离散小波变换（Discrete Wavelet Transform）的自适应系数掩码实现精确重建，并在多个代表性噪声族（如Whistle、Scattered-Light）上验证了有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波干涉仪中的非高斯瞬态噪声（glitches）会干扰天体物理信号的检测、导致参数估计偏差并影响探测器表征。现有机器学习方法仅能对glitch形态进行分类，缺乏从数据中完整分割和提取这些干扰的机制。

Method: 首先利用均匀流形近似与投影（Uniform Manifold Approximation and Projection, UMAP）进行预标记并诊断学习表征；然后基于连续小波变换（Continuous Wavelet Transform, CWT）频谱图的传统学习模型通过显著性图（saliency maps）识别时频区域；最后将这些显著性模式通过离散小波变换（Discrete Wavelet Transform, DWT）转移到可逆的多分辨率表示中，利用自适应系数掩码实现glitch-only和glitch-suppressed波形的精确重建。

Result: 该方法在多个代表性glitch族（包括'Whistle'和'Scattered-Light'瞬态噪声）上实现了有效提取，并在低信噪比事件与部分重叠结构等挑战性场景中表现出鲁棒性，优于经典阈值法或带限滤波方法。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一种可解释且计算高效的瞬态噪声提取方案，为扩展到更大规模glitch目录及未来观测运行奠定了基础。

Abstract: Gravitational-wave interferometers exhibit a wide variety of short-duration non-Gaussian transients, commonly referred to as glitches, that complicate the detection of astrophysical signals, bias parameter estimation, and detector characterisation. Existing machine-learning approaches classify glitch morphologies but do not provide a complete mechanism to segment and extract these disturbances from the strain data. We introduce a wavelet-based, saliency-guided framework for the supervised extraction of transient noise. Candidates are first pre-tagged using Uniform Manifold Approximation and Projection, which is also used as a diagnostic of the learned representations. A traditional learning model operating on Continuous Wavelet Transform spectrograms then identifies relevant time-frequency regions through saliency maps. These saliency patterns are transferred to an invertible multiresolution representation via the Discrete Wavelet Transform, where adaptive coefficient masking enables exact reconstruction of both glitch-only and glitch-suppressed waveforms. We demonstrate effective extraction across several representative glitch families, including 'Whistle' and 'Scattered-Light' transients, and show robustness in challenging regimes such as low signal-to-noise events and partially overlapping structures, where classical thresholding or band-limited filtering methods typically fail or introduce leakage. The proposed framework offers an interpretable and computationally efficient approach to transient-noise extraction, establishing a foundation for scalable applications to larger glitch catalogs and future observing runs.

</details>

### [114] [Physically Constrained Ensemble Gaussian Process Modelling for Expensive Quantum Systems with Heteroskedastic Noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11240)
*Arpan Biswas,Surtirtha Paul,Joseph Agada,Matthias Thamm,Adrian Del Maestro*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种物理约束集成高斯过程（pc-EGP）框架，用于在物理一致性约束下高效建模含异方差噪声（heteroskedastic noise）的复杂量子多体系统。该方法将物理约束作为加权惩罚项融入高斯过程（Gaussian Process, GP）的数据驱动损失函数，并通过数值求积法（numerical quadrature method）训练GP集成模型。在Bose-Hubbard模型的DMRG模拟和纳米孔硅酸盐中量子液体的QMC模拟两个案例中，pc-EGP相比传统GP在精度和物理合理性之间取得了更优的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确建模量子多体系统（quantum many-body systems）通常依赖密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）或量子蒙特卡洛（QMC）等计算昂贵的模拟方法，这些方法在参数空间的大规模探索中受到严重的时间和资源限制。此外，这些昂贵模拟在未知参数空间上存在可变误差，需要被量化和传播。因此，亟需一种能够在稀疏采样数据上准确估计函数空间、处理异方差噪声并保持物理相关性的预测建模方法。

Method: 提出物理约束集成高斯过程（pc-EGP）框架。首先，将物理约束作为用户可控的加权惩罚项添加到高斯过程（GP）代理模型的数据驱动损失函数中。其次，通过数值求积法训练一组GP模型，将不同节点上的多个GP以求积加权平均方式集成，从而处理可变噪声的模拟数据。

Result: 在第一个案例中，利用Bose-Hubbard模型的DMRG模拟预测超流-莫特绝缘体转变的关键相互作用参数Uc。在第二个案例中，对纳米孔硅酸盐内受限量子液体的QMC模拟进行建模，以优化实现一维超流体的化学环境。与传统GP相比，pc-EGP在精度和物理有意义预测之间实现了更优的平衡。

Conclusion: pc-EGP框架能够有效建模含异方差噪声的复杂量子系统，在物理一致性约束下实现比传统GP更准确的预测。该方法为在昂贵模拟数据稀缺且存在噪声的情况下进行物理信息驱动的参数空间探索提供了一种可行的建模途径。

Abstract: Accurate modeling of quantum many-body systems often requires computationally expensive simulations such as Density Matrix Renormalization Group (DMRG) or Quantum Monte Carlo (QMC) calculations. These methods, while precise, impose significant time and resource constraints, limiting their use in exhaustive parameter exploration. Moreover, these expensive simulations can contain variable errors over the large unknown parameter space, which needs to be quantified and propagated. Thus, predictive modelling is required to estimate the functional space accurately over scarcely sampled data with heteroskedastic noise, while preserving the physical relevance of the estimation. Therefore, we present a Physically Constrained Ensemble Gaussian Process (pc-EGP) framework designed to efficiently model complex and noisy quantum systems under physical consistency constraints. The proposed method first enforces physical constraints as a user controlled weighted penalty to the data-driven loss function of the Gaussian Process (GP) surrogates. Then an ensemble of such GP models is trained with variable noisy simulations via numerical quadrature method where these multiple GP(s) at different nodes is integrated as a quadrature weighted average. We first demonstrate the framework on synthetically generated data before applying to quantum systems. In the first case study, we leverage DMRG simulations of the Bose-Hubbard Model to predict the critical interaction parameter Uc governing the superfluid-to-Mott-insulator transition. In the second case study, we demonstrate our method on QMC simulations, of a quantum liquid confined inside a nanoporous silicate with the goal of optimizing a chemical environment to realize a one-dimensional superfluid. Compared to conventional GP, pc-EGP achieves a better balance of accuracy and physically meaningful predictions.

</details>
