### [115] [Chiral anomaly and planar Hall conductance in pseudospin-$1$ Fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11364)
*Azaz Ahmad*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用半经典玻尔兹曼输运理论，系统研究了赝自旋-1 外尔半金属（pseudospin-1 Weyl semimetals）中的磁输运性质，重点分析了平面霍尔电导（PHC）在倾斜能带、动量相关散射及轨道磁矩修正下的行为，揭示了正负符号反转、各向异性角依赖及非单调倾斜效应等特征，为多折费米子（multifold fermions）的输运实验提供了可检验的预言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 外尔半金属（Weyl semimetal）中正纵向磁电导（LMC）与平面霍尔电导（PHC）是手征反常（chiral anomaly）的标志性输运特征。近期理论将外尔费米子推广至具有更高赝自旋准粒子激发的多折费米子系统（multifold fermionic systems），因而有必要研究其磁输运特性。

Method: 采用半经典玻尔兹曼输运理论（semiclassical Boltzmann transport theory）和弛豫时间近似（relaxation-time approximation），考虑动量相关散射（momentum-dependent scattering）、轨道磁矩修正（orbital magnetic moment corrections）以及电荷守恒约束（charge-conservation constraints）。通过引入准粒子色散的倾斜（tilt）或电场与磁场之间的有限夹角（misalignment）打破方位对称性，以获得有限的 PHC。

Result: 在无倾斜情况下，PHC 为正值且随磁场强度呈二次方标度；增大散射强度可导致 PHC 从正值反转为负值；PHC 呈现 sin2γ 的角依赖特征。倾斜沿 x 和 z 方向分别将角依赖改变为 sinγ 和 cosγ，产生强烈的平面霍尔信号各向异性；PHC 对倾斜幅度呈现非单调依赖，揭示了倾斜诱导的对称性破缺与手征反常驱动输运之间的竞争。

Conclusion: 本文结果为多折费米子提供了实验可及的输运特征，并构建了用于解释空间群 199、214 及 220 候选材料中磁输运测量的理论框架。

Abstract: Positive longitudinal magnetoconductance (LMC) and planar Hall conductance (PHC) are hallmark transport signatures of the chiral anomaly in Weyl semimetals. Recent theoretical developments have extended Weyl fermions to multifold Fermionic systems with higher-pseudospin quasiparticle excitations, motivating the study of their magnetotransport properties. Here, we employ semiclassical Boltzmann transport theory within the relaxation-time approximation to investigate magnetotransport in pseudospin-1 Weyl semimetals, incorporating momentum-dependent scattering, orbital magnetic moment corrections, and charge-conservation constraints. To obtain a finite PHC, we break azimuthal symmetry through either a generic tilt of the quasiparticle dispersion or a finite misalignment between the electric and magnetic fields. In the untilted case, the PHC is positive and scales quadratically with magnetic field strength. Increasing the scattering strength induces a sign reversal of the PHC, producing a transition from positive to negative values. The PHC further exhibits the characteristic angular dependence $\sin 2γ$, where $γ$ is the angle between the magnetic field and the $x$-axis. Tilt qualitatively alters this behavior: tilt along the $x$- and $z$-directions changes the angular response to $\sinγ$ and $\cosγ$, respectively, generating strong anisotropy in the planar Hall signal. Moreover, the PHC shows a nonmonotonic dependence on tilt magnitude, revealing the interplay between tilt-induced symmetry breaking and chiral-anomaly-driven transport. Our results provide experimentally accessible signatures of multifold fermions and a framework for interpreting magnetotransport measurements in candidate materials of space groups 199, 214, and 220.

</details>


### [116] [Extrinsic quantum geometry in the quadrupolar bulk photovoltaic effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11434)
*Steven Gassner,Swati Chaudhary,Martin Claassen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了中心对称晶体中由光有限动量引起的光子拖曳效应，发现了一项此前被忽略的贡献——源于电四极修正的光-物质耦合，并将其识别为一个多能带度规张量。研究表明，在动量空间中有三个及以上能带强混合的系统（如扭曲MoTe₂双层），会因这种四极效应产生异常大的光子拖曳信号。该工作为能带几何组织原理与非线性光学中的电磁多极修正之间建立了概念桥梁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管在偶极近似下体光伏效应（bulk photovoltaic effect）仅限于反演对称破缺的体系，但光子的有限动量（finite momentum of light）即使在中心对称晶体中也能引发类似效应，即光子拖曳（photon drag）。此前对该效应的处理尚不完整，尤其是在电四极修正对光-物质耦合的贡献方面存在未被充分认识的部分。

Method: 作者在光学波矢（optical wavevector）主导阶下重新表述了光子拖曳效应，指出一个此前被忽略的贡献来源于电四极修正（electric quadrupole correction）对光-物质耦合的修正。从能带几何（band geometry）的语言出发，将此带间四极矩（interband quadrupole）识别为一个多能带度规张量（multiband metric tensor），用于量化两个共振驱动态在它们所张子空间之外的变化。

Result: 在动量空间中三个及以上能带发生强混合的系统，例如扭曲MoTe₂双层（twisted MoTe₂ bilayers），会由于上述四极效应而展现出异常大的光子拖曳效应。

Conclusion: 该工作为能带几何组织原理（band-geometric organizing principles）与非线性光学（nonlinear optics）中的电磁多极修正（electromagnetic multipole corrections）之间建立了概念桥梁，揭示了多能带几何量在光电效应中的新角色。

Abstract: The bulk photovoltaic effect has become a valuable probe of the quantum geometry of Bloch bands. While it is restricted to inversion-broken systems within the dipole approximation, the finite momentum of light is appreciated to give rise to this effect even in centrosymmetric crystals, an effect referred to as "photon drag." In this work, we recast the photon drag effect at leading order in the optical wavevector, highlighting a previously neglected contribution arising intuitively from the electric quadrupole correction to light-matter coupling. In the language of band geometry, we identify this interband quadrupole as a multiband metric tensor that quantifies the variation of two resonantly driven states extrinsic to the subspace they span. We predict that systems in which three or more bands strongly admix in momentum space, such as twisted MoTe$_2$ bilayers, will have anomalously large photon drag due to this quadrupolar effect. Our work provides a conceptual bridge between band-geometric organizing principles and electromagnetic multipole corrections in nonlinear optics.

</details>


### [117] [Polarization-Resolved Photon Statistics of Cavity Quantum Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11550)
*Benjamin Kass,Spenser Talkington,Martin Claassen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出利用腔透射光子的偏振分辨二阶关联函数 $g^{(2)}$ 作为诊断光-物质耦合效应的探针，将其与物质关联函数（如拉曼结构因子）建立联系，并在 Kitaev-Heisenberg 自旋模型中展示了该方法如何编码磁点群对称性并表征相变边界行为，同时预言测量正交偏振光子对可孤立高阶光-物质散射过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光学腔通过形成混合光-物质态为调控材料性质提供了途径，但明确探测光-物质耦合效应仍然困难；因此需要一种可直接测量的诊断手段来解析耦合对材料性质的影响。

Method: 将腔透射光子的偏振分辨统计量 $g^{(2)}$ 与物质关联函数（如拉曼结构因子（Raman structure factor））建立关联，从而将光子聚束（bunching）与反聚束（antibunching）行为映射至材料性质。

Result: 在 Kitaev-Heisenberg 自旋模型从条状（stripy）相到反铁磁（antiferromagnetic）相的转变中，偏振依赖的聚束与反聚束模式编码了各相的磁点群对称性（magnetic point-group symmetry），并表征了相边界处的行为。

Conclusion: 测量与输入场正交偏振的输出光子对的 $g^{(2)}$ 可用于孤立高阶光-物质散射过程，从而探测更高阶的物质关联函数，为材料性质研究提供新的探针。

Abstract: By forming hybrid light-matter states, optical cavities offer a route for engineering material properties, however, unambiguously probing the effects of light-matter coupling remains difficult. Here, we show that the polarization-resolved statistics of photons transmitted through a cavity, measurable via $g^{(2)}$, provide one such diagnostic. By relating $g^{(2)}$ to matter correlation functions such as the Raman structure factor, we link photon bunching and antibunching to material properties. By applying this method to the stripy-to-antiferromagnetic transition in the Kitaev-Heisenberg spin model, we find that polarization-dependent patterns of bunching and antibunching encode the magnetic point-group symmetries of each phase and characterize the behavior at the phase boundary. Finally, we predict measuring $g^{(2)}$ for output photon pairs polarized orthogonal to the input field will isolate higher-order light-matter scattering processes that probe higher-order material correlations.

</details>


### [118] [Consistent Evaluation of Operators Involving the Position Operator in the Bloch Representation: Application to the Orbital Moment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11679)
*Daehyeon An,Junmo Jeon,Se Kwon Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文针对凝聚态物理中位置算符（position operator）在布洛赫表示（Bloch representation）下的评价不一致问题，提出三条评价规则和一种称为“规范过滤”（gauge filtration）的方案，以系统去除规范依赖贡献，确保算符评价结果对应可观测物理现象，并统一了波包自旋（self-rotation of wave packet）与万尼尔函数局域环流（local circulation of Wannier function）之间的矛盾。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 位置算符在速度、轨道矩（orbital moment）和电极化（electric polarization）等凝聚态可观测量中处于核心地位，但固态物理中对其在布洛赫表示下的算符评价尚未达成共识，典型矛盾体现为万尼尔函数的局域环流与波包自旋在算符层级上的不一致。

Method: 提出三条用于布洛赫表示中涉及位置算符的算符评价规则：独立于单胞（unit cell）选择、保持算符乘积的厄米共轭性（Hermitian conjugacy）、恢复正确的带内速度（intraband velocity）。引入规范过滤方案，系统性地从含位置算符的算符中去除规范依赖部分。

Result: 该框架确保了从算符评价所得的量对应可观测物理现象，并成功调和了波包自旋与万尼尔函数局域环流之间的矛盾。

Conclusion: 所提出的三条规则与规范过滤方案有望建立一个评价含位置算符的算符的一致框架（consistent framework），为凝聚态物理中相关可观测量的计算提供统一基础。

Abstract: The position operator plays a central role in condensed-matter observables such as velocity, orbital moment, and electric polarization. In solid-state physics, the evaluation of operators incorporating the position operator has not reached a consensus, as observed in the operator-level discrepancy between the local circulation of Wannier functions and the self-rotation of wave packets. Here, to achieve a consistent evaluation of such operators, we propose three rules for evaluating operators involving the position operator in the Bloch representation. The rules are devised to satisfy physical conditions: independence from the choice of unit cell, preservation of Hermitian conjugacy for the product of operators, and recovery of the correct intraband velocity. We further address the gauge dependence of the position operator and introduce a scheme termed gauge filtration, which systematically removes gauge-dependent contributions from the operators containing the position operator. This methodology ensures that the quantities obtained from the operator evaluation correspond to observable physical phenomena. By applying our framework, we reconcile the results concerning the self-rotation of the wave packet and the local circulation of the Wannier function. We expect our proposal to establish a consistent framework for evaluating operators involving the position operator.

</details>


### [119] [DSpinGNN: A Physics-Informed Equivariant Graph Neural Network for Dynamic Magnetic Exchange Prediction in Strain-Deformed Monolayer CrI$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11685)
*Isam A. Balghari,M. Faryad,M. Sabieh Anwar*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出DSpinGNN，一种结合E(3)-等变图神经网络与物理信息Δ-MLP的分叉式机器学习架构，能够在动态变形的晶格上同时解析结构力学和磁性相互作用，实现了对单层CrI₃中交换耦合的介观尺度（mesoscale）映射，并揭示了应变波传播引发的空间异质交换耦合纹理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在动态变形的晶体晶格上解析瞬时、位置依赖的各向同性磁交换耦合（isotropic magnetic exchange coupling）需要一种能够同时处理结构力和磁相互作用的计算方法，而第一性原理方法（first-principles methods）无法触及所需的长度尺度。

Method: DSpinGNN采用分叉式机器学习架构：一个E(3)-等变图神经网络（E(3)-equivariant graph neural network, E-GNN）用于经典朗之万结构动力学（Langevin structural dynamics），和一个物理信息Δ-MLP用于将瞬时局部Cr-I-Cr键几何映射为各向同性交换耦合，其中Goodenough-Kanamori超交换关系作为分析性归纳偏置（analytical inductive bias）嵌入。

Result: 在345个DFT+U构型上训练并在61个严格保留构型上评估，DSpinGNN同时实现了能量MAE为1.1 meV/原子、力MAE为6.5 meV/Å、交换耦合MAE为0.18 meV（R²=0.91）。在3200原子超胞中以400倍规模部署后，模型将局部交换响应映射到传播的双轴应变波（biaxial strain wave）上；波在周期边界反射产生瞬态相长干涉（constructive interference）区域，使局部压缩应变超过DFT建立的铁磁-反铁磁阈值，产生空间异质交换耦合纹理。定量分析得到畴壁宽度ξ=1.7±0.3 nm，相长干涉振荡周期τ=0.27 ps。

Conclusion: DSpinGNN提供了可复现、可迁移的介观交换映射框架（mesoscale exchange mapping framework），适用于应变驱动的二维磁性材料，生成的介观可观测量是直接DFT无法获取的、可作为低温磁力显微镜（cryogenic magnetic force microscopy）可检验的预测。

Abstract: Resolving the instantaneous, position-dependent isotropic magnetic exchange coupling $J_{ij}$ across a dynamically deforming crystal lattice requires a computational approach that simultaneously handles structural forces and magnetic interactions at length scales inaccessible to first-principles methods. Here we introduce DSpinGNN, a bifurcated machine-learning architecture comprising an $E(3)$-equivariant graph neural network (E-GNN) for classical Langevin structural dynamics and a physics-informed $Δ$-MLP that maps instantaneous local Cr-I-Cr bond geometry to isotropic exchange couplings, with the Goodenough-Kanamori superexchange relationship embedded as an analytical inductive bias. Trained on 345 DFT+U configurations of monolayer CrI$_3$ and evaluated on a strictly withheld 61-configuration test set, DSpinGNN simultaneously achieves an energy MAE of $1.1$ meV/atom, a force MAE of $6.5$ meV/Å, and an exchange coupling MAE of $0.18$ meV ($R^2 = 0.91$). Deployed at 400$\times$ scale in a 3,200-atom supercell under a collinear Ising-constrained adiabatic approximation at $5$ K, the model maps the local exchange response to a propagating biaxial strain wave. Wave reflection at periodic boundaries generates transient constructive interference regions where local compressive strain exceeds the DFT-established FM-to-AFM threshold, producing spatially heterogeneous exchange coupling textures that damp as the wave dissipates. Quantitative analysis yields a domain wall width of $ξ= 1.7 \pm 0.3$~nm and a constructive-interference oscillation period of $τ= 0.27$~ps -- mesoscopic observables inaccessible to direct DFT and constituting testable predictions for cryogenic magnetic force microscopy. DSpinGNN provides a reproducible, transferable framework for mesoscale exchange mapping in strain-driven 2D magnetic materials.

</details>


### [120] [Spin-Orbit Torque and Magnetization Switching in 2D Ferromagnetic Devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11752)
*Bao-Huei Huang,Hong Guo,Yu-Hui Tang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 基于第一性原理量子输运计算，本文研究了范德华异质双层Cr₃Te₄/PtTe₂中的非平衡自旋扭矩效应，揭示局域自旋感应（Rashba-Edelstein效应）主要产生类场扭矩，主导具有强面内磁各向异性的体系中的磁化翻转电流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电流诱导的自旋轨道扭矩（spin-orbit torque）是操纵铁磁/非磁（ferromagnet/nonmagnet, FM/NM）存储单元磁化翻转的重要技术，但其微观机制在范德华异质结中尚需深入理解。

Method: 采用第一性原理量子输运计算（first-principles quantum transport calculations），研究三角晶格Cr₃Te₄/PtTe₂范德华异质双层中的非平衡自旋扭矩效应，同时确定由铁磁层中Rashba-Edelstein效应产生的局域自旋感应，以及从非磁层流向铁磁层的自旋电流注入。

Result: 局域自旋感应显著产生类场扭矩（fieldlike torque），该扭矩主导具有强面内磁各向异性（in-plane magnetic anisotropy, IMA）体系中的翻转电流。在垂直磁各向异性（perpendicular magnetic anisotropy, PMA）体系中，非磁层的自旋霍尔效应（spin Hall effect）起关键作用；在IMA体系中，铁磁层的Rashba效应则更为重要。

Conclusion: 优化非磁层的自旋霍尔效应对基于垂直磁各向异性的磁化翻转至关重要，而最大化铁磁层的Rashba效应用于面内磁各向异性（IMA）的翻转。

Abstract: Current-induced spin-orbit torque has emerged as a powerful technique for manipulating magnetization switching of ferromagnet/nonmagnet (FM/NM) based memory cell. By investigating nonequilibrium spin torque effect in a van der Waals heterobilayer, trigonal $\text{Cr}_{3}\text{Te}_{4}/\text{PtTe}_{2}$, the first-principles quantum transport calculations are applied to determine both local spin induction, resulting from Rashba-Edelstein effect in the FM layer, and spin current injection, flowing from the NM to the FM layer. Our work reveals that local spin induction significantly generates the fieldlike torque, which primarily governs the switching current in systems with strong in-plane magnetic anisotropy. Our work emphasizes the importance of optimizing spin Hall effect in the NM layer for perpendicular magnetic anisotropy (PMA)-based magnetization switching and maximizing the Rashba effect in the FM layer for in-plane magnetic anisotropy (IMA)-based switching.

</details>


### [121] [Berry-phase-based Topological Charge in Quasicrystals and their Observable Features in Photonic System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11777)
*Ziyi Chen,Jinyu Zou,Jinhua Gao,Gang xu*

TL;DR: 本文基于贝里相位（Berry phase）的拓扑荷（topological charge）概念，通过群表示论（group representation theory）和低能有效哈密顿量（low-energy effective Hamiltonian），建立了二维准晶（quasicrystal）中拓扑荷的通用理论框架。以C8v对称性准晶为例，发现了传统周期系统中无法实现的高阶拓扑荷C=4，并在光子准晶中揭示了通过电磁场分布模式绕数来实验探测拓扑荷的方法，从而桥接了周期性与准周期性拓扑能带理论。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于贝里相位（Berry phase）的拓扑荷（topological charge）是拓扑物理的核心，但此类拓扑荷在准晶（quasicrystal）中尚未被探索，阻碍了对准周期系统中拓扑态的系统性理解。

Method: 利用群表示论（group representation theory）推导所有允许的拓扑荷，并结合对应的低能有效哈密顿量（low-energy effective Hamiltonian），建立适用于二维准晶的拓扑荷通用框架；以C8v对称性准晶为例进行验证，并推广至光子准晶（photonic quasicrystal）。

Result: 在C8v对称性准晶中发现了传统周期系统中不可实现的高阶拓扑荷C=4；在光子准晶中，光子动量围绕拓扑荷的绕行会导致电磁场分布模式出现C倍的缠绕（winding），该特征可被直接实验观测。

Conclusion: 该工作为探索准周期物质中的拓扑荷奠定了理论基础，并从根本上桥接了周期性与准周期性拓扑能带理论（topological band theory）。

Abstract: Topological charges based on Berry phase play the fundamental role in the topological physics. However, such topological charges remain unexplored in quasicrystals, impeding the systematic understanding of topological states in such quasiperiodic systems. In this work, by deriving all the allowed topological charges according to group representation theory and the corresponding low-energy effective Hamiltonians, we establish a universal framework for Berry-phase-based topological charges in two-dimensional quasicrystals. Taking the $C_{8v}$ quasicrystal as an example, we demonstrate and characterize a higher topological charge of $C=4$, which is inaccessible in conventional periodic systems. Applying our framework to photonic quasicrystals, we uncover that the circling of photon momentum around the charge gives a $C$ times winding of the electromagnetic field distribution pattern. Such observable feature provides a direct experimental method to probe the topological charges. Our work paves the way for exploring topological charges in quasiperiodic matter, and fundamentally bridges periodic and quasiperiodic topological band theories.

### [122] [Ferroelectric Altermagnetic Chern Insulator in magnetic field: electrical control of the Chern number](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11862)
*Meysam Bagheri Tagani,Carmine Autieri*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从Bernevig-Hughes-Zhang模型出发，结合外磁场、自旋倾斜和铁电轨道杂化，在交变磁体中实现了电场可控的Chern绝缘体相，揭示了自旋倾斜响应与铁电性驱动Berry曲率重组从而改变拓扑相（C = ±1, ±2）的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnets）中量子反常霍尔效应难以实现，因为在非相对论极限下，Γ点处自旋向上与自旋向下态保持简并。本文旨在通过引入外磁场、自旋倾斜（spin canting）和铁电轨道杂化（ferroelectric orbital hybridization）来解除该简并，从而实现电场可控的Chern数（Chern number）。

Method: 以Bernevig-Hughes-Zhang（BHZ）模型为起点引入非平庸能带拓扑；构建一个最小化的二维d波交变磁模型（包含能带反转），在其中结合外磁场、自旋倾斜和铁电轨道杂化的联合效应。通过铁电极化（ferroelectric polarization）控制拓扑相和轨道角动量（orbital angular momentum），实现Berry曲率（Berry curvature）的重组。

Result: 外加磁场、自旋倾斜与铁电性共同解除了Γ点处的简并，实现了电场对Chern数的调控。铁电极化可控制拓扑相变，通过Berry曲率重组获得C = ±1和C = ±2的丰富相图，该重组与自旋倾斜响应及铁电性直接相关。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一条对称性一致的路径，在交变磁材料中实现电场可调的Chern绝缘体相（Chern insulator phase），为低功耗拓扑器件（topological devices）和轨道电子学器件（orbitronic devices）开辟了新的机遇。

Abstract: The quantum anomalous Hall effect in altermagnets is difficult to realize because spin-up and spin-down states remain degenerate at the $Γ$ point in the nonrelativistic limit. We start from the Bernevig-Hughes-Zhang model to incorporate nontrivial band topology. We demonstrate that the combined effects of an external magnetic field, spin canting, and ferroelectric orbital hybridization lift the degeneracy at the $Γ$ point, enabling electric-field control of the Chern number. A minimal two-dimensional d-wave altermagnetic model with band inversion then realizes a ferroelectrically tunable Chern insulator with spontaneous spin canting. The ferroelectric polarization controls the topological phase and the orbital angular momentum, enabling a rich phase diagram with C = $\pm 1$ and C = $\pm 2$ through a Berry-curvature reorganization linked to the spin canting response and ferroelectricity. Our results establish a symmetry-consistent route to electrically tunable Chern insulating phases in altermagnetic materials, opening opportunities for low-power topological and orbitronic devices.

### [123] [Intrinsic Nonreciprocity in Electron-Phonon Interaction Driven Thermoelectric Diodes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11904)
*Hao-Kun Ke,Lie-Run Tian,Jun-Feng Liu,Pei-Hao Fu,Jun Wang,H. Xu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了由电子-声子相互作用驱动的热电二极管，揭示了由声子发射与吸收概率不对称及结构反射不对称引起的固有非互易性（intrinsic nonreciprocity），并发现了两种新型输运现象：一种由引线（lead）与中心器件区的温差驱动的新型热电效应，以及负载电阻中电子背散射（electronic backscattering）的抑制导致欧姆加法法则（Ohm's addition law）失效；在适当条件下，电子-声子相互作用可产生更大的热电电流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索电子-声子相互作用（electron-phonon interaction）驱动的热电二极管中的非互易性（nonreciprocity）的内在机制，并揭示其导致的新型输运现象，为低功耗电子学和非互易热电装置开辟新路径。

Method: 通过分析电子-声子相互作用中声子发射与吸收概率的不对称性以及结构反射不对称性（structural reflection asymmetry），研究热电二极管的非互易输运行为。

Result: 发现固有非互易性导致两种新现象：1) 一种由引线与中心器件区之间的温差而非两引线间温差驱动的新型热电效应（thermoelectric effect）；2) 负载电阻中电子背散射被抑制，使电阻降低并导致欧姆加法法则失效。在适当条件下，电子-声子相互作用反而能产生比无相互作用时更大的热电电流。

Conclusion: 电子-声子相互作用驱动的固有非互易性为低功耗电子学（low-power electronics）和非互易热电装置（nonreciprocal thermoelectric devices）提供了除拓扑（topology）和超导电性（superconductivity）之外的新途径。

Abstract: We study an electron-phonon interaction driven thermoelectric diode. The nonreciprocity in this diode arises from the asymmetry between the probabilities of phonon emission and absorption in the electron-phonon interaction, as well as the structural reflection asymmetry. We reveal the intrinsic nature of this nonreciprocity, as the forward and backward electron transport remains asymmetric even when the applied temperature difference is not reversed. This intrinsic nonreciprocity gives rise to two novel transport phenomena. One is a novel thermoelectric effect which is driven by the temperature difference between the leads and the central device region, rather than the conventional temperature difference between the two leads. The second, and more significant, phenomenon is the suppression of electronic backscattering in the load resistor. This suppression decreases the resistance of the load resistor, which leads to the breakdown of Ohm's addition law. Under suitable conditions, the presence of electron-phonon interaction can yield a larger thermoelectric current compared to the case without it. This intrinsic nonreciprocity opens up a new pathway for low-power electronics besides topology and superconductivity, and for nonreciprocal thermoelectric devices.

### [124] [Robust Spin Logic Enabled by Generalized $\mathrm{SU}(2)$ Symmetry in $p$-Wave Magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11912)
*Hao-Kun Ke,Gong Zhao,Siqing Li,Ruixiang Chen,Chui-Zhen Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文展示了通过精确调控三维p波磁体（p-wave magnet）的内禀动量依赖交换场与栅极诱导Rashba自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling），建立了一种广义的SU(2)自旋旋转对称性（spin-rotation symmetry），从而产生对称保护的自旋螺旋（Persistent Spin Helix, PSH），实现了高可见度、抗无序和几何变化的Datta-Das振荡，为非磁化自旋电子学（spintronics）提供了新范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非传统磁体（unconventional magnets）兼具反铁磁体（antiferromagnets）的零杂散场和铁磁体（ferromagnets）的强自旋劈裂，但实现功能化的自旋逻辑器件面临保持长程自旋相干性（long-range spin coherence）的关键挑战，亟需克服动量退化散射和栅极诱导退相干的限制。

Method: 通过调控三维p波磁体的内禀动量依赖交换场与栅极诱导Rashba自旋-轨道耦合，建立广义SU(2)自旋旋转对称性，形成对称保护的自旋螺旋（PSH），并建模构建p波磁性自旋场效应晶体管（spin-FET），进行量子输运模拟（quantum transport simulation）。

Result: 实现了纯电学控制的高可见度Datta-Das电导振荡（Datta-Das conductance oscillations）；量子输运模拟证实该对称工程化输运机制对强非磁性安德森无序（Anderson disorder）和几何变化具有卓越抗性。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了非磁化自旋电子学（non-magnetized spintronics）的协同范式，证明主动整合自旋-轨道耦合与非传统磁性可产生抗无序的自旋逻辑器件。

Abstract: Unconventional magnets combine the vanishing stray fields of antiferromagnets with the strong spin-splitting of ferromagnets, offering a unique material platform for spintronics. However, a critical challenge in realizing functional spin-logic devices lies in preserving long-range spin coherence against momentum-degrading scattering and gate-induced dephasing. Here, we demonstrate that the intrinsic momentum-dependent exchange field of a three-dimensional $p$-wave magnet can be precisely tuned against gate-induced Rashba spin-orbit coupling to establish a \textit{generalized} $\mathrm{SU}(2)$ spin-rotation symmetry. This emergent conservation law generates a symmetry-protected Persistent Spin Helix (PSH), effectively integrating the high energy scales of 3D bulk magnetic exchange with the macroscopic coherence of symmetry protection. By modeling a synergistic $p$-wave magnetic spin field-effect transistor (spin-FET), we reveal high-visibility Datta-Das conductance oscillations controlled purely by electrical gating. Crucially, our quantum transport simulations confirm that this symmetry-engineered transport regime exhibits exceptional resilience against strong non-magnetic Anderson disorder and geometric variations. These results establish a synergistic paradigm for non-magnetized spintronics, demonstrating how the active integration of spin-orbit coupling and unconventional magnetism can yield disorder-resilient spintronic logic.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 所构建的反射式q-plate能够在宽波长范围内有效转换轨道角动量，且对超短激光脉冲不引起时间展宽（temporal broadening），在法向与掠入射条件下均表现出良好的工作性能。

Conclusion: 基于等离激元超表面的高反射率q-plate为产生携带轨道角动量的超短激光脉冲提供了一种有效方案，避免了传统透射元件的限制，具备宽波长适用性与反射模式下的灵活性。

Abstract: The orbital angular momentum of light is an intriguing property for developing light driven applications. It emerged as an independent degree of freedom by which to manipulate light and, consequently, the interaction of light with matter. Several methods exist for the generation of light carrying orbital angular momentum, mostly employing transmitting or reflecting optical components, which radially modulate the phase profile of the light. As one of such components, transmissive q-plates established themselves as standard elements due to their usability over a broad wavelength range. Here, we present our approach to build a highly reflective q-plate based on a plasmonic metasurface capable of converting orbital angular momentum from the nanostructure to ultrashort laser pulses without temporal broadening. We highlight its working principle over a wide range of wavelengths for reflection under normal and gracing incidence.

### [126] [Heisenberg-Langevin theory of an exciton mirror](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12053)
*Sergueï V. Andreev*

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个考虑延迟效应和长程电子-空穴交换的激子镜（exciton mirror）的海森堡-朗之万理论（Heisenberg-Langevin theory），详细分析了强横向磁场情形，揭示了光学双稳态（optical bistability）对调制不稳定性（modulational instability）的倾向性，以及泵浦二维激子气体在阈值上下分别表现为光参量发生器（optical parametric generator）和相位共轭镜（phase-conjugating mirror）的两种行为。

Method: 采用海森堡-朗之万理论（Heisenberg-Langevin theory）进行建模，将延迟效应与长程交换相互作用纳入激子镜的动力学描述，并针对强横向磁场情形进行解析分析。

Result: 光锥（light cone）内激子之间的排斥作用导致的光学双稳态（optical bistability），容易发生朝向非辐射表面极化激元模式（non-radiative surface polariton modes）的调制不稳定性（modulational instability）。在阈值之上，泵浦的二维激子气体充当产生孪生极化激元光束的光参量发生器（optical parametric generator）；在阈值之下，激子镜则表现出相位共轭（phase-conjugating）特性。

Conclusion: 激子镜在阈值上下分别呈现光参量发生与相位共轭两种截然不同的非线性光学功能，为二维激子体系在量子光学和非线性光学中的应用提供了新途径。

Abstract: We develop a Heisenberg-Langevin theory of an exciton mirror accounting for the retardation and the long-range electron-hole exchange. A particular case of a strong transverse magnetic field is analyzed in detail. The optical bistability due to repulsion between the excitons inside the light cone appears to be prone to a modulational instability towards the non-radiative surface polariton modes. Above the corresponding threshold, the pumped 2D exciton gas acts as an optical parametric generator of twin polariton beams. Conversely, below the threshold, the mirror acquires the phase-conjugating properties.

### [127] [Experimental straintronics in nanotube quantum dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12180)
*L. Huang,I. G. Rebollo,A. R. Champagne*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究在单壁碳纳米管量子点（SWCNT-QD）晶体管中实验展示了量子输运应变电子学（QTS），通过原位可逆的单轴应变（0–3%）实现对量子点掺杂和带隙的精确机械调控，排除了电容门控效应，验证了能带结构变化的定量机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单壁碳纳米管（single-wall carbon nanotubes, SWCNTs）具有原子级精确的边缘和单一的量子输运通道，是研究量子输运应变电子学（quantum transport straintronics, QTS）的理想平台，即利用机械应变精确控制量子输运。

Method: 制备悬空SWCNT晶体管（沟道长度约30 nm），通过移动金夹钳对纳米管施加可逆单轴应变（Δε_mech ≈ 0–3%），并采集dI/dV_B–V_B–V_G和dI/dV_B–V_B–Δε_mech的详细电荷输运数据。

Result: 数据显示了SWCNT-QD显著的门控效应，且具有精确的可逆性，与QTS理论高度吻合，证明纳米管处于弹性应变状态。机械控制量子点掺杂并非源于电容门控效应（capacitive-gating effect），而是源于可定量预测的能带结构变化，包括应变可调带隙（strain-tunable bandgap）。

Conclusion: 对SWCNT-QD掺杂和带隙的精确机械控制在量子比特（qubits）、凝聚态物理（condensed matter physics）和同质结分子晶体管（homojunction molecular transistors）中具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: Single-wall carbon nanotubes (SWCNTs) are narrow ribbons of graphene with atomically precise edges and a single quantum transport channel, at experimentally-relevant dopings. This makes them ideal systems to harness quantum transport straintronics (QTS), i.e. using mechanical strain to control accurately quantum transport. We present QTS data from three single-wall carbon nanotube quantum dot (SWCNT-QD) transistors over a broad range of in-situ tunable and reversible uniaxial strain ($Δ\varepsilon_\text{mech}\approx$ 0 to 3 %). We first present the nanofabrication of the suspended SWCNT transistors whose channel lengths are $\approx$ 30 nm. The channels are strained by moving gold clamps holding firmly the nanotubes. We present detailed charge transport data, $dI/dV_{\text{B}} - V_{\text{B}} - V_{\text{G}}$ and $dI/dV_{\text{B}} - V_{\text{B}} - Δ\varepsilon_\text{mech}$, showing a large mechanical-gating effect of the SWCNT-QDs. The precise reversibility of the data, and their agreement with QTS theory, confirms that the tubes are strained elastically. We demonstrate that the mechanical control of the QD doping is not due to capacitive-gating effects, but to quantitatively predictable bandstructure changes including a strain-tunable bandgap. This precise mechanical control of the doping and bandgap of SWCNT-QDs could find applications in qubits, condensed matter physics, and homojunction molecular transistors.

### [128] [Enhanced localization length in a disordered one-dimensional band via cavity coupling to delocalized states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12224)
*Francesco Mattiotti,Guido Pupillo,Jérôme Dubail,David Hagenmüller*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究无序系统中腔耦合电子态的局域化性质。通过最小二带模型和微扰论-转移矩阵方法，发现腔辅助跳跃随距离指数衰减，本征态在微扰区域外仍保持局域化，但局域化长度随光-物质耦合增强而增大。在无序朗道带中，边缘态间的有效腔介导耦合也呈指数衰减，但局域化长度在实验参数下可达微米尺度，使得对应态在介观尺度上呈现有效退局域化行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于量子霍尔系统中腔介导跳跃（cavity-mediated hopping）的最新理论提议，旨在探索腔耦合对无序系统中电子态局域化性质的影响。

Method: 首先引入一个最小二带模型（minimal two-band model），其中无序一维能带中的局域态通过均匀腔模与激发扩展态能带耦合。将微扰论（perturbation theory）与转移矩阵方法（transfer-matrix approach）相结合进行分析；对于无序朗道带，则采用文献[1,2]中发展的理论框架。

Result: 腔辅助跳跃随距离指数衰减，表明即使在微扰区域外本征态仍保持局域化，但局域化长度随光-物质耦合强度增大，在单电子超强耦合（ultrastrong-coupling）区域可覆盖多个格点。无序朗道带中边缘态间的有效耦合也呈指数衰减，但局域化长度在实验可行参数下可达微米尺度。通过反参与比（inverse participation ratio）分析，证实这种增强耦合主要由上朗道带中最扩展的态介导。

Conclusion: 在无序量子霍尔系统中，腔诱导跳跃虽仍呈指数局域化，但对应的局域化长度可以足够大，使得相关态在介观尺度上表现出有效的退局域化行为。

Abstract: We investigate the localization properties of cavity-coupled electronic states in disordered systems, motivated by recent proposals of cavity-mediated hopping in quantum Hall systems. We first introduce a minimal two-band model in which localized states in a disordered one-dimensional band are coupled, through a homogeneous cavity mode, to an excited band of delocalized states. Combining perturbation theory with a transfer-matrix approach, we show that cavity-assisted hopping between localized states decays exponentially with distance, implying that the eigenstates remain localized even beyond the perturbative regime. Nevertheless, the corresponding localization length increases with the light-matter coupling strength and can extend over several lattice sites in the single-electron ultrastrong-coupling regime. We then study a disordered Landau band coupled to a cavity mode within the framework developed in Refs.[1,2]. We find that the effective cavity-mediated coupling between edge states also decays exponentially with distance, but with a localization length that can reach micrometer scales for experimentally realistic parameters. By analyzing the inverse participation ratio, we show that this enhanced coupling is predominantly mediated by the most extended states of the upper Landau band. Our results demonstrate that, while cavity-induced hopping in disordered quantum Hall systems remains exponentially localized, the associated localization length can become sufficiently large for the corresponding states to exhibit effectively delocalized behavior on mesoscopic length scales.

</details>


### [129] [Stacking switching between correlation-protected radial Rashba field and persistent spin textures in graphene encapsulated by 1T-TaS$_2$ monolayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12239)
*Juraj Mnich,Marko Milivojević,Martin Gmitra*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算、紧束缚模型和Kubo形式主义，研究了被电荷密度波相1T-TaS₂单层封装的双层石墨烯异质结中的电子结构、自旋织构以及电荷-自旋/轨道转换。发现非对称(AA)堆叠产生近π/2的累积Rashba相位，导致非常规Rashba-Edelstein效应，其响应强度是常规效应的35倍；对称(AA')堆叠则产生稳定的纯面外持续自旋织构。此外，轨道霍尔效应效率远超自旋霍尔效应三个数量级，且在近邻诱导的能隙中轨道霍尔电导呈现有限平台而自旋霍尔电导消失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索通过改变堆叠次序来调控石墨烯异质结中电荷-自旋与电荷-轨道相互转换（interconversion）的不同机制，为自旋电子学（spintronics）和轨道电子学（orbitronics）器件提供设计原则。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）、紧束缚模型（tight-binding modeling）以及Kubo形式主义（Kubo formalism）进行理论分析。

Result: (1) 非对称(AA)堆叠中近邻场（proximity fields）的相长干涉产生近π/2的Rashba相位，形成纯径向Rashba自旋模式，导致非常规Rashba-Edelstein效应，比常规效应强35倍；(2) 对称(AA')堆叠保持水平镜面对称（horizontal mirror symmetry），产生稳定的纯面外持续自旋织构（persistent spin texture）；(3) 轨道霍尔效应（orbital Hall effect）效率超过自旋霍尔效应（spin Hall effect）三个数量级；(4) 在近邻诱导能隙中，轨道霍尔电导（orbital Hall conductivity）呈现有限平台，而自旋霍尔电导（spin Hall conductivity）为零。

Conclusion: 石墨烯封装异质结可通过堆叠次序的选择，实现截然不同的电荷-自旋与电荷-轨道转换机制，是一种有前景的材料平台。

Abstract: We investigate the electronic structure, spin textures, and charge to spin/orbital transport in graphene encapsulated by 1T-TaS$_{2}$ monolayers in the charge density wave phase. Using first-principles calculations, tight-binding modeling, and the Kubo formalism, we show that the encapsulation stacking dictates fundamentally distinct transport regimes. In the asymmetrical (AA) stacking, proximity fields from both interfaces constructively interfere, yielding a cumulative Rashba phase of nearly $π/2$. This pure radial Rashba spin pattern leads to the unconventional Rashba-Edelstein effect, which robustly dominates over the conventional response by a factor of 35 across a wide energy range. Conversely, the symmetrical (AA') stacking preserves a horizontal mirror symmetry, establishing a stable, purely out-of-plane persistent spin texture. Furthermore, the computed orbital Hall effect is exceptionally efficient, surpassing the spin Hall effect by three orders of magnitude. Within the proximity-induced spectral gaps, the orbital Hall conductivity exhibits a finite plateau, whereas the spin Hall conductivity vanishes. Our findings establish graphene encapsulated heterostructures as a promising system for realizing distinct charge to spin and charge to orbital interconversion regimes determined by the choice of stacking order.

### [130] [Gate-tunable spin-valley transport via carrier velocity in monolayer WSe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12353)
*Otman Bouladiane,Hocine Bahlouli,Clarence Cortes,David Laroze,Ahmed Jellal*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从理论上研究了单层二硒化钨（WSe₂）中自旋和谷分辨的量子输运，通过有效有质量狄拉克哈密顿量描述，重点分析了在有限势垒区域中同时调制费米速度和标量势的影响。结果表明，速度与势垒的联合调控可作为控制二维过渡金属硫族化合物中自旋-谷物理的强大理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索通过速度与势垒联合工程控制二维过渡金属硫族化合物（transition-metal dichalcogenides）中自旋和谷自由度（spin and valley degrees of freedom）的全新理论途径。

Method: 采用有效有质量狄拉克哈密顿量（massive Dirac Hamiltonian）描述单层WSe₂，通过引入速度比ξ=v₂/v₁模拟光学中斯涅尔-笛卡尔定律（Snell-Descartes law）的类比，求解狄拉克方程并在界面处施加流守恒匹配条件，计算自旋和谷分辨的透射概率与电导。

Result: 势垒速度、标量势、入射角、入射能量和势垒宽度可作为输运的有效控制参数，产生强各向异性和共振隧穿特征；自旋和谷极化电流的幅度与方向可通过速度及势垒调制连续调控。

Conclusion: 联合速度与势垒工程为控制二维过渡金属硫族化合物中的自旋-谷物理提供了强大的理论框架。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate spin- and valley-resolved quantum transport in monolayer tungsten diselenide (WSe$_2$) described by an effective massive Dirac Hamiltonian. Particular attention is devoted to a finite barrier region characterized by simultaneously modulated Fermi velocity and scalar potential. The barrier velocity $v_2$ is related to the external velocity $v_1$ through a velocity ratio $ξ=v_2/v_1$, motivated by an optical analogy with the Snell-Descartes law. The exact refraction condition depends on the full spin- and valley-resolved dispersion, and the simple ratio $ξ=v_2/v_1$ is recovered only in the massless, symmetric limit. The interplay of intrinsic spin-orbit coupling in the conduction and valence bands, quantified by $λ_c$ and $λ_v$, with spin- and valley-dependent Zeeman fields, $M_s$ and $M_v$, gives rise to substantial changes in the quasiparticle dispersion, leading to pronounced modifications of the transport characteristics. By solving the Dirac equation and enforcing current-conserving matching conditions at the interfaces, we compute the spin- and valley-dependent transmission probability and conductance. Our results demonstrate that the barrier velocity, scalar potential, incidence angle, incident energy, and barrier width serve as effective control parameters for transport, giving rise to strong anisotropy and resonant tunneling features. Furthermore, we show that both the magnitude and orientation of spin- and valley-polarized currents can be continuously tuned via velocity and potential modulation. These findings establish combined velocity and potential engineering as a powerful theoretical framework for controlling spin-valley physics in two-dimensional transition-metal dichalcogenides.

### [131] [Arithmetic Symmetry in Ideal Prouhet-Tarry-Escott Solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07735)
*Yu-Dai Tsai,Junseok Lee,Fuminobu Takahashi*

Main category: math.NT

TL;DR: 本文研究了手征规范理论（chiral gauge theory）中积分电荷谱反常抵消所启发的理想三次Prouhet-Tarry-Escott问题的对称解集，发现其计数函数满足 $N_{\mathrm{sym}}(H) = \frac{4\log 2}{3π^2}H^3\log H+O(H^3)$ 的渐近式，对数增强因子源自平方和表示函数的二阶矩，表明对称解集蕴含着丰富的数论结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手征规范理论中积分电荷谱的反常抵消（anomaly cancellation）问题在数论层面催生了对理想三次Prouhet-Tarry-Escott问题对称解集的系统研究。

Method: 利用对称性将原问题约化为两平方和方程（sum-of-two-squares equation）$x^2+y^2=u^2+v^2$ 在适当奇偶性条件下的整数求解，进而借助平方和表示函数（representation function）的解析性质推导计数函数的渐近行为。

Result: 对称解集的计数函数满足 $N_{\mathrm{sym}}(H) = \frac{4\log 2}{3π^2}H^3\log H+O(H^3)$，其中对数增强项来自平方和表示函数的二阶矩，表明对称解集规模显著大于朴素度加权盒计数（degree-weighted box-counting）标度 $H^3$ 的预期。

Conclusion: 该渐近结果揭示了一个具有丰富算术结构的三次理想解子族，并表明成对的无反常积分电荷谱可能反映了某种深层次的数论结构。

Abstract: Motivated in part by anomaly cancellation for integral charge spectra in chiral gauge theory, we study the symmetric locus in the ideal degree-three Prouhet-Tarry-Escott problem. A symmetric integer solution is one whose entries are paired about a common center $c\in \frac12\mathbb Z$. This symmetry reduces the problem to a sum-of-two-squares equation, $x^2+y^2=u^2+v^2$, in integer variables, subject to the appropriate parity conditions. Thus the problem is governed by representations as sums of two squares. For the full symmetric locus, let $N_{\mathrm{sym}}(H)$ denote the number of nontrivial symmetric integer solutions of height at most $H$, counted with unordered multiset conventions and summed over the admissible centers. Then \begin{align*} N_{\mathrm{sym}}(H) = \frac{4\log 2}{3π^2}H^3\log H+O(H^3). \end{align*} The logarithmic enhancement comes from the second moment of the sum-of-two-squares representation function. In particular, the symmetric locus is larger than one would expect from the naive $H^3$ degree-weighted box-counting scale alone. This asymptotic identifies a large arithmetically structured subfamily of the ideal degree-three solution space, and suggests that paired anomaly-free integral charge spectra reflect a fundamental number-theoretic structure.

</details>

### [132] [Unusual half-metallic state in unconventional magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11384)
*Yuri B. Kudasov*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新型半金属态——螺旋磁性（helimagnet）中的半金属，其能隙的出现与否取决于波矢方向，源于能带结构的多叶覆盖拓扑（multi-sheeted covering topology），并通过p波和f波的紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）加以说明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统半金属铁磁体（half-metallic ferromagnets）中，能隙固定出现在一种自旋投影（spin projection）上，而作者试图探索在螺旋磁体（helimagnets）中是否可能存在一种非常规的半金属态，其中能隙对应的自旋投影由波矢方向决定。

Method: 采用二维紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）分别构建p波和f波半金属，分析其能带结构的多叶覆盖拓扑性质，并进一步讨论纳米结构中非常规p波半金属的复杂能带结构。

Result: 在螺旋磁体中实现了波矢方向决定能隙自旋投影的非常规半金属态；在量子阱（quantum well）中形成了具有螺旋自旋结构（helical spin structure）的驻波（standing wave），并存在持久的自旋电流（persistent spin current）。

Conclusion: 这种基于拓扑能带结构的半金属态可在晶体和范德瓦尔斯系统（van der Waals systems）中实现，为探索新型自旋电子学（spintronics）器件提供了可能。

Abstract: Half-metallic ferromagnets exhibit a gap in the density of states for one spin projection while remaining gapless for the opposite spin. We show that in helimagnets an unusual half-metallic state can exist, where the spin projection that experiences the gap is determined by the direction of the wave vector. This state originates from the nontrivial topology of the band structure, specifically from the dispersion forming a multi-sheeted covering over the Brillouin zone. We present two-dimensional tight-binding models for $p$-wave and $f$-wave half metals. These structures can be realized in crystalline and van der Waals systems. The complex band structure of the unusual $p$-wave half metal in nanostructures is also discussed. In a quantum well, a standing wave with a helical spin structure is formed, and a persistent spin current exists.

### [133] [Synthetic Altermagnetism Beyond the Crystal Limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11481)
*Rodolfo A. Gallardo,Andrea M. León,Jürgen Lindner,Jhon W. González*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本研究首次在由反铁磁耦合铁磁薄膜构成的人工连续介质平台中实验实现了交变磁（altermagnetic）自旋波（magnonics），验证了其动量依赖劈裂、节点结构及各向异性等频轮廓等关键特征，并揭示了长程偶极相互作用与多层结构奇偶性对交变磁激发谱的重构效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统交变磁（altermagnetism）现象源于晶体材料中磁子晶格旋转的点群对称性，其研究局限于晶态体系。本文旨在突破这一限制，在非晶态连续介质中人工合成交变磁自旋波动力学（altermagnetic magnonics），并探索偶极相互作用及多层结构对其能谱的影响。

Method: 采用反铁磁耦合的铁磁薄膜交替排列并引入面内交换各向异性（in-plane exchange anisotropies），构建连续介质平台；在偶极-交换（dipole-exchange）框架下求解线性化朗道-利夫希茨方程（linearized Landau-Lifshitz equation），分析体系的磁激发谱。

Result: 该人工结构成功复现了A型交变磁体（A-type altermagnets）的特征：动量依赖劈裂（momentum-dependent splitting）、节点方向（nodal directions）和各向异性等频轮廓（anisotropic isofrequency contours）。长程偶极相互作用使交换主导的能谱发生定性重构：消除名义节点简并、混合相反手性模式，并在交换极限下为节点的波矢方向产生有限且依赖厚度的劈裂。将双层推广至多层结构后，交变磁效应发生奇偶性依赖重构，区分了表面与体交变磁激发。

Conclusion: 本研究交变磁自旋波现象是一种可在偶极-交换多层体系中工程化设计的集体响应，其存在超越微观晶体对称性，为人造交变磁体系的研究开辟了连续介质途径。

Abstract: Altermagnetic magnons in crystalline materials exhibit momentum-dependent splitting whose nodal structure and chiral character are governed by the point-group symmetry of the magnetic sublattice rotation. Here, we demonstrate the first synthetic realization of altermagnetic magnonics in a continuum platform composed of antiferromagnetically coupled ferromagnetic films with alternating in-plane exchange anisotropies, showing that the key signatures of altermagnetic magnonics emerge beyond the crystalline setting. Solving the linearized Landau-Lifshitz equation within a dipole-exchange framework, we show that this architecture reproduces the characteristic momentum-dependent splitting, nodal directions, and anisotropic isofrequency contours of A-type altermagnets. Long-range dipolar interactions qualitatively reconstruct this exchange-driven spectrum by lifting the nominal nodal degeneracy, hybridizing opposite-chirality modes, and producing a finite, thickness-dependent wave-vector splitting along directions that are nodal in the exchange-only limit. Extending the bilayer to finite multilayers reveals that synthetic altermagnetism undergoes a parity-dependent reconstruction that separates surface and bulk altermagnetic excitations. These results establish altermagnetic magnon phenomenology as an engineerable collective response of dipole-exchange multilayers beyond microscopic crystal symmetries.

### [134] [Ferromagnetism from the geometry of localized wavefunctions in moiré systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11302)
*Miguel Gonçalves,Sarang Gopalakrishnan*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于安德森局域态（Anderson-localized states）窄带中的铁磁性机制，利用单粒子局域化（single-particle localization）推导交换相互作用（exchange interactions）的可控理论。研究发现，准周期莫尔带（moiré band）中，铁磁性的临界相互作用强度对局域轨道实空间重叠的几何形状高度敏感，存在明显共振点，在此处远低于带隙的相互作用能量即可引发铁磁性。该机制区别于以往基于布洛赫带（Bloch bands）量子几何（quantum geometry）的铁磁性机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用单粒子局域化特性，在窄带内推导交换相互作用理论；分析准周期系统中半填充莫尔带情形，考察局域轨道实空间重叠几何与铁磁临界相互作用强度的关系。

Result: 发现铁磁临界相互作用强度对局域轨道实空间重叠几何高度敏感，存在明确共振点；在此共振点附近，铁磁性可在远低于其他能带带隙的相互作用能量下出现，且所有理论近似可控，临界点预测具有定量准确性。

Conclusion: 识别出一条基于实空间波函数几何（geometry of real-space wavefunctions）的新型铁磁性路径，与先前基于布洛赫带量子几何的机制截然不同。

Abstract: We present a mechanism for ferromagnetism in narrow bands consisting of Anderson-localized states. We exploit single-particle localization to derive a controlled theory of exchange interactions within the narrow band. For quasiperiodic systems with a half-filled moiré band, we show that the critical interaction strength for ferromagnetism is highly sensitive to the geometry of real-space overlaps between localized orbitals: we find well-defined resonances at which ferromagnetism sets in for interaction energies that are far lower than the gap to other bands. Near these resonances, all the approximations in our theory are controlled, so our critical point predictions are quantitative. We show examples both in one and two dimensions. Our work identifies a route to ferromagnetism based on the geometry of real-space wavefunctions, distinct from previously found mechanisms based on the quantum geometry of Bloch bands.

### [135] [Exact distribution of the output of a deep-layered machine](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11965)
*Thomas M. A. Fink*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该论文推导了深层布尔网络（deep Boolean network）输出的精确有限深度分布，发现该分布仅依赖于输出的汉明权重（Hamming weight），且随着深度增加会偏向低权重和高权重函数，但在与 $2^k$ 成正比的交叉深度（crossover depth）处达到峰值，随后坍缩为常数函数 true 和 false。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管深度分层机器（deep-layered machines）是深度学习和数字计算的基石，但其全局输出函数的统计特性仍缺乏理解。本文旨在揭示这类网络输出分布的数学结构。

Method: 论文针对宽度为 $k$、深度为 $n$ 的布尔函数机器，推导了输出分布的精确有限深度解析表达式。该分布仅依赖于输出结果的汉明权重（Hamming weight）。

Result: 随着深度 $n$ 增加，分布倾向于偏好汉明权重极低或极高的函数。这种偏向在深度约正比于 $2^k$ 的交叉深度（crossover depth）处达到峰值，之后分布坍缩为仅包含常数函数 true 和 false 的极端情形。

Conclusion: 深层布尔网络的输出统计存在一个从偏向极端函数到完全退化为常函数的相变行为，交叉深度由网络宽度指数决定。该发现为理解深度架构的表示能力与统计偏置提供了理论洞见。

Abstract: Deep-layered machines, in which each node computes a Boolean function of all nodes below it, underpin deep learning and digital computation. Yet the statistics of their global output function remain poorly understood. We derive the exact finite-depth distribution of the output of a machine with width $k$ and depth $n$. The distribution depends only on the Hamming weight of the output, and as $n$ increases favors functions with low and high Hamming weights. But this bias peaks at a crossover depth proportional to $2^k$ before collapsing onto the constant functions true and false.

</details>


### [136] [Non-Hermitian Delocalization Realizes Random Dirac Criticality in One Dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12089)
*Bo Li,Shen Zhang,Ren Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该论文证明非厄米（non-Hermitian）系统在周期边界条件（PBC）下的退局域态本质上属于临界态，实现了一维随机狄拉克费米子（random Dirac fermions）的普适类，并通过谱拓扑（spectral topology）机制系统性地解释了这种临界性如何普遍出现于非厄米系统中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究非厄米系统如何规避安德森局域化（Anderson localization）并在一维中展现退局域态的物理本质，探索这种退局域态是否具有内在的临界性及其所属的普适类（universality class）。

Method: 通过厄米化（Hermitization）方法将谱缠绕（spectral winding）与拓扑安德森相变（topological Anderson transitions）联系起来，分析非厄米系统在周期边界条件下的退局域态性质。

Result: 发现非厄米系统在周期边界条件下的退局域态本质上是临界态，属于一维随机狄拉克费米子的普适类，并展现出具有普适代数关联（universal algebraic correlations）的狄拉克型临界性（Dirac-type criticality）。

Conclusion: 非厄米性通过谱拓扑机制普遍地促进了临界性的产生，为理解一维非厄米退局域化现象提供了一个统一的描述框架。

Abstract: Non-Hermitian systems can evade Anderson localization and exhibit delocalized states even in one dimension. Here, we show that such non-Hermitian delocalized states under periodic boundary conditions (PBC) are intrinsically critical, realizing the universality class of one-dimensional random Dirac fermions. By linking spectral winding to topological Anderson transitions via Hermitization, we demonstrate that the delocalized PBC states exhibit a Dirac-type criticality with universal algebraic correlations. In contrast to Hermitian systems, where this criticality occurs only at fine-tuned transition points, it emerges generically in non-Hermitian systems as a consequence of spectral topology. These results identify a universal mechanism by which non-Hermiticity promotes criticality, providing a unified description of non-Hermitian delocalization in one dimension.

</details>


### [137] [Roughening of active nonlinear interfaces with broken tilt symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12190)
*Ailén M. Cámara,Alejandro B. Kolton,José Luis Iguaín*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文研究具有非线性弹性且受时间关联噪声驱动的界面的粗糙化行为，通过标度分析、自洽 Hartree 近似和大规模数值模拟，揭示了 Larkin、非简谐 Larkin 与 Edwards–Wilkinson 三个普适类及其交叉标度，为最小非线性弹性 Ornstein–Uhlenbeck 活性界面的有限尺寸与交叉效应提供了统一描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间关联噪声会破坏统计倾斜对称性（statistical tilt symmetry），使界面的标度行为与经典理论不同；现有研究缺乏对这一情形下非线性弹性界面粗糙化过程的系统分析。

Method: 采用标度论证（scaling arguments）和自洽 Hartree 近似（self-consistent Hartree approximation）推导交叉图（crossover diagram）与稳态结构因子（steady-state structure factor）；并进行大规模数值模拟验证理论预测。

Result: 识别出三个标度区间（scaling regimes），分别对应 Larkin、非简谐 Larkin（anharmonic Larkin）和 Edwards–Wilkinson 普适类（universality classes），并得到分隔这些区间的交叉长度（crossover lengths）；数值模拟在完整参数范围内定量确认了理论结果。

Conclusion: 该工作为具有非线性弹性和时间关联噪声的活性界面提供了统一的有限尺寸效应与交叉行为的描述，揭示了一个最小非线性弹性 Ornstein–Uhlenbeck 活性界面（minimal nonlinear-elastic Ornstein–Uhlenbeck active interface）的完整标度图像。

Abstract: We study the roughening of an interface with nonlinear elasticity driven by temporally correlated noise, which breaks statistical tilt symmetry. Using scaling arguments and a self-consistent Hartree approximation, we derive the crossover diagram and the steady-state structure factor. We identify three scaling regimes associated with the Larkin, anharmonic Larkin, and Edwards--Wilkinson universality classes, and obtain the crossover lengths separating them. Numerical simulations of large systems confirm the analytical predictions over the full parameter range. Our results provide a unified description of finite-size and crossover effects in a minimal nonlinear-elastic Ornstein--Uhlenbeck active interface.

</details>

# hep-ex [[Back]](#toc)

### [138] [A High-Precision Clock Synchronization System for the CEPC Accelerator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11590)
*Jun Hu,Xin Zhou,Xiaoshan Jiang,Dapeng Jin*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 针对环形正负电子对撞机（CEPC）100公里隧道中192个控制节点的30皮秒同步精度需求，本文提出并验证了一种基于增强型White Rabbit（WR）的时钟同步系统，通过硬件重构（DSPLL替代DAC+VCXO）、重启不确定性优化、级联全局控制架构及强化学习辅助PID自整定等方法，在点对点和多级级联测试中均显著优于CEPC 30皮秒预算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 环形正负电子对撞机（CEPC）需要沿100公里地下隧道向192个控制节点分发参考时钟，同步精度要求达到30皮秒（标准偏差），现有标准White Rabbit（WR）系统在噪声预算和重启不确定性方面存在瓶颈，无法满足该指标。

Method: 通过噪声预算分析识别标准WR从环路的模拟驱动链（DAC+VCXO+倍频PLL）和重启时序不确定性为主要限制因素；将DAC+VCXO替换为Si5345A DSPLL时钟发生器（DCO相位控制），去除板级模拟调谐级；采用GTX收发器相位对齐与手动字节对齐修复降低重启不确定性；引入级联全局控制架构，采用TD3强化学习自动整定PC端PID参数，并加入片上温度前馈校准（-0.76 ps/°C）。

Result: 点对点同步精度在1米光纤下为3.38皮秒、50公里光纤下为3.92皮秒；12级级联末端节点在恒温下为6.66皮秒、13°C温度波动下为7.30皮秒；同步时钟TIE抖动保持在1皮秒以下；重启不确定性为2.82皮秒（标准偏差）；4级级联系统连续稳定运行25小时。所有指标均优于CEPC 30皮秒预算。

Conclusion: 所提出的增强型White Rabbit（WR）时钟同步系统在点对点、多级级联及温度波动条件下均满足并显著优于CEPC 30皮秒同步精度要求，硬件重构、级联架构与智能控制策略的有效性得到实验验证。

Abstract: The Circular Electron Positron Collider (CEPC) distributes a reference clock distributed to 192 control nodes along its 100~km underground tunnel. The required synchronization precision is 30~ps (standard deviation). We present an enhanced White Rabbit (WR)-based clock synchronization system designed to meet this requirement. A noise-budget analysis of the standard WR slave loop identifies the analog actuation chain (DAC + VCXO + multiplier PLL) and restart-induced timing uncertainty as the dominant limitations. In our redesigned node, the DAC+VCXO chain is replaced by a Si5345A DSPLL clock generator with DCO-based phase control, removing the board-level analog tuning stage. GTX transceiver phase alignment and manual byte-alignment fixing reduce restart uncertainty from 88.8~ps to 12~ps peak-to-peak. For multi-node operation, we introduce a cascaded global-control architecture with PC-side PID auto-tuned by TD3 reinforcement learning, on-chip-temperature feed-forward calibrated to $-0.76\,\mathrm{ps}/^\circ\mathrm{C}$. The measured point-to-point synchronization precision is 3.38~ps over 1~m fiber and 3.92~ps over 50~km. In a 12-level cascade, the end-node precision reaches 6.66~ps at constant temperature and 7.30~ps under a 13$\,^\circ$C temperature swing. Synchronized-clock TIE jitter stays below 1~ps regardless of cascade depth. Restart uncertainty is 2.82~ps (std.\ dev.). A 4-level cascade operated stably for 25 hours of continuous monitoring. All measured metrics fall well within the CEPC 30~ps budget.

</details>

Zhu,Lin Zhu,S. H. Zhu,T. J. Zhu,W. D. Zhu,W. J. Zhu,W. Z. Zhu,Y. C. Zhu,Z. A. Zhu,X. Y. Zhuang,J. H. Zou*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于BESIII探测器采集的7.33 fb$^{-1}$数据，更新测量了$D_s^+ \to τ^+ ν_τ$的分支比，通过四种τ衰变道得到最精确结果，并进一步提取了CKM矩阵元$|V_{cs}|$与$D_s^+$衰变常数$f_{D_s^+}$的乘积，结果与标准模型轻子味普适性（lepton flavor universality）预言一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通过更高统计量的数据对$D_s^+ \to τ^+ ν_τ$分支比进行更新测量，以提高测量精度，并基于此提取CKM矩阵元$|V_{cs}|$和$D_s^+$衰变常数$f_{D_s^+}$，检验轻子味普适性（lepton flavor universality）。

Method: 利用BESIII探测器在质心能量4.128至4.226 GeV下采集的7.33 fb$^{-1}$ $e^+e^-$湮灭数据，通过四种τ衰变道（$τ^+ \to e^+ ν_e \barν_τ$、$μ^+ ν_μ \barν_τ$、$π^+\barν_τ$、$π^+ π^{0} \barν_τ$）测量分支比。

Result: 测得$\mathcal{B}({D_s^+ \to τ^+ ν_τ}) = (5.37 \pm 0.08_{\rm stat} \pm 0.06_{\rm syst})\%$，为目前最精确结果；$f_{D_s^+} |V_{cs}| = (248.2 \pm 1.9_{\rm stat} \pm 1.4_{\rm syst} \pm 0.6_{\rm input} \pm 0.8_{\rm EM})$ MeV；结合格点量子色动力学（lattice QCD）得到$|V_{cs}| = 0.993 \pm 0.008_{\rm stat} \pm 0.006_{\rm syst} \pm 0.003_{\rm input} \pm 0.003_{\rm EM}$；利用CKMfitter组输入得到$f_{D_s^+} = (255.0 \pm 1.9_{\rm stat} \pm 1.4_{\rm syst} \pm 0.6_{\rm input} \pm 0.8_{\rm EM})$ MeV；与$D_s^+ \to μ^+ ν_μ$世界平均值的分支比之比为$10.04 \pm 0.29$。

Conclusion: 测量结果与标准模型（Standard Model）的轻子味普适性（lepton flavor universality）预言一致，确认了当前理论框架在该过程的有效性。

Abstract: Using a dataset of 7.33 fb$^{-1}$ of $e^+ e^-$ annihilation data collected with the BESIII detector at center-of-mass energies from 4.128 to 4.226 GeV, we report an updated measurement of the branching fraction of $D_s^+ \to τ^+ ν_τ$ via four $τ^+$ decay modes: $τ^+ \to e^+ ν_e \barν_τ$, $μ^+ ν_μ \barν_τ$, $π^+\barν_τ$, and $π^+ π^{0} \barν_τ$. The branching fraction is determined to be $\mathcal{B}({D_s^+ \to τ^+ ν_τ}) = (5.37 \pm 0.08_{\rm stat} \pm 0.06_{\rm syst})$ %. The product of the modulus of the Cabibbo-Kobayashi-Maskawa matrix element $|V_{cs}|$ and the $D_s^+$ decay constant $f_{D_s^+}$ is measured to be $f_{D_s^+} |V_{cs}| = (248.2 \pm 1.9_{\rm stat} \pm 1.4_{\rm syst} \pm 0.6_{\rm input} \pm 0.8_{\rm EM})$ MeV. Both the branching fraction and the product $f_{D_s^+} |V_{cs}|$ are the most precise results yet obtained. Then, taking $f_{D_s^+}$ from lattice quantum chromodynamics calculations results in $|V_{cs}| = 0.993 \pm 0.008_{\rm stat} \pm 0.006_{\rm syst} \pm 0.003_{\rm input} \pm 0.003_{\rm EM}$. Conversely, one finds $f_{D_s^+} = (255.0 \pm 1.9_{\rm stat} \pm 1.4_{\rm syst} \pm 0.6_{\rm input} \pm 0.8_{\rm EM})$ MeV when taking $|V_{cs}|$ from the CKMfitter group as an input. Combining with the world average value of $D_s^+ \to μ^+ ν_μ$, the ratio of the branching fractions between $D_s^+ \to τ^+ ν_τ$ and $D_s^+ \to μ^+ ν_μ$ is estimated to be $10.04 \pm 0.29$, which is consistent with the Standard Model prediction of lepton flavor universality.

</details>

Zhu,Lin Zhu,S. H. Zhu,T. J. Zhu,W. D. Zhu,W. J. Zhu,W. Z. Zhu,Y. C. Zhu,Z. A. Zhu,X. Y. Zhuang,M. Zhuge,J. H. Zou,J. Zu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于J/ψ共振附近26个能量点的直接扫描，首次测量了J/ψ→K̄⁰K*(892)⁰+c.c.和J/ψ→K⁺K*(892)⁻+c.c.过程中强振幅与电磁振幅之间的相对相位φ_{γ, 3g}。中性道相位意外偏离正交性（90°）达4.2σ，而带电道相位与180°在1σ内一致。分支比精度提高两倍以上，电磁贡献扣除后强振幅比在1.8σ内满足同位旋对称性，直接CP破坏搜索显示不对称性为零。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在J/ψ衰变中，强振幅与电磁振幅之间的相对相位是理解强相互作用与电磁相互作用干涉机制的关键物理量，但此前从未被直接测量。该研究旨在填补这一空白，并检验相关过程中是否存在超出预期的新物理效应。

Method: 利用J/ψ共振附近26个能量点的直接扫描数据，对J/ψ→K̄⁰K*(892)⁰+c.c.和J/ψ→K⁺K*(892)⁻+c.c.两个衰变道的强振幅与电磁振幅之间的相对相位φ_{γ, 3g}进行了首次实验测量。同时测量了各道的分支比及其比值，并基于电磁贡献扣除提取了强振幅比，以及搜索了直接CP破坏效应。

Result: 中性道相位约150°，与正交性（90°）偏离4.2σ，与相对实振幅（0°或180°）分别偏离10.0σ或1.6σ。带电道相位与180°在1σ内一致，表现出模型依赖行为。分支比与世界平均值一致但精度提高两倍以上。扣除电磁贡献后的强振幅比在1.8σ内满足同位旋对称性。直接CP破坏不对称性与零一致。

Conclusion: 中性道相位与期望的正交性存在显著偏离，而带电道相位接近180°，提示不同电荷道可能呈现不同的干涉特性。电磁贡献扣除后强振幅比支持同位旋对称性，且未发现直接CP破坏迹象。

Abstract: Using a direct scan of 26 energy points near the $J/ψ$ resonance, we perform the first measurement of the relative phase $φ_{γ, 3g}$ between the strong and electromagnetic amplitudes in $J/ψ\to\bar K^0 K^*(892)^0+c.c.$ and $J/ψ\to K^+ K^*(892)^-+c.c.$. Unexpectedly, the phase in the neutral channel is found to be $\sim 150^\circ$, deviating from orthogonality ($90^\circ$) by 4.2$σ$ and from a relative real amplitude (0$^\circ$ or 180$^\circ$) by 10.0$σ$ or 1.6$σ$, respectively. In contrast, the charged channel phase is consistent with $\sim 180^\circ$ within 1$σ$, exhibiting model-dependent behavior. The corresponding branching fractions are consistent with the world averages but achieve better than twofold improvement in precision. The ratios between the branching fractions of $J/ψ\to\bar K^0 K^*(892)^0+c.c.$ and $J/ψ\to K^+ K^*(892)^-+c.c.$ are also measured. After subtracting the electromagnetic contribution, the corresponding strong amplitude ratios obey isospin symmetry within $1.8σ$. A search for direct $CP$ violation yields asymmetries consistent with zero.

</details>


### [141] [Hidden-sectors search and probe of discrete symmetries at the REDTOP experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12158)
*The REDTOP COllaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出 REDTOP 实验装置，通过收集约 $10^{14}$ 个 η 介子和 $10^{12}$ 个 η′ 介子，利用四种新物理“门户”（Vector、Scalar、Axion-like、Heavy Lepton）寻找超出标准模型的新物理，同时进行 CP/T 不变量、轻子普适性检验，并改进 η/η′ 跃迁形状因子测量，为缪子反常磁矩中的强子光-光散射贡献提供关键输入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: η 和 η′ 介子近乎是准戈德斯通玻色子（nearly Goldstone bosons），其衰变动力学受到强约束，为探测超出标准模型（Beyond the Standard Model）的新物理提供了独特窗口；而先前的实验仅收集约 $10^9$ 个 η，统计量不足，限制了寻找新物理的灵敏度。

Method: REDTOP（Rare Eta Decays To Observe Physics Beyond the Standard Model）设施旨在收集 $\mathcal{O}(10^{14})$ 个 η 和 $\mathcal{O}(10^{12})$ 个 η′，通过四个“门户”（portal）：矢量（Vector，对应暗光子）、标量（Scalar，对应希格斯混合）、类轴子（Axion-like）和重轻子（Heavy Lepton），评估其对连接标准模型与新物理的耦合过程的灵敏度；同时利用高统计量进行对称性检验与形状因子测定。

Result: REDTOP 的高统计量使之能够通过四个新物理门户在广泛参数空间内搜索超出标准模型的现象；此外，还可高精度检验 CP（电荷共轭-宇称）和 T（时间反演）不变性以及轻子普适性（lepton universality），并改进 η/η′ 跃迁形状因子（transition form factors）的测定——后者是缪子反常磁矩 $(g-2)_μ$ 中强子光-光散射（hadronic light-by-light contribution）的关键输入。

Conclusion: REDTOP 装置有望在 η/η′ 稀有衰变领域实现比此前实验高约 5 个数量级的灵敏度，同时为 CP/T 不变量、轻子普适性及其对缪子 $(g-2)_μ$ 的间接贡献提供重要约束。

Abstract: The $η$ and $η^{\prime}$ mesons are nearly unique in the particle universe since they are nearly Goldstone bosons, and their decay dynamics are strongly constrained. While earlier experiments collected samples of order $\sim 10^{9}$ $η$, the proposed REDTOP (Rare Eta Decays To Observe Physics Beyond the Standard Model) facility targets $\mathcal{O}(10^{14})$ $η$ and $\mathcal{O}(10^{12})$ $η'$, enabling broad searches for physics beyond the Standard Model. In this work, we present studies evaluating REDTOP sensitivity to processes that couple the Standard Model to New Physics through four portals: the Vector (dark photon), the Scalar (Higgs-mixing), the Axion-like, and the Heavy Lepton. In parallel, the proposed statistics allow precise tests of $CP$ and $T$ invariance and lepton universality and improve determinations of the $η/η'$ transition form factors, which are crucial inputs to the hadronic light-by-light contribution to the muon anomalous magnetic moment $(g-2)_μ$.

</details>

### [142] [Mean-field limits for stochastic particle systems on dense graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11369)
*Angeliki Koutsimpela,Elena Magnanini*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了相互作用结构由收敛到图论（graphon）的稠密加权有向图描述的随机相互作用粒子系统。在热力学极限下，证明了经验测度过程的大数定律，并推导了描述宏观演化的确定性非线性主方程（master equation）。该极限方程通过极限图论保留了微观系统的异质相互作用结构，从而允许出现局部化或社区型等空间非均匀行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为具有异质相互作用结构的随机相互作用粒子系统建立宏观极限描述，填补微观网络结构与宏观聚合动力学之间的理论空白。

Method: 采用图论（graphon）作为稠密加权有向图的极限对象，在热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）下对经验测度过程（empirical measure process）进行大数定律（law of large numbers）分析。

Result: 推导出一个确定性的非线性主方程（master equation），该方程通过图论保留了微观系统的异质相互作用结构。

Conclusion: 该极限方程能描述局部化或社区型等空间非均匀行为，展现了微观拓扑结构对宏观动力学的持续影响。

Abstract: We study stochastic interacting particle systems whose interaction structure is described by dense weighted directed graphs converging to a graphon. In the thermodynamic limit, we prove a law of large numbers for the empirical measure process and derive a deterministic nonlinear master equation describing the macroscopic evolution. The limiting equation retains the heterogeneous interaction structure of the microscopic system through the limiting graphon, allowing for spatially non-homogeneous behaviors such as localized or community-type interactions.

</details>

# math.SG [[Back]](#toc)

### [143] [Quantum cohomology and split generation in Lagrangian Floer theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12257)
*M. Abouzaid,K. Fukaya,Y. -G. Oh,H. Ohta,K. Ono*

Main category: math.SG

TL;DR: 本文在紧辛流形（compact symplectic manifold）上给定一族拉格朗日子流形（Lagrangian submanifolds），构造了一个环形的、带滤过的、严格幺元的弯曲 $A_{\infty}$ 范畴（curved $A_{\infty}$ category），并发展了闭开映射和开闭映射的Floer理论。在此基础上证明：若量子上同调（quantum cohomology）到Fukaya范畴的Hochschild上同调（Hochschild cohomology）的映射为单射，则其他带弱边界上链（weak bounding cochain）的拉格朗日子流形必被原族分裂生成（split-generated），且Fukaya范畴的Hochschild同调（Hochschild homology）与上同调同构于量子上同调。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为一般紧辛流形上的Fukaya范畴（Fukaya category）建立闭开映射与开闭映射的Floer理论框架，并探究Fukaya范畴的代数不变量与辛流形量子上同调之间的深层联系，尤其是将已知在恰当情形（exact case）下的结果[Ab]推广至更一般的紧辛流形。

Method: 首先构造一个环形的、带滤过的、严格幺元的弯曲 $A_{\infty}$ 范畴 $\mathcal L$，其对象为给定的一族拉格朗日子流形 $\mathscr L$。然后发展该范畴上的闭开映射（closed-open map）和开闭映射（open-closed map）的Floer理论，利用这些映射分析Fukaya范畴的代数结构与量子上同调之间的关系。

Result: 证明了若从量子上同调到Fukaya范畴 $\mathcal L$ 的Hochschild上同调的映射为单射，则：(1) 任意其他带有弱边界上链的拉格朗日子流形均属于由 $\mathscr L$ 分裂生成的子范畴；(2) Fukaya范畴的Hochschild同调与上同调均同构于量子上同调。

Conclusion: 将Abouzaid在恰当情形下关于Fukaya范畴分裂生成与Hochschild（上）同构于量子上同调的结论推广到了紧辛流形的一般情形，并为相关应用提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Given a finite collection of Lagrangian submanifolds $\mathscr L$ in a compact symplectic manifold $X$, we construct a cyclic, filtered, strictly unital curved $A_{\infty}$ category $\mathcal L$ and develop Floer theory of closed-open maps and open-closed maps. Using them, we prove that, whenever the map from the quantum cohomology of $X$ to the Hochschild cohomology of the Fukaya category $\mathcal L$ with objects $\mathscr L$ is injective, the following consequences follow: (1) any other Lagrangian submanifold equipped with a weak bounding cochain lies in the category split-generated by $\mathscr L$, and (2) the Hochschild homology and cohomology of the Fukaya category are isomorphic to quantum cohomology. In the exact case a similar result was obtained in [Ab]. We also provide some applications.

</details>

### [144] [APTLAS: An Indexed APT Literature Repository](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11241)
*Bavley Guerguis,Nabil Bassim*

Main category: cs.DL

TL;DR: 本文介绍APTLAS，一个针对原子探针断层扫描（APT）领域文献的索引数据库与网页工具，收录约2300条记录并保留领域特定元数据（如分析模式、激光波长、仪器配置），以弥补通用搜索引擎在该专业领域检索中的不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原子探针断层扫描（APT）文献分散在众多期刊中，通用搜索引擎（如Google Scholar）虽然擅长广泛检索，但无法保留领域特定的元数据（domain-specific metadata），例如分析模式、激光波长或仪器配置等对判断APT文献相关性至关重要的信息，因此需要专门化的索引工具。

Method: 构建了APTLAS索引数据库，收录约2300条APT出版文献记录，每条记录附带从原文提取的元数据；并开发了配套网页工具（https://aptlas.bavleyguerguis.com/），支持用户按材料体系（material system）、仪器（instrument）、应用（application）、出版物类型（publication type）或关键词搜索进行浏览与筛选。

Result: 该数据库目前包含约2300条记录及对应的领域相关元数据，并已在网页端实现可交互的检索与筛选功能。

Conclusion: APTLAS为APT研究者提供了一个保留领域特定元数据的文献索引与检索平台，有望弥补通用搜索引擎在该专业领域的不足。

Abstract: Atom probe tomography (APT) literature is broad, rapidly growing, and dispersed across a wide range of journals, which can make it difficult to identify prior work on a given material system, instrument, or analytical approach. Conventional search engines (e.g., Google Scholar) excel at general retrieval but do not preserve the domain-specific metadata that often determines the relevance of an APT publication (e.g., analysis mode, laser wavelength, or instrument configuration). Herein, APTLAS is presented, which is an indexed repository of published APT literature. At present, the database contains ~2,300 records, each accompanied by metadata extracted from the source publication. The accompanying web tool, available at https://aptlas.bavleyguerguis.com/, allows users to browse and filter by material system, instrument, application, publication type, or keyword search.

</details>

### [145] [Generalizing Perron--Frobenius theory and eigenvector-based centralities to networks with complex edge weights](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12026)
*Yu Tian,Mason A. Porter,Lucas Böttcher*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本文将线性代数中的佩龙-弗罗贝尼乌斯定理（Perron-Frobenius theorem）推广到复值权重矩阵，提出适用于复边权网络的广义特征向量中心性测度（eigenvector-based centrality measures），并在量子信息、电路分析、数学化学等应用领域验证了其存在性与有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统佩龙-弗罗贝尼乌斯定理及其导出的特征向量中心性、PageRank 等测度仅适用于实值权重网络，但量子信息、电动力学、机器学习等领域的网络常具有复值边权（complex-valued edge weights），亟需相应的理论推广与中心性分析方法。

Method: 研究佩龙-弗罗贝尼乌斯定理到复值矩阵的推广形式，建立不同推广之间的联系，并基于这些推广提出适用于复边权网络的广义特征向量中心性测度。

Result: 证明了满足广义佩龙-弗罗贝尼乌斯性质的复加权网络的存在性，并在电子输运（electron transport）、电路分析（circuit analysis）、数学化学（mathematical chemistry）和通信网络（communication networks）等领域的实例中计算了相应的中心性测度。

Conclusion: 推广后的佩龙-弗罗贝尼乌斯定理及中心性测度可有效分析具有复值边权的网络节点重要性，拓展了传统网络分析方法的适用范围。

Abstract: A fundamental concept in linear algebra and its applications to network analysis is the Perron--Frobenius (PF) theorem, which underpins eigenvector-based centrality measures such as eigenvector centrality, PageRank, and hubs and authorities. By invoking the PF theorem, we know for strongly connected networks with positive edge weights that the eigenvector corresponding to the largest eigenvalue of the weight matrix yields a well-defined centrality measure (namely, eigenvector centrality). Traditional formulations of the PF theorem and associated centrality measures assume that networks have real-valued weights. However, many networks in areas such as quantum information, quantum chemistry, electrodynamics, and machine learning have complex-valued edge weights. In this paper, we study generalizations of the PF theorem to complex-valued matrices, establish connections between these generalizations, and propose generalized eigenvector-based centrality measures to analyzing node importances in networks with complex edge weights. We also prove results about the existence of complex-weighted networks that satisfy generalized PF properties and calculate associated centrality measures for several examples, which we draw from application areas such as electron transport, circuit analysis, mathematical chemistry, and communication networks.

### [146] [Pure Point Spectrum is Generic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12121)
*Artur Avila,David Damanik*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本文证明了在 $\ell^2(\mathbb{Z})$ 上，对于具有 $\ell^\infty(\mathbb{Z})$ 中有界实值势的薛定谔算子（Schrödinger operator），其通有谱型（generic spectral type）为纯点谱（pure point）；并且通有有界势对应的本质谱（essential spectrum）是康托尔集（Cantor set），且相对于所有谱测度（spectral measures）的权重为零。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究一维离散薛定谔算子（Schrödinger operator）的谱性质，特别是通有（generic）有界势能下谱型的分类问题，以理解随机或一般势场中局域化（localization）现象。

Method: 采用泛函分析和算子理论的方法，在 $\ell^2(\mathbb{Z})$ 上考虑具有 $\ell^\infty(\mathbb{Z})$ 中实值势的薛定谔算子，通过通有性（genericity）论证分析谱型及其测度性质。

Result: 通有有界势对应的谱型为纯点谱（pure point）；通有有界势的本质谱（essential spectrum）是康托尔集（Cantor set），并且该集合相对于所有谱测度（spectral measures）的测度为零。

Conclusion: 对于一维离散薛定谔算子，通有有界势的谱性质表现出高度奇异性：谱型为纯点谱，且本质谱为测度为零的康托尔集，揭示了通有势下谱结构的典型行为。

Abstract: We consider Schrödinger operators in $\ell^2(\mathbb{Z})$ with real-valued potentials in $\ell^\infty(\mathbb{Z})$ and show that the generic spectral type is pure point. More specifically, we show that for a generic bounded potential, the essential spectrum of the associated Schrödinger operator is a Cantor set and has zero weight with respect to all spectral measures.

</details>

### [147] [Exact Dynamics of Topological Order Across a CDW--SPT Transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11303)
*Pradip Kattel,Yicheng Tang,Natan Andrei*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究一维相互作用系统从电荷密度波（CDW）相到对称保护拓扑（SPT）相的非平衡动力学，发现突然淬火无法产生长程SPT序，而缓慢斜坡（ramp）则可通过基态绝热跟随和Kibble-Zurek缺陷形成机制建立拓扑序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究一维系统从CDW相到SPT相的非平衡动力学，特别是拓扑序在突然淬火（sudden quench）和缓慢斜坡（slow ramp）两种协议下能否形成及其机制差异。

Method: 通过幺正映射（unitary mapping）将相互作用系统转化为可解的二次费米子哈密顿量（quadratic fermionic Hamiltonian），进而精确计算Loschmidt回波、关联函数和弦关联子（string correlator）。

Result: 突然淬火后因有限密度的激发存在，长程SPT序无法建立；缓慢斜坡使系统在远离临界区域时跟随瞬时基态，SPT序的偏差由Kibble-Zurek缺陷产生机制控制。Loschmidt率函数出现尖点（cusps），表明发生动力学量子相变（dynamical quantum phase transitions）。

Conclusion: 进入拓扑相区域不足以保证拓扑序的出现，决定性因素是演化过程中对激发产生的抑制（suppression of excitation production）。

Abstract: We investigate the nonequilibrium dynamics of a one-dimensional interacting system across a transition from a charge-density-wave (CDW) phase to a symmetry-protected topological (SPT) phase. Starting from a CDW initial state, we study both sudden quenches and slow ramps into the SPT regime. While the CDW order melts under both protocols, the fate of topological order is sharply different. Following a sudden quench, long-range SPT order does not emerge because the post-quench state contains a finite density of excitations above the topological ground state. In contrast, slow ramps allow the system to follow the instantaneous ground state away from the critical region, enabling the buildup of SPT order with deviations governed by Kibble-Zurek defect production. The dynamics is solvable via a unitary mapping to a quadratic fermionic Hamiltonian, allowing us to compute the Loschmidt echo, correlation functions, and string correlator. The Loschmidt rate function exhibits cusps signaling dynamical quantum phase transitions, while the correlation dynamics reveal the contrasting mechanisms governing quenches and ramps across the transition. These results demonstrate that entering the topological regime is not sufficient for the emergence of topological order; the decisive factor is the suppression of excitation production during the evolution.

### [148] [Invariants of Sequential Circuits and Generalized Non-Abelian Statistics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11527)
*Shintaro Sato,Yoshimasa Hidaka,Ryohei Kobayashi*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了量子多体系统中由非可逆对称性（non-invertible symmetry）引发的顺序酉电路（sequential unitary circuits）所定义的不变量，证明该不变量在局域形变下具有不变性，并可用于探测非可逆对称性的't Hooft反常。作者将该框架应用于三维空间中的环激发（loop excitations），在(3+1)维 $\mathbb{D}_4$ 拓扑序中发现了一种新的非阿贝尔费米子环（non-Abelian fermionic loop），并表征了其统计性质，同时发现了一种由顺序电路不变量保护长程纠缠的新型混合拓扑序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非可逆对称性在量子多体系统中通常产生移动对称缺陷的顺序酉电路。作者旨在研究由这些电路序列定义的不变量，以理解非可逆缺陷的贝里相位（Berry phase），并探索该不变量在探测对称性反常和表征新型拓扑激发中的作用。

Method: 作者分析了移动非可逆缺陷的顺序酉电路序列所定义的贝里相位不变量，证明其在顺序电路保持局域形变的局域性条件下具有形变不变性。随后将该不变量框架应用于(3+1)维空间中的环激发，系统考察了 $\mathbb{D}_4$ 拓扑序中的激发结构。

Result: 该不变量排除了保持非可逆对称性的短程纠缠态，从而纯粹通过作用在态上的酉算子揭示了非可逆对称性的't Hooft反常。在(3+1)维 $\mathbb{D}_4$ 拓扑序中发现了一种新的环激发——非阿贝尔费米子环（non-Abelian fermionic loop），并利用顺序电路不变量表征了其统计性质。此外，还发现了一种仅含单个非阿贝尔费米子环的新型(3+1)维混合拓扑序，其长程纠缠受顺序电路不变量保护。

Conclusion: 顺序电路不变量为研究非可逆对称性及其反常提供了一种纯酉算子框架，并可推广至更高维度的拓扑激发分类与表征。该工作揭示了非可逆对称性在保护长程纠缠和定义新型拓扑序中的关键作用。

Abstract: Non-invertible symmetries in quantum many-body systems generally give rise to sequential unitary circuits that move symmetry defects. In this paper, we investigate invariants defined by sequences of such circuits, which move non-invertible defects and generate a Berry phase evaluated on quantum states with defects. We show that this Berry phase generally defines an invariant under local deformations, provided that the sequential circuits preserve the locality of those deformations. This invariant also rules out a short-range-entangled state that preserves the non-invertible symmetry, thereby signaling the 't Hooft anomaly of a non-invertible symmetry purely in terms of unitary operators acting on a state. We then apply this framework to loop excitations in three spatial dimensions and identify a new loop excitation in the (3+1)D $\mathbb{D}_4$ topological order, which we dub a non-Abelian fermionic loop. Using the invariant of sequential circuits, we characterize the statistics of non-Abelian fermionic loops. In addition, we find a new (3+1)D mixed topological order with a single non-Abelian fermionic loop, whose long-range entanglement is protected by an invariant of sequential circuits.

</details>


### [149] [The Kondo effect in ferromagnetic quantum critical CeRh$_6$Ge$_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11978)
*Martin Sundermann,Joe D. Thompson,Eric D. Bauer,Chun Fu Chang,Sheng-Huai Chen,Chang-Yang Kuo,Liu Hao Tjeng,Getrud Zwicknagl,Andrea Severing*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本论文通过光电子能谱和X射线吸收谱研究了重费米子铁磁体CeRh₆Ge₄中4f电子的电子结构，发现其呈现多轨道基态和轨道依赖的近藤效应（orbital-dependent Kondo effect），为理解压力诱导的量子临界点（quantum critical point）提供了关键微观图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CeRh₆Ge₄在压力下呈现量子临界点，但清洁巡游Ce化合物中通常规避铁磁量子临界性（ferromagnetic quantum criticality），其机制尚不明确。4f电子的局域与巡游特性被认为是理解该行为的关键，但缺乏直接的电子结构实验证据。

Method: 采用核心能级光电子能谱（core-level photoelectron spectroscopy）和X射线吸收谱（X-ray absorption spectroscopy）测量CeRh₆Ge₄中4f壳层的电子结构。利用线性偏振X射线吸收谱观测温度依赖的线性二色性（linear dichroism），并结合单杂质安德森模型在非交叉近似下（single-impurity Anderson model in the non crossing approximation, SIAM/NCA）的理论计算进行对比分析。

Result: 实验观测到的线性二色性与静态磁化率推断的晶场（crystal-electric-field, CEF）序列一致，但无法仅用离子全多重态模型（ionic full-multiplet model）描述。引入近藤效应（Kondo effect）后，SIAM/NCA模型成功重现了观测的二色性。近藤效应将更高晶场态混合到多轨道基态中，4f占据数n_f ∼ 0.9。低温下实验与计算二色性出现偏差，提示存在轨道依赖的近藤效应。

Conclusion: CeRh₆Ge₄中4f电子呈现多轨道基态和轨道依赖的近藤杂化（orbital-dependent Kondo hybridization），这一图像应作为构建该材料压力诱导量子临界性模型的出发点。

Abstract: The mechanism of a pressure-induced quantum critical point in the heavy fermion ferromagnet CeRh$_6$Ge$_4$ has attracted interest, as ferromagnetic quantum criticality in a clean itinerant Ce compound is typically avoided. The localized versus itinerant character of the 4\textit{f} electrons is a key aspect for understanding this behavior. We investigated the electronic structure of the 4\textit{f} shell in CeRh$_6$Ge$_4$ using core-level photoelectron and x-ray absorption spectroscopy, demonstrating the hybridization of Ce 4\textit{f} with the conduction electrons. Linearly polarized x-ray absorption reveals a temperature-dependent linear dichroism consistent with the crystal-electric-field (CEF) sequence as inferred from the static susceptibility. This dichroism cannot be described by an ionic full-multiplet model alone, but is reproduced by including the Kondo effect within a single-impurity Anderson model in the non crossing approximation (SIAM/NCA). The Kondo effect mixes higher lying crystal-field states into a resulting multiorbital ground state with 4\textit{f} occupancy \textit{n}$_f$\,$\sim$\,0.9. Deviations at low temperatures between the measured linear dichroism and calculated dichroism suggest an orbital-dependent Kondo effect. A scenario in which there is a multiorbital ground state and orbital-dependent Kondo hybridization should be a starting point for a model of pressure-induced criticality in CeRh$_6$Ge$_4$.

</details>


### [150] [Phonons and magnetism of kagome FeGe probed by nuclear resonant scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12038)
*Yu Tang,Saizheng Cao,Sijie Xu,Xiaokun Teng,Sven Velten,Ilya Sergeev,Pengcheng Dai,Yilin Wang,Yu Song*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用$^{57}$Fe核共振散射（nuclear resonant scattering, NRS）技术，结合第一性原理计算（first-principle calculation），测量Fe原子局域的声子态密度（partial phonon density of states）和超精细相互作用（hyperfine interaction）参数。

Result: 进入CDW态后，Fe局域声子态密度中声学声子和约22、27、31 meV的光学声子出现硬化，与第一性原理计算定性一致；进入非公度磁相后，声子态密度和超精细相互作用参数未发生显著变化，但时域Mössbauer谱中检测到与非公度磁序或慢涨落相关的细微特征。

Conclusion: Kagome FeGe中的CDW显著改变了其晶格动力学和磁性，表明自旋、电荷与晶格自由度之间存在相互交织（intertwined）的耦合关系。

Abstract: Kagome FeGe hosts a $2\times2\times2$ charge-density wave (CDW) that strongly interplays with antiferromagnetic order. Here, we report $^{57}$Fe nuclear resonant scattering measurement to study FeGe across its long-range CDW and incommensurate magnetic transitions. Upon entering the CDW state, hardening of acoustic phonons and optical phonons around 22~meV, 27~meV, and 31~meV are observed in the Fe partial phonon density of states, which can be qualitatively captured by first-principle calculations. Upon entering the incommensurate magnetic phase, neither the phonon density of states nor the hyperfine interaction parameters change significantly, although a subtle feature associated with the incommensurate magnetic order or slow fluctuations is detected in the time-domain Mössbauer spectra. These findings show that the CDW in kagome FeGe significantly modifies its lattice dynamics and magnetism, evidencing an intertwined nature of the spin, charge, and lattice degrees of freedom.
