### [151] [From Topological Order to Mixed-State Phases: A Ground-State Probe of Fractionalized Excitations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12132)
*Yunlong Zang,Yu-Bin Li,Shenghan Jiang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出通过单个基态（ground state）的约化密度矩阵（RDM）来检测二维拓扑序（topological order），将RDM视为一维混合态相，并引入强到弱自发对称性破缺（SW-SSB）框架，揭示任意子退禁闭和对称性分数化（symmetry fractionalization）的可观测特征，适用于量子模拟平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法依赖纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）和纠缠谱（entanglement spectrum）检测拓扑相，但约化密度矩阵本身包含更丰富的信息。本文旨在探索如何仅从单个基态的RDM中提取拓扑相的标志性特征。

Method: 将二维拓扑有序系统的RDM在纠缠切割（entanglement cut）处解释为一维混合态相；对于$\mathbb{Z}_2$ toric code相，该一维相表现出$\mathbb{Z}_2$强到弱自发对称性破缺（SW-SSB），其中任意子退禁闭（deconfinement of anyons）体现为RDM中$\mathbb{Z}_2$电荷和$\mathbb{Z}_2$畴壁的短程关联；体$e$-$m$对偶性转化为SW-SSB相的Kramers–Wannier自对偶性；推广至有能隙的$\mathbb{Z}_2$自旋液体，全局自旋旋转对称性成为一维RDM的附加弱对称性，自旋-$\frac12$自旋子（spinon）在自旋旋转的无序参数（disorder parameter）$\theta=\pi$处产生尖点（cusp）。理论分析采用矩阵乘积密度算符（matrix product density operator）形式，数值验证在kagome晶格共振价键（RVB）态上进行。

Result: 对于$\mathbb{Z}_2$ toric code相，RDM对应的一维SW-SSB相验证了任意子退禁闭与短程关联的对应关系。对于有能隙的$\mathbb{Z}_2$自旋液体，自旋旋转无序参数在$\theta=\pi$处的尖点提供了对称性分数化的直接基态特征，该预测通过解析分析和kagome晶格RVB态的数值计算得到验证。

Conclusion: 所提出的可观测量仅需单个基态波函数（single ground-state wavefunction），适用于量子模拟平台（quantum simulation platforms），为探测拓扑相提供了一种不依赖纠缠谱的全新途径。

Abstract: How do we detect topological phases from a single ground state? Entanglement entropy and spectrum have long been the standard tools -- but the reduced density matrix (RDM) itself contains far more information. We show that the RDM of a 2D topologically ordered system, expressed at the entanglement cut, realizes a 1D mixed-state phase. For the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ toric code phase, it is a 1D $\mathbb{Z}_2$ strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking (SW-SSB) phase, where deconfinement of anyons manifests as the short-range correlation of both $\mathbb{Z}_2$ charge and $\mathbb{Z}_2$ domain-wall in the RDM. The bulk $e$-$m$ duality translates into a Kramers--Wannier self-duality of the SW-SSB phase. Extending the framework to gapped $\mathbb{Z}_2$ spin liquids, the global spin-rotation symmetry manifests as an additional weak symmetry for the 1D RDM. Spin-$\frac{1}{2}$ spinons result in a cusp on the disorder parameter of spin-rotation at $θ=π$, providing a direct, ground-state signature of symmetry fractionalization. We verify this prediction analytically using the matrix product density operator formalism and numerically for the kagome-lattice resonating valence bond state. The proposed observable requires only a single ground-state wavefunction, making it amenable to quantum simulation platforms.

</details>


### [152] [Kinetic kagome magnetism: from self-trapping RVB polarons to semiclassical correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12204)
*Yufei Pei,Shuai A. Chen,Claudio Castelnovo,Roderich Moessner*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过研究kagome晶格上的单空穴反Nagaoka问题，发现在近完全极化态下掺杂空穴通过束缚自旋反转形成共振价键（RVB）极化子而退局域化；随着自旋极化降低，这些态演化为√3×√3反铁磁关联，为理解RVB物理与常规磁关联之间的跨尺度演化提供了框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在深入理解空穴动力学（hole kinetics）在高度阻挫掺杂Mott绝缘体（doped Mott insulators）中决定磁性质的作用，特别关注从完全极化到非极化极限下自旋与空穴行为的转变机制。

Method: 以kagome晶格上的单空穴反Nagaoka问题（single-hole counter-Nagaoka problem）为模型，将磁化强度（magnetization）作为可调参数，系统研究不同自旋极化程度下掺杂空穴的局域化与退局域化行为。

Result: 近完全极化下，掺杂空穴通过束缚反转自旋形成共振价键（resonating-valence-bond, RVB）极化子（RVB polaron）而退局域化；这些RVB极化子有效带宽极小，表现出自陷（self-trapping）现象。随着自旋极化降低，系统演化至非极化区域时出现√3×√3反铁磁关联（antiferromagnetic correlation），该关联让人联想到kagome晶格上的经典Potts模型和Heisenberg模型。

Conclusion: 上述结果为理解RVB物理如何在短尺度上演化为常规磁关联在长尺度上的行为提供了理论框架。

Abstract: To gain deeper insight into the role of hole kinetics in determining magnetism in highly frustrated doped Mott insulators, we consider the single-hole counter-Nagaoka problem on the kagome lattice, using magnetization as a tuning parameter. Near full polarization, a doped hole delocalizes upon binding reversed spins in a pattern of singlet bonds which we term resonating-valence-bond (RVB) polaron. These RVB polarons can have extremely small effective bandwidths, and hence exhibit self-trapping. By tuning the spin polarization, we track the evolution of these states toward the unpolarized sector, where we observe the emergence of $\sqrt{3}\times\sqrt{3}$ antiferromagnetic correlation reminiscent of the classical Potts and Heisenberg models on the kagome lattice. These results provide a framework to understand how RVB physics at short scales evolves into conventional magnetic correlations at long scales.

</details>


### [153] [Structural responses incipient to pressure-driven antiferromagnetic quantum critical point of van der Waals heavy-fermion metal CeSiI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12222)
*Hanming Ma,Tong Shi,Wenhao Li,Qingxin Dong,Xiaoli Ma,Shaoheng Ruan,Zhongjin Wu,Pengtao Yang,Zhaoming Tian,Jianping Sun,Yoshiya Uwatoko,Xiaohui Yu,Hechang Lei,Bosen Wang,Jinguang Cheng*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究通过室温高压单晶X射线衍射实验，揭示了CeSiI在压力驱动的反铁磁量子临界点（QCP）附近（约6 GPa）存在各向异性的晶格异常响应，包括a轴收缩与c轴突增，且这些结构变化源于Ce-Ce、Ce-Si键长改变以及内层蜂窝状Si层的扁平化，建立了低温电子量子临界转变与室温结构响应之间的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期发现CeSiI是一种范德华重费米子金属（van der Waals heavy-fermion metal），在压力诱导的反铁磁量子临界点（antiferromagnetic quantum critical point, QCP）附近表现出非常规超导电性，但其微观结构响应机制尚不明确。本研究旨在探究CeSiI在高压下、特别是在QCP附近是否存在结构层面的前兆性变化。

Method: 作者在室温条件下对CeSiI单晶进行了高压单晶X射线衍射（single-crystal X-ray diffraction）实验，压力范围覆盖至8.3 GPa，系统测量了晶格参数和原子位置的压强依赖性。

Result: 在研究的整个压力范围内未观察到结构相变，晶胞体积随压力平滑减小。然而，在约6 GPa（即QCP位置）附近，晶格参数出现了突变且各向异性的响应：a轴突然收缩，c轴突然伸长；同时，Ce-Ce与Ce-Si键长变化以及内层蜂窝状Si层发生扁平化是导致上述晶格异常的主要微观结构因素。

Conclusion: 该发现建立了低温QCP附近压力驱动电子跃迁与室温下前兆性结构响应之间的有趣关联，为理解CeSiI的压力-温度相图提供了新的视角。

Abstract: CeSiI is a van der Waals heavy-fermion metal recently found to exhibit unconventional superconductivity near a pressure-induced antiferromagnetic quantum critical point (QCP) at Pc =6 GPa. Here, we report a comprehensive single-crystal X-ray diffraction study of CeSiI under high pressures up to 8.3 GPa at room temperature, revealing subtle structural responses that precede pressure-driven QCP. We find that the unit-cell volume decreases smoothly upon compression without showing any structural phase transition in the investigated pressure range. Intriguingly, we observe abrupt and concurrent anisotropic responses of the lattice parameters around Pc =6 GPa, i.e., the a-axis contracts while the c-axis enlongated suddenly, with the unit-cell volume smoothily varies with pressure. Structural refinements further show that these lattice anomalies primarily originate from changes of Ce-Ce and Ce-Si bond lengths, as well as a flattening of the inner honeycomb Si layer within the CeSiI monolayer around Pc. Our findings establish an interesting case linking pressure-driven electronic transition of QCP at low temperatures to incipient structural responses at room temperature, thereby providing fresh insight into the pressure-temperature phase diagram of CeSiI.

</details>

### [154] [Isotropic random walks and Brownian diffusion on complex projective space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11438)
*Gyula I. Tóth*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在复射影空间（complex projective space）上构建了各向同性随机游走（isotropic random walks）的随机几何框架，用于探索量子态空间。该框架结合紧致秩一对称空间上的调和分析与随机纯态演化，导出了转移核、保真度统计量和Fubini–Study度规下几何观测量的显式解析表达式，从而为各向同性退极化（isotropic depolarization）和Haar均衡化（Haar equilibration）提供了可解参考模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为量子态空间的随机探索提供一个正则化且解析可处理的随机几何框架，以替代传统上需要指定微观Lindblad生成元（Lindblad generator）的方法，并统一描述各向同性退极化过程和Haar均衡化行为。

Method: 采用紧致秩一对称空间上的调和分析（harmonic analysis）与随机纯态演化（stochastic pure-state evolution）相结合的方法，在复射影空间上构造各向同性随机游走，并由此导出转移核、保真度统计量和Fubini–Study度规下几何观测量的解析表达式。

Result: 在短时间极限下，随机演化收敛为由Fubini–Study Laplace–Beltrami算子生成的布朗扩散（Brownian diffusion）；长时间极限下展现出高维随机量子态特有的测度集中行为（concentration-of-measure）。进一步导出了首达时间问题（first-passage-time problem）的解析结果，包括布朗极限下平均首达时间（mean first passage time）的闭式表达式和首达时间分布的长时间尾部行为。高保真度目标态的平均首达时间表现出强烈的维度依赖发散，源于Fubini–Study几何的集中性质。

Conclusion: 所提出的框架为一个无需指定微观Lindblad生成元即可重现Haar随机保真度统计量和射影Hilbert空间上不变测度的可解参考模型，兼具短时布朗扩散与长时测度集中的渐近行为，并为量子态空间中的首达时间问题提供了解析结果。

Abstract: We show that isotropic random walks on the complex projective space provide a canonical and analytically tractable stochastic-geometric framework for the exploration of quantum-state space. The approach combines harmonic analysis on compact rank-one symmetric spaces with stochastic pure-state evolution and yields explicit analytical expressions for transition kernels, fidelity statistics, and geometric observables associated with the Fubini--Study metric. In particular, the framework provides a solvable reference model for isotropic depolarization and Haar equilibration, reproducing Haar-random fidelity statistics and the invariant measure on projective Hilbert space without specifying a microscopic Lindblad generator. In the short-time regime, the stochastic evolution converges to Brownian diffusion generated by the Fubini--Study Laplace--Beltrami operator, while the long-time limit exhibits concentration-of-measure behaviour characteristic of high-dimensional random quantum states. We further derive analytical and asymptotic results for the first-passage-time problem, including closed-form expressions in the Brownian limit for the mean first passage time and the long-time tail of the first-passage-time distribution. For high-fidelity target states, the mean first passage time exhibits a strong dimension-dependent divergence originating from the concentration properties of the Fubini--Study geometry.

### [155] [Exact Entanglement Dynamics Beyond Nearest-Neighbor Dual-Unitary Floquet Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11311)
*Tanay Pathak*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过在交错子格上引入对偶幺正性（dual-unitarity），构建了一类可解析求解的有限程踢伊辛模型（finite-range kicked Ising models），并推导出所有 n-雷尼熵（n-Rényi entanglement entropies）的精确封闭表达式。该框架自然推广至更大相互作用程及异质局域希尔伯特空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对偶幺正性（dual-unitarity）的精确结果主要局限于最近邻（nearest-neighbor）结构，而有限程相互作用（finite-range interactions）通常带来复杂性。作者希望超越最近邻限制，构建一个可解析求解的有限程模型，用以精确研究纠缠动力学。

Method: 提出一种交错（staggered）结构，在子格内部保持对偶幺正性（dual-unitarity），再将这些子格相互耦合。关键观察是，子格间的耦合并未破坏整体模型的对偶幺正性。对于最小相互作用程 r=2，推导出所有 n-雷尼纠缠熵（n-Rényi entanglement entropies）的精确表达式。

Result: 对于 r=2 的模型，所有时刻的 n-雷尼纠缠熵可精确表达为两个耦合子格贡献之和。该框架可自然地推广至更大相互作用程及异质局域希尔伯特空间（heterogeneous local Hilbert spaces），无需额外假设。

Conclusion: 该工作为严格最近邻对偶幺正模型之外的可控精确纠缠增长研究提供了一个解析框架，填补了有限程相互作用下精确纠缠动力学的空白。

Abstract: Exact results using dual-unitarity largely rely on nearest-neighbor structures, while finite-range interactions typically lead to complications. Going beyond the usual nearest-neighbor setting, we introduce an analytically tractable family of finite-range kicked Ising models that admit exact closed-form entanglement dynamics. The construction is based on a staggered structure in which dual-unitarity is present on sublattices that are then coupled to each other. The central observation is that these inter-sublattice couplings do not obstruct the dual-unitarity of the resulting model. For the minimal interaction range of $r= 2$, we derive exact expressions for all the $n-$Rényi entanglement entropies at all times and show that the result is the sum of the two coupled sublattice contributions. Our framework extends naturally to larger finite interaction ranges and to systems with heterogeneous local Hilbert spaces, without additional assumptions. It thus provides a controlled setting for studying exact entanglement growth beyond strictly nearest-neighbor dual-unitary models.

</details>


### [156] [Bound State Solutions of the Relativistic Finite-difference Equation for the Ring-shaped Quesne Oscillator Potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12082)
*Sh. M. Nagiyev,Narmin Nasibova,V. A. Tarverdiyeva,G. H. Guliyeva*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文精确求解了量子三维环形Quesne振荡子势的相对论有限差分方程，基于相对论量子力学的有限差分版本，利用连续对偶Hahn多项式和Jacobi多项式表示径向和角向波函数，得到了离散能谱并建立了SU(1,1)动力学对称群。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对相对论框架下环形Quesne振荡子势的精确解仍不充分，特别是基于有限差分方法（finite-difference method）的相对论量子力学处理尚待完善。作者旨在通过这一非标准方法获得该势场的精确解，并揭示其代数结构。

Method: 采用相对论有限差分方程（relativistic finite-difference equation）描述三维环形Quesne振荡子势，并利用相对论构型r空间（relativistic configurational r-space）概念进行求解。通过连续对偶Hahn多项式（continuous dual Hahn polynomials）和Jacobi多项式（Jacobi polynomials）分别表达径向波函数和角向波函数，并构造了径向运动方程的SU(1,1)动力学对称群。

Result: 获得了该势场下量子系统的精确解，径向波函数和角向波函数分别由连续对偶Hahn多项式和Jacobi多项式给出；得到了离散能谱（discrete energy spectrum），并验证了径向波函数和能谱的正确非相对论极限（nonrelativistic limit）。

Conclusion: 通过建立SU(1,1)动力学对称群，实现了对径向部分运动方程的纯代数求解（algebraic solution），从而完整解析地描述了该相对论量子系统。这一工作展示了有限差分相对论量子力学在处理复杂势场时的有效性。

Abstract: We solve exactly the relativistic finite-difference equation for the quantum three-dimensional ring-shaped Quesne oscillator potential. Our investigation is based on a finite-difference version of relativistic quantum mechanics. So-called relativistic configurational r-space is a key concept here. We show that the radial wavefunctions and angular wavefunctions are expressed through the continuous dual Hahn polynomials and Jacobi polynomials, respectively. A discrete energy spectrum has been found. The radial wave functions and energy spectrum have the correct nonrelativistic limit. We also build a dynamical symmetry group SU (1, 1) for the radial part of the equation of motion, which allows us to find the energy spectrum purely algebraically.

### [157] [Quantum ergodicity and semiclassical measures: mathematical results](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12098)
*Stéphane Nonnenmacher*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本章综述了紧致流形或欧几里得区域上拉普拉斯算子高频本征模（eigenmodes）的宏观分布，聚焦于半经典测度（semiclassical measure）概念，详细证明了量子遍历定理（Quantum Ergodicity theorem），并讨论了量子唯一遍历猜想（Quantum Unique Ergodicity conjecture）及其在混沌系统（Anosov系统）中的进展，包括对半经典测度的柯尔莫戈洛夫-辛奈熵（Kolmogorov-Sinai entropy）约束与离域化结果。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用半经典测度作为描述本征模宏观分布的工具；详细给出量子遍历定理的完整证明，并针对带边界流形的情况进行必要调整；同时利用柯尔莫戈洛夫-辛奈熵对允许的半经典测度施加约束。

Result: 提供了量子遍历定理的详细证明（含边界情况的调整）；给出了对强混沌（Anosov）系统中量子唯一遍历猜想的最新进展，包括半经典测度的熵约束条件及离域化结果。

Conclusion: 量子遍历定理已获严格证明并在带边界情形下适用；量子唯一遍历猜想在Anosov系统中取得重要进展，半经典测度受到熵约束，且存在更近期的离域化结果。

Abstract: In this chapter we review some results describing the high-frequency eigenmodes of the Laplacian on compact manifolds, or Euclidean domains, for which the geodesic flow is chaotic. We focus on the macroscopic distribution of these eigenmodes, which is described by the concept of semiclassical measure. The main result on the question is the Quantum Ergodicity theorem, originally due to Schnirelman. We provide the detailed proof of this theorem, including the adjustments necessary to treat the case of manifolds with boundary. We also discuss the Quantum Unique Ergodicity conjecture, and some progress towards this conjecture for strongly chaotic (Anosov) systems. In particular, we describe the constraints on admissible semiclassical measures, in terms of their Kolmogorov-Sinai entropy, as well as more recent delocalization results.

</details>


### [158] [Mach's principle in atomic transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11608)
*Subhajit Barman,Bibhas Ranjan Majhi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 研究了原子-镜面体系中原子处于圆周运动（circular motion）时的跃迁概率（transition probabilities）：在静态圆柱镜面内原子做圆周运动，以及圆柱镜面绕轴旋转而原子静止两种情形下，发现两者的跃迁概率结构相似，只需交换场频率（field frequencies）即可等价，并将其解释为类似于经典马赫原理（Mach's principle）的半经典现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨原子-镜面（atom-mirror）设置中圆周运动对原子跃迁概率的影响，并对比原子运动与镜面旋转两种相对运动情形是否具有物理上的对称性或等价性。

Method: 比较两种情景下的原子跃迁概率：情景一为原子在静态圆柱镜面（cylindrical mirror）内做圆周运动，情景二为圆柱镜面绕中心轴旋转而原子保持静止。

Result: 两种情形的原子跃迁概率在交换两场景的场频率后完全等价，表现出结构相似性（structural similarity）。

Conclusion: 将观测到的跃迁概率等价性解释为一种半经典（semi-classical）现象，与经典的马赫原理存在类比关系。

Abstract: We investigate the atomic transition probabilities in atom-mirror set-ups that are in circular motion. In one scenario, the atom is in circular motion inside a static cylindrical mirror. In the other scenario, the cylindrical mirror rotates around its central axis while the atom remains static. We report structural similarity in the atomic transition probabilities between these two cases -- these probabilities are equivalent upon interchanging the field frequencies between the two scenarios. We interpret such an observation as a semi-classical phenomenon analogous to the classical Mach's principle.

</details>


### [159] [Scaling law of asymptotic freedom in collective charging of quantum batteries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10054)
*Gentaro Watanabe,Chunlin Chen,B. Prasanna Venkatesh*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立了量子电池（quantum batteries）集体充电过程中的普适标度律（universal scaling law），证明提功比（ergotropy-to-energy ratio）随电池数量 $N$ 以至少 $\sim N^{-1}$ 的速度趋近于 1，并进一步揭示了可通过纯态实现更快收敛（包括指数级加速），同时给出了有限 $N$ 下的严格上下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子电池集体充电过程中是否存在不依赖微观细节的普适行为，并分析提功比趋于完全提取的收敛速率及其极限。

Method: 通过理论证明建立普适标度律，推导提功比相较于电池数 $N$ 的渐近下界（$\sim N^{-1}$），并针对渐近纯态情形分析了超越 $1/N$ 标度的加速机制（如 $N^{-b}$ 乃至 $N^2$ 指数衰减）；同时推导了有限 $N$ 下的严格上下界。

Result: 提功比趋近 1 的速率至少为 $\sim N^{-1}$，具有普适性且与微观细节无关；在电池状态渐近纯化时，收敛速度可显著提升，包括 $b>1$ 的幂律标度乃至 $N^2$ 下的指数标度；获得了有限 $N$ 下的严格上下界，为非渐近情形提供了 $1/N$ 标度的理论保证。

Conclusion: 量子电池集体充电存在普适的 $1/N$ 标度律，且通过纯态设计可突破此极限实现更快的能量提取收敛，这一结果对量子电池（quantum batteries）的实际性能优化具有指导意义。

Abstract: We establish a universal scaling law for collective charging of quantum batteries, independent of microscopic details. We prove that the ergotropy-to-energy ratio approaches unity at least as fast as $\sim N^{-1}$ with the number of batteries $N$, implying generic asymptotic freedom. We further show how the universal $1/N$ scaling can be overcome: when the battery state becomes asymptotically pure, the convergence can be substantially faster, including $\sim N^{-b}$ with $b>1$ and even exponential scaling in $N^2$. Rigorous finite-$N$ upper and lower bounds on the ergotropy-to-energy ratio are further derived, providing nonasymptotic guarantees for the universal $1/N$ scaling.

</details>


### [160] [Observable signatures of exceptional points from left-right eigenstate distinction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11333)
*Leela Ganesh Chandra Lakkaraju,Soumik Bandyopadhyay,Sudipto Singha Roy,Philipp Hauke*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文基于非厄米XY自旋链模型，提出通过左右本征态差异构造全局量及局域可观测量的方法，用于探测多体非厄米系统中的奇异点（exceptional points），并在RT与PT对称区域分别展示了时间平均纠缠熵差值的不同标度行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非厄米量子系统（non-Hermitian quantum systems）中奇异点（exceptional points）在量子传感、单向输运和鲁棒激光等领域具有重要应用，因此需要通过多体系统的可观测量来识别奇异点。

Method: 以一维复XY自旋链为模型，该模型同时实现旋转时间（RT）和宇称时间（PT）对称区域。利用非厄米哈密顿量中左右本征向量不再互为伴随矢量的特性，构建哈密顿量与其伴随算子之间的全局差异量来定位奇异点；同时在可观测层面，计算左右本征态上的局域自旋关联（local spin correlations）差异，以及时间平均的左右纠缠熵差值（right-left entanglement entropy difference）。

Result: 全局量在奇异点处表现出非解析行为；局域自旋关联差异可作为静态探测方案可靠识别奇异点，而静态二分纠缠测量则无法捕捉该差异。在RT对称区域，时间平均左右纠缠熵差值在奇异点处呈现显著峰值；在PT对称区域，该差值表现为序参量（order-parameter-like），在一个相位中有限而在相变处消失。

Conclusion: 结果建立了非厄米本征态结构与奇异点可观测特征之间的直接联系，为在现有量子模拟器中识别奇异点提供了实用途径。

Abstract: Non-Hermitian quantum systems exhibit qualitatively distinct physical behavior compared to Hermitian systems, a prime example being spectral singularities known as exceptional points. Their relevance in, e.g., quantum sensing, unidirectional transport, and robust lasing makes it important to be able to identify exceptional points through observable features of a many-body system. Here, using as an example a one-dimensional complex XY spin chain realizing both rotation-time RT- and parity-time PT-symmetric regimes, we develop a framework for detecting exceptional points based on the distinction between left and right eigenvectors of the Hamiltonian, which in a non-Hermitian system are no longer the adjoint of each other. We first show that a global measure constructed from the difference between the Hamiltonian and its adjoint locates exceptional points via distinct non-analytic behavior. At the level of observables, differences in local spin correlations evaluated on the right and left eigenstates provide a reliable static detection scheme. In contrast, static bipartite entanglement measures fail to capture this distinction, urging us to study the quantum dynamics of the model. Following a sudden quench, we demonstrate that the time-averaged right-left entanglement entropy difference directly encodes signatures of the exceptional point. In the RT-symmetric regime, it exhibits a pronounced peak at the exceptional point, whereas in the PT-symmetric regime it behaves as an order-parameter-like quantity, remaining finite in one phase and vanishing at the transition. Our results establish a direct link between the structure of non-Hermitian eigenstates and observable signatures of exceptional points, providing a practical route to identify them in existing quantum simulators.

</details>


### [161] [Handbook of Error-Correcting Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11484)
*Victor V. Albert,Philippe Faist*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文以手册形式呈现了《纠错动物园》（The Error Correction Zoo），这是一个关于保护经典或量子信息免受存储与传输错误的纠错码（error-correcting codes）的策展式参考集，包含代码描述、符号分类、代码间关系及其与球堆积（sphere packings）、格点（lattices）、设计（designs）、群（groups）以及经典与量子物相（phases of matter）等对象的关联编目。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纠错技术（error correction）是条码扫描、清晰通话、可靠数据存储、卫星通信和大规模量子计算等广泛应用的基础，然而现有的纠错码知识分散庞杂，需要系统化的整理和分类以方便查阅与发现新联系。

Method: 采用策展式（curated）参考方法，以手册形式组织纠错码信息，提供描述性条目，按照符号类型（symbols）进行分类，并编目代码之间以及与球堆积、格点、设计、群和物相等数学与物理对象之间的关联。

Result: 生成了《纠错动物园》的手册版本，涵盖经典纠错码与量子纠错码（quantum error-correcting codes）的描述、按符号的分类体系，以及代码间关系与跨领域对象关联的全面编目。

Conclusion: 该手册既可作为严谨的学术参考，也可作为追踪代码关系网络和发现新联系的实用工具，旨在弥合纠错码领域内外的知识连接。

Abstract: Barcode scans, clear phone calls, reliable data storage, satellite communication, and large-scale quantum computation are all made possible by error correction. We present a handbook version of The Error Correction Zoo, a curated reference of methods for protecting classical or quantum information from errors during storage and transmission. The handbook includes descriptions of these error-correcting codes and a classification according to the symbols they use. It also catalogues relations among codes and related objects such as sphere packings, lattices, designs, groups, and classical and quantum phases of matter. The collection is intended both as a rigorous reference and as a practical aid for tracing the web of code relationships and uncovering new connections.

</details>


### [162] [A Cryogenic Uniaxial Strain Cell for Quantum Devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11485)
*Bradley Lloyd,Davis Rash,Chandler Wilburn,Paul Kliewer,Meenakshi Singh*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出并验证了一种专为厚、方截面半导体量子器件芯片设计的压电单轴应变装置（piezoelectric uniaxial strain cell），通过对称双芯片加载构型（dual-chip loading configuration）和集成RF/DC转接器（interposer），在保持电隔离的同时实现了均匀应变调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有压电应变单元（piezoelectric strain cells）通常针对易碎、高长宽比的单晶样品优化，不适用于半导体量子器件常用的厚、方截面芯片；同时，将其适配到量子比特（qubit）系统需要容纳密集的射频（RF）和直流（DC）布线，并与高压压电致动器（piezo actuators）保持严格电隔离。

Method: 提出一种高对称性的双芯片加载构型以抑制弯曲变形（flexural deformation）和剪切应力（shear stress）；集成高密度RF/DC转接器以支持标准引线键合（wire bonding）；将致动器封装在接地的法拉第笼（Faraday cage）内以防止器件层产生不应有的斯塔克位移（Stark shift）；采用有限元模拟（finite element simulation）验证设计。

Result: 有限元模拟表明，结合刚性致动器（stiff actuators）与对称安装可显著提升应变均匀性（strain homogeneity）。实验验证中，对200 μm厚的硅芯片施加单轴应变，在200 V压电偏压下测得215 με的表面应变。

Conclusion: 该应变装置能够对厚方截面半导体衬底施加均匀单轴应变，并兼容高频布线要求，为量子器件的应变量子调控（strain tuning）提供了一种可行的实验平台。

Abstract: Mechanical strain is a powerful resource for tuning quantum systems, but existing piezoelectric strain cells are generally optimized for fragile, high-aspect-ratio single crystals rather than the thick, square-profile chips typical of semiconductor quantum devices. Furthermore, adapting these cells for qubits requires accommodating dense RF and DC wiring while maintaining strict electrical isolation from high-voltage piezo actuators. Here, we present a piezoelectric uniaxial strain cell designed to homogeneously strain thick, square-profile substrates. We introduce a highly symmetric dual-chip loading configuration that effectively suppresses flexural deformation and shear stress. The cell integrates a high-density RF/DC interposer to support standard wire bonding and encloses the actuators in a grounded Faraday cage to prevent unwanted Stark shifts in the device layer. Finite element simulations confirm that combining stiff actuators with this symmetric mounting drastically improves strain homogeneity. Finally, we validate the apparatus experimentally by applying uniaxial strain to a 200 $μ$m thick silicon die. Surface strain measurements demonstrate an applied strain of 215 $με$ for 200 V applied piezo bias.

</details>


### [163] [Diffusive Relaxation of Participation Entropy in U(1)-symmetric Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11561)
*Hanchen Liu,Tianci Zhou,Xiao Chen*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，在具有U(1)守恒律的多体量子系统中，参与熵（participation entropy）的弛豫被守恒量导致的慢流体力学模式显著减缓，弛豫行为呈现扩散控制的幂律衰减$t^{-1/2}$，并在长时交叉到指数形式$\exp[-O(t/L^2)]$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 参与熵（participation entropy, PE）用于量化多体波函数在构型空间中的散布程度。尽管在一般混沌系统中PE快速弛豫，但U(1)守恒律（$\mathrm{U}(1)$ conservation laws）是否以及如何通过缓流体力学模式（hydrodynamic modes）减缓其弛豫过程尚不清楚。

Method: 采用围绕平衡态的团簇展开（cluster expansion）方法，推导出局部密度不均匀性衰落后，主导的PE亏损由平方连接密度关联（squared connected density correlations）决定。使用精确计算和无限系统张量网络模拟（tensor network simulations）在多种量子U(1)守恒线路中验证该熵-关联关系。

Result: 在流体力学区域，弛豫呈现扩散控制的幂律行为$\Delta S(t) \sim t^{-1/2}$；当时间$t \geq L^2$时，交叉到指数衰减$\sim \exp[-O(t/L^2)]$。数值结果与理论预测一致。

Conclusion: 参与熵可作为探测流体力学记忆（hydrodynamic memory）的灵敏探针，弛豫减缓（slow relaxation）是守恒律在量子多体系统中的普适后果。

Abstract: Participation entropy (PE) quantifies the spread of a many-body wavefunction across configuration space. While PE relaxes rapidly in generic chaotic systems, we show that $\mathrm{U}(1)$ conservation laws slow it down by imprinting with the slow hydrodynamic modes. Using a cluster expansion around equilibrium, we show that, after local density inhomogeneities decay, the leading PE deficit is dominated by squared connected density correlations. The long time relaxation is therefore controlled by diffusive correlation spreading, giving $ΔS(t)\sim t^{-1/2}$ in the hydrodynamic regime and crossing over to $\sim \exp[-O(t/L^2)]$ when $t\geq L^2$. We confirm this entropy correlation relation using exact computation and infinite system tensor network simulations in various quantum $\mathrm{U}(1)$ conserving circuits. Our results establish PE as a sensitive probe of hydrodynamic memory and suggest that slow relaxation is a generic consequence of conservation laws.

</details>


### [164] [Tensor-Network Algorithm for Many-Body Trace Norms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11882)
*Seunghun Lee,Eun-Gook Moon*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于张量网络（tensor network）的受控算法，用于估计矩阵乘积算符（matrix product operator）的迹范数（trace norm），无需全对角化（full diagonalization），并将该方法成功应用于纠缠负性（entanglement negativity）、量子保真度（quantum fidelity）和量子费舍尔信息（quantum Fisher information）的计算中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 迹范数是量子信息理论（quantum information theory）中的基本量，但在多体系统（many-body systems）中，其计算通常需要对指数级增长的算符进行对角化，构成严重的计算瓶颈。现有方法难以在大规模混合态场景下高效地逼近迹范数。

Method: 该方法的核心是将Zolotarev有理逼近（Zolotarev's rational approximation）用于符号函数（sign function），并结合变分公式（variational formulation），通过类似密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix-renormalization-group, DMRG）的算法进行求解。逼近精度由有理逼近参数（rational approximation parameters）和靠近零的谱权重（spectral weight near zero）系统可控。

Result: 该方法超越了精确对角化（exact diagonalization）的可处理范围，在纠缠负性、量子保真度和量子费舍尔信息等量的计算中取得了显著优于基于多项式的Lanczos方法（polynomial-based Lanczos approaches）的精度。

Conclusion: 该工作将基于迹范数的量确立为实用的张量网络可观测量（tensor-network observables），为混合态（mixed states）量子信息的张量网络研究开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Trace norms are fundamental to quantum information theory, yet in many-body systems their evaluation remains a major computational bottleneck, as it generally requires diagonalizing exponentially large operators. Here, we overcome this bottleneck by introducing a controlled tensor-network algorithm for estimating the trace norm of matrix product operators without full diagonalization. The key idea is to combine Zolotarev's rational approximation to the sign function with a variational formulation solved using a density-matrix-renormalization-group-like algorithm. The resulting approximation is systematically improvable, with its accuracy controlled by the rational approximation parameters and the spectral weight near zero. Beyond the reach of exact diagonalization, we demonstrate controlled trace-norm calculations for entanglement negativity, quantum fidelity and quantum Fisher information, achieving substantially improved accuracy over polynomial-based Lanczos approaches. Our results establish trace-norm-based quantities as practical tensor-network observables, opening a route toward tensor-network studies of quantum information in mixed states.

</details>

### [165] [Collective Emission in LH2 Assembly Beyond the Point-Dipole Approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11227)
*Javed Akhtar,Himangshu Prabal Goswami*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过非厄米哈密顿量与量子电动力学并矢格林张量，研究了紫色细菌光捕获组装体中有限偶极子几何对集体发射的调控，发现P42$_1$2晶胞对称性反转了单环的明暗态序，并揭示了倾斜开关仅在特定晶体几何下被激活，且空位与取向无序协同重整化开关阈值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的点偶极子近似（point-dipole approximation）无法正确描述光捕获组装体中由有限几何与局部跃迁偶极子（local transition dipole）决定的集体发射（collective emission）行为，因此需要发展超越该近似的理论框架。

Method: 利用量子电动力学并矢格林张量（quantum electrodynamic dyadic Green's tensor）构建非厄米哈密顿量（non-Hermitian Hamiltonian），分别针对紫色细菌中孤立的24-细菌叶绿素（bacteriochlorophyll）锥台结构及其P42$_1$2晶体学组装进行建模。

Result: P42$_1$2晶胞对称性反转了单环的明暗态序（bright-dark ordering），使亚辐射态（subradiant states）位于低能端，表明整个晶体才是能量捕获实体（energy-harvesting entity）。倾斜开关（tilt-driven switching）仅在有限偶极子载体（LH2）垂直于生长平面的晶体几何中被激活。空位（vacancy）与取向无序（orientational disorder）协同作用，将开关阈值从高极角（higher polar angles）重整化至较低值。

Conclusion: 超越点偶极子近似是理解光捕获组装体中集体发射的关键；晶体对称性、有限几何与无序的协同效应共同决定了系统的光物理行为，为设计人工光捕获材料提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Collective emission in light-harvesting assemblies is governed by the local transition dipole and finite geometry of emitting units, a fact that point-dipole approximation obscures. To go beyond this picture, we develop a non-Hermitian Hamiltonian using the quantum electrodynamic dyadic Green's tensor for a purple bacteria. We construct it for the isolated 24-bacteriochlorophyll conical frustum and its P42$_1$2 crystallographic assembly. The P42$_1$2 unit-cell symmetry is found to invert the bright-dark ordering of the single ring, placing subradiant states at the low-energy end and revealing the entire crystal to be the energy-harvesting entity. Tilt-driven switching is activated only in crystal geometries where the finite dipole-carrier (LH2) lies perpendicular to the growth plane. Vacancy and orientational disorder work only in cooperation to renormalize the switching threshold from higher polar angles to lower values.

</details>
